Disease: dama (Asthma) Description: sookasham shavaas naliyon men koi rog utapanan ho jaane ke kaaran jab kisi vayakati ko sns lene men pareshaani hone lagati hai tab yah sathiti dama rog kahalaati hai, is rog men vayakati ko khnsi ki samasaya bhi hoti hai। Symptoms: - jab dama rog se piṛit rogi ko daura paṛata hai to use sookhi ya aithanadaar khnsi hoti hai। - jab rog bahut adhik baṛh jaata hai to daura aane ki sathiti utapanan ho jaati hai jisase rogi ko sns lene men bahut adhik dikakat aati hai tatha vayakati chhatapataane lagata hai। - dama rog se piṛit rogi ko kaph sakhata, badaboodaar tatha doridaar nikalata hai। - piṛit rogi ko sns lenen men bahut adhik kathinaai hoti hai। - yah rog satari-purush donon ko ho sakata hai। - raat ke samay men lagabhag 2 baje ke baad daure adhik paṛate hain। - rogi ko rog ke shuruaati samay men khnsi, sarasaraahat aur sns ukhaṛane ke daure paṛane lagate hain। - sns lete samay adhik jor lagaame par rogi ka chehara laal ho jaata hai। - sns lete samay halaki-halaki siti bajane ki aavaaj bhi sunaai paṛati hai। - sns lene tatha sns ko baahar chhoṛane men kaaphi jor lagaana paṛata hai। Reasons: - aushadhiyon ka adhik parayog karame ke kaaran kaf dama ho sakata hai। - bhookh se adhik bhojan khaane se dama ho sakata hai। - miracha-masaale, tale-bhune khaaday padaarathon tatha garishath bhojam karame se yah rog ho sakata hai। - phephaṛon men yah rog ho sakata hai। - manushay ke sharir ki paachan maliyon men jalan utapanan karane vaale padaarathon ka sevan karane se bhi dama ho sakata hai। - mala-mootar ke veg ko baara-baar rokane se yah rog ho sakata hai। - garada, dhun, gndagi, badaboo, gnde bisatara, puraani kitaaben aur kapadon ki jhaad, kheton ki jhaad, sakhat saradi, barasaata, jukaama, phaloo, aadi sookasham kanom ka sns davaara phephadon men jaane se dama ho sakata hai। - vaataavaran men paradooshan se hone vaali elaraji - isake alaava kai logon men kuchh nishachit davaaom (esapirin aur betaa- balaॉkarasa) ke sevan baṛhaakar daure ki sathiti utapanan kar sakati haim। - asathama ya elaraji ka paarivaarik itihaas (aanivnshik damaa) - janam ke samay kam vajam aur samay se pahale bachachon ka janama, janam ke pahale nashile padaarathon ka sevan nahin karana chaahie। Home Remedies: - lahasun dama ke ilaaj men kaaphi kaaragar saabit hota hai। 30 mili doodh men lahasun ki pmch kaliyn ubaalen aur is misharan ka har bhoone ki upar ka patata jale। thnda hone par kele ka chhilaka nikaalakar kela kha len। Disease: madhumeh (Diabetes) Description: madhumeh ya daayabitij haal ke saalon men hone vaala sabase khataranaak jivanashaili rog maana jaata hai। har saal kai hajaar log isase parabhaavit hote hain। aaiyen jaanem madhumeh ke baaren men jise log aam bolachaal ki bhaasha me shugar (Sugar ki Bimari) bhi kahate hain। Symptoms: - atayadhik payaas lagama aur baar baar peshaab aana (Excessive Thirst): yah madhumeh hone ke pukhata lakashan hain - jakhamon ka jaladi nahi bharana aur baar baar snkaraman se raahat milati hai। - rogi ka kamara savachachha, aur garam hona chaahie। kamare men sooray ki raushani avashay aani chaahiye। - rogi ke sharir ko garam rakhen, visheshakar chhaati aur pairon ko। - tulasi bhi nimoniya men bahut upayogi hai। tulasi ke kuchh taaje pataton ka rasa, ek chutaki kaali mirach men milakar rakh len aur har chh ghnte ke baad den। Disease: enorekasiya (Anorexia) Descriptiom: bhookh n lagane ko medikal bhaasha men enorekasiya (Anorexia) ya aruchi rog kahate hain। emorekasiya (Anorexia) ya aruchi rog mem rogi ko bhookh nahin lagati, yadi jabaradasati bhojan kiya bhi jaay to vah aruchikar lagata hai। is rog se pidit vayakati 1 ya 2 garaas se jayaada nahin kha paata aur use bina kuchh khaaye -piye hi khatati dakaaren aame lagati hain। Symptoms: - kam khaane par bhi pet bhara paratit homa - kisi kaaray ko karane ki ichachha nahin hona - khaana khaane ki ichachha m hona - khoon ki kami hona - chehara kmtihin evn kaala pad jaana - jayaada payaas lagana - thodi sa kaam karame par thakaan homa - maanasik ashnti se garasat hona - mumh men garami evn munh se badaboo aama - sharir ke vajan men dima-ba-dim kami hote jaana - sookhi dakaaren aama - haृday ke samip lagaataar jalan hona Reasoms: enorekasiya ke shaaririk kaaranon (Physical Reason of Humger Disorder): - paachan tntar men gaṛabaṛi hone ke kaaran jibh men kisi bhi parakaar ka savaad n banaakar khaane se bhookh tej hoti hai। - ek seb ya seb ke ras ke paratidin sevan se khoon saaph hota hai aur bhookh bhi lagati hai। - ek gilaas paani men jiraa, hinga, pudimaa, kaalimirach aur namak kabaj door hokar paachanakariya tej ho jaati hai। Home Remedies: bhojan men aruchi ko enorekasiya (Amorexi Nervosa) bhi kahate hain। kai logon ko apane vajan aur phitanes ki itami chimta ho jaati hai ki vo haarash daayating karane lagate hain aur phir shuru ho jaati hai enorekasiya ki bimaari। isamen sharir ka vajan kaaphi kam ho jaata hai। sharir men hadadi aur mnsapeshiyon par ki jami vasa lagaataar bhookhe rahane se jalame lagati hai aur sharir men siraph hadadi ka ṛhncha hi shesh rah jaata hai। enorekasiya ki bimaari khaasakar maॉdaling aur phaishan indasatari men kaam kar rahi kam umar ki laṛakiyon men jayaada hota hai, kayonki unahen samaarat aur phit dikhane ke lie 'jiro phigara' jaisi kaaya banaami paṛati hai। lekin baad men yahi jiro phigar unake lie jaanaleva bam jaati hai। enorekasiya bimaari ke baad n aapako bhookh lagati hai aur n hi kisi chij men ruchi। is bimaari ke baad aap khud ko bhaavamaatamaka, manovaijaञaanika, saamaajik aur shaaririk rup se itana to paida ki hi jaati hai। enorekasiya ke ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies for Anorexia) lahasun (Garlic) lahasun bhookh jagaane ki sabase kaaragar ghareloo upaay hai। ise khaane ke baad ek khaas tarah bhojan khaana shuru karen। Disease: darad (Pain) Description: darad ya piṛa (About Pain im Hindi) Reasoms: darad ke kai kaaran hote haim jaise chot laganaa, pooraani bimaari aadi। darad (dard) ke hai vahn haladi ka chooran aur choona mila kar laga diya jaae to phauran darad thik ho jaati hai aur soojan bhi kam ho jaati hai। Disease: anidara (Insomnia) Description: achachhi nind achachhe hi kamar darad ka kaaran hota hai। kamar darad sahi tarah se n uthane-baithane, sone ya kamar par kashamata se adhik dabaav padne se hota hai। lagabhag 80 % log kabhi n kabhi kamar darad se pareshaan hote hain। kamar darad naya bhi ho sakata hai aur puraana bhi ho sakata hai। satahi taur par dekhane par kamar men hone vaala darad bhale hi ek saamaanay si sathiti lagati hai, lekin ise nazarndaaj karane se samasaya kaaphi barh sakati hai। jaanie kamar darad door karane ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Back Pain): 1. ghutane moden (Band knee)- niche rakhi koi vasatu uthaate vakat pahale apane ghutane moden phir us vasatu ko uthaaen। aisa karane se kamar par anaavashayak dabaav nahim padega aur kam takaliph hogi। 2. lahasun (Garlic)- bhojan men lahasun ka parayaapat upayog karem। lahasun kamar darad ka achachha upachaar maana gaya hai। lahasun ke parayog se puraane se puraana kamar darad bhi thik hone lagata hai। 3. googul (Benzoin)- googul kamar darad men behad raahat deta hai। kamar darad men upachaar ke lie googul ki aadha chamamach garam paani ke saath subaha-shaam sevan karen। aisa karane se kamar darad men aaraam milata hai। 4. masaala chaay (Tea)- chaay bamaane munh pet ke bal sona bhi haanikaarak hai। 6. daalachini (Cimnamon)- 2 garaam daalachini ka paaudar ek chamamach shahad mem milaakar din men do baar lete rahane se kamaradarad men raahat milati hai। 7. to dhayaan rakhen ki darad vaala hisasa hava ke snparak men n aae। 8. baraph ki sikaai (Ice Foment)- darad vaali jagah par baraph ka parayog karana bhi laabhakaari upaay hai। isase bhitari soojan bhi samaapat hogi। kuchh roj baraf ka upayog karane ke baad garam sikaai paraarnbh kar dene se anukool parinaam aate hain। 9. paushatik bhojan (Proper Nutrition)- bhojan me tamaatara, gobhi, chukndara, khiraa, kakadi, paalaka, gaajara, flom ka parachur maatara men upayog karen। 10. bhaap ki sikaai (Steam Foment)- namak mile garam paani men ek tauliya daalakar nichod len। pet ke bal letakar darad ke sathaan par tauliye davaara bhaap lene se kamar darad men raahat milati hai। 11. maalish (Massage)- roj subah sarason ya naariyal ke tel mem lahasun ki tina-chaar kaliyn daalakar (jab tak lahasum ki kaliyn kaali n ho jaayen) garam kar len phir thnda kar parabhaavit jagah par maalish karen। 12. namak (Salt)- karhaai men do-tin chamamach namak daalakar ise achachhe se sek len। thode mote sooti kapade men yah garam namak daalakar potali bndh len। kamar par isake davaara sek karen। Disease: sine men darad (Chest Pain) Description: sine men darad ( Chest Pain) ki baat aate hi ham dil ke daure (Heart Attack) ki baat sochame lagate hain, magar sine men darad kai kaaranon se ho sakata hai। phephade, mmsapeshiyn, pasali, ya nason mem bhi koi samasaya utapanam hone par sine men darad hota hai। isako chhoṛana phaayademnd hai। Home Remedies: sine men darad (Chest Pain) hamesha haarat ataik ka maamala nahin hotaa। sine ya chhaati men darad ke aur bhi kai kaaran ho sakate hain। esiditi, saradi, kainsar se bhi bachaav karata hai। anaar men maujood tatav kainsar ko paida karane vaale selas ko maar dete hain jisase kainsar nahin hotaa। anaar ke daanon ko yoom hi khaaya ja sakata hai ya amaar ka joos nikaalakar bhi piya ja sakata hai। 5. kadadoo ke bij (Pumpkin seeds)- kadadoo ke bij dayooretik (diuretic) roop se kaaray karate hain jo ki kai bimaariyon men laabhakaari hain। khaasakar mootar aur parosatet se snbndhit rogom men behad laabhakaari hain। kadadoo ke bijom men bahut sa jink (zinc) hota hai jo ki imayooniti barhaame men madad karata hai, jisase parosatet kainsar se teji se rikavari snbhav hoti hai। upachaar ke lie kadadoo ke bijon ko ikatatha karake unahen kachacha hi khaaen। isake alaava in bijon ki chaay banaakar bhi pi sakate hain। is chaay ko laabh hone tak rojaana pien। 6. soya (Soya)- soya men saayatosatarojan (phytoestrogen) hota hai jo ki tesatosatiron (testosterone) ka sataraav tej karata hai। is kaaran parosatet galaind men rakat snchaar tej hota hai jisase kainsar paida karane vaale selas ki snkhaya ghatati chali jaati hai। 7. vitaamin di (Vitamin D)- vitaamin di ki uchit maatara home se parosatet kainsar hone ka khatara nahin rahataa। yah n keval parosatet kainsar se rakasha karata hai balaki hone ke baad isase upachaar bhi snbhav hai। phoratiphaaid (fortified) daalen aur thnde paani mem rahane vaali machhaliyn vitaamin di ki achachhi satarot hoti hain। isake saath hi aap vitaamin di 3 ke sapaliment bhi le sakate hain। 8. garin ti (Greem tea)- garin ti ek aisi harab hai jisamen bahut se gun hote hain aur yah parosatet kainsar ke upachaar men bhi sahaayak hai। garin ti men poliphinolas (polifenoles) uchit maatara men hote haim jo kainsar paida karane vaale selas ko maar dete hain। 9. phaiti phish (Fatty fish)- phaiti phish omega 3 ki achachhi satarot hoti hai, jo ki kainsar se bachaav men sahaayak hai। isake alaava phalaik sid bhi omaga 3 ke achachhe satarot hote hain। sharir men omega 3 ki maatara barhaane ke lie phish ऑyal ke kaipasool sapaliment ke roop men bhi lie ja sakate hain। Disease: haipetaaitis (Hepatitis) Description: livar sharir ka ek mahatatavapooran ng hai। vah bhojan pachaane men mahatatavapooran bhoomika nibhaata hai। sharir men hone vaali chayaapachay kariyaaon (Metabolic Process) men livar (Liver) vishesh sahaayata karata hai। Symptoms: - atayadhik kamajori v thakaan - nkha, jibha, mootar v tavacha men pilaapan - paachan samasayaaom jaise ulati - bhookh men kami - chiṛachiṛaapan Reasons: haipetaaitis ko saamaanayata: paani se honi vaali bimaari maana jaata hai jo poori tarah galat hai। daॉkataron ke anusaar niman kaaranom se bhi haipetaaitis ho sakata hai: haipetaaitis ke kaaran (Causes of Hepatitis) - aanuvnshika, - kuposhana, - sharaaba, - phaiti livar Treatments: haipetaaitis se bachaav ke lie saapha-saphaai behad aavashayak hai। khaane aur pine men hamesha saaph chijon ke parayog se isase bacha ja sakata hai। haipetaaitis se bachaav ke anay upaay miman hain: - livar ko savasath rakhane ke lie saapha-suthara bhojan aur saaph paani jaroori hai। - baahar ka khaana khaane se bachen, lekin khaama bhi paṛe to saapha-saphaai dekhakar hi khaaen। - haipetaaitis e (Hepatitis A Vaccine) ka tika jaroor lagavaana chaahie। - kisi doosare ki sui, rejar aur toothabarash isatemaal nahin karana chaahie। - rakat chaṛhaane par is baat ka vishesh dhayaam rakhen ki nai sui ho aur rakat snkaramit n ho। - adhik tela, ghi, haladi aur mirach masaale ka bhojan n karen। - hari patatidaar sabajiyn khaaen, mausami aur ganane ka ras pien। - naariyal paani, chaavala, dahi ya chhaachha, ubale aaloo aur chhaime vaala rasagulala khaaen। - pila bukhaar - livar kainsar Home Remedies: hepetaaitis roga, livar men soojan aur jalan (inflammation) ke kaaran hota hai। livar sharir ko savasath rakhane men mahatavapooran kaaray karata hai। poshak tatavon ko satorej karane ke saath hi sharir men uraja ke smchaar ko kmtarol karana aur kolesataraॉl aadi ka niramaan bhi livar hi karata hai। livar yaani gurade men pareshaani tab aati hai jab haanikaarak pey ya bhojan adhik maatara men khaaya jaata hai। sharaab ya amay nashile padaarath livar par bura asar daalate hain। isase imayoom sisatam bhi kamajor ho jaata hai। kai baar yah aanuvmshik samasaya bhi ho sakati hai। hepetaaitis ke lakashanon men pet ke daayin or ke hisase men bhaaripan lagata hai, piliya ho sakata hai, thakaavat mahasoos hoti hai tatha khujali hoti hai। hepetaaitis ka upachaar ghareloo saamagari se bhi smbhav hai lekin sathiti agar kaaboo men n aae to chikitasak ke paas jaana hi thik hota hai। aaie aapako bataate hain hepetaaitis ke upachaar ke lie kuchh ghareloo upaayon ke baare mem- 1. ajavaayan aur jira (Ajwaim aur jeera) ek chamamach ajavaayam aur ek chamamach jira pisakar paaudar bana len। isamen ek chutaki namak milaaen। is chooran ko rojaana do baar khaaen। isase imayooniti barhegi aur hepetaaitis men aaraam hogaa। 2. likoris paaudar aur shahad (Liquorice powder and honey) ek bada chamamach likoris paaudar men do chamamach shahad milaakar paratidin khaaen। hepetaaitis ke upachaar men yah bhi behad phaayademnd hai। isake saath hi likoris ki jad ko paani men ubaalakar usaki chaay bhi banaai ja sakati hai। 3. lahasun (Garlic) lahasun rakat ko saaph karata hai aur sharir se vishaakat padaarathom ko baahar mikaalata hai aise men rojaana subah khaali pet lahasun ki ek se do kali chabaaen। saath hi khaana banaane men bhi lahasun ka parayog masaale ke roop men jaroor karen। 4. haladi (Haldi) haladi inaphalementari (inflammatory) gunon se bharapoor hoti hai। haladi ka isatemaal bhi hepetaaitis se rakasha kar sakata hai। haladi ko doodh men daalakar pine se bhi bahut laabh hota hai। haalmki piliya hone men haladi lene ki manaahi hoti hai। 5. kaali gaajar (Black carrot) kaali gaajar ke bhi bahut phaayade hain। vitaamin se bharapoor kaali gaajar se khoom ki kami poori hoti hai tatha rakat smchaar sudharata hai। hepetaaitis men bhi gaajar ko salaad ke roop mem khaane se bahut phaayade hote hain। 6. garin ti (Green tea) garin ti yaami harabal chaay gumon se bharapoor hoti hai। garin ti men entiऑkasident (antioxidant) hote hain jo sharir ke saath hi masatishak ko bhi savasath rakhate hain। hepetaaitis ke upachaar aur bachaav ke lie garin ti ko apani dinacharaya men shaamil karen। 7. nvala (Amla) nvala vitaamin si se bharapoor hota hai jo livar ko har tarah se phaayada pahunchaata hai। nvala ka parayog chayavanaparaash men bhi kiya jaata hai jisase imayooniti barhe aur paachan shakati majaboot ho। aise mem nvala ka parayog dainik aahaar men bhi kiya ja sakata hai। mvala joosa, chatani, achaar aadi ko dainik aahaar men shaamil karen। 8. alasi ke bij (Flax seed) alasi ke bij sharir mem haaramon ka sntulan donon banaae rakhate hain aur unahen rakat men sahi tarike se bhejane ka kaam bhi karate hain। phalaikas sid men saayatoknsatitayooemtas (phytoconstituents) hote hain jo ki haaramon ki baainding ka kaam karate haim aur livar par atirikat bhaar nahin padne dete। phalaikas sid ko yoon hi tosat ke upara, salaad me ya daal aadi mem daalakar khaaya ja sakata hai। yah livar ko majaboot banaane men sahaayak hai jisase hepetaaitis rog se bachaav hota hai। Disease: pile dnt (Yellow Teeth) Description: dmt siraph hamen bhojan chabaane men hi madad nahin karate, balaki hamaare vayakatitav ko bhi parabhaavit karate haim। saapha, savasath v sundar dmt chehare ka aakarashan hote hain। lekim agar dmt pile ho to yah sharamindagi ka bhi kaaran ban sakate haim। Symptoms: - pile dnt Reasons: dnton men pilaapan aana hamaare galat rahana-sahan ke kaaran to kai baar saapha-saphaai na rakhane ke kaaran hota hai। kuchh anay kaaran bhi hain jimake kaaran dnt pile hote hain, jaise: pile dnton ka mukhay kaaram (Causes of Yellow teeth in Hindi) - tnbaakoo, gutakaa, sharaab aadi ke jayaada sevan karane se dnt pile ho sakate haim। - kuchh logon men umar baṛhane ke saatha-saath dnton par palaik ki parat chaṛhati jaati hai। isase bhi dnt pile dikhane lagate hain। - jayaada maatar men chaaya, kaॉphi aur kolad darink ka sevam karane se bhi dnt pile hone lagate hain। - phalorosis : desh ke kai shaharon ke paani men phaloraaid ki maatara adhik hone ke kaaran dntom ka rng badarng ho jaata hai। unamen upar pile evn saphed chikatate dikhaai padte hain। Treatments: agar dnton ko saaph karane ke baad bhi dnton se pilaapan ma jaae to miman upachaar apanaane chaahie: - vahaaitamara, shaainar aur vishesh kemikalas ke jariye dnton ki chamak aasaani se lautaai ja sakati hai। - dental baliching se dnton ka pilaapana, pile-laal dhababe, gutakaa, tnbaakoo aadi ke daag aasaani se khatam kie ja sakate hain। - pile dnton ko saphed karane ka ghareloo upachaara, bekimg soda hai। garam paani men beking soda mila kar usase kulala (Gargle) karen। jab munh se paani baahar nikaalen tab apane dntom ko ungaliyon se ragaden, isase dnt chamak jaaenge। - dnton ko savasath rakhane ke lie phaloraaid yukat toothapesat aur mulaayam barash se dim men do baar dnt saaph karane ki aadat daalen। - isake saath jibh ki saphaai bhi karen, kayonki baikatiriya jayaadaatar yahim panapate haim। - din men ek baar phalaॉs bhi karen। isase dmton ke bich phnse bhojan ke tukaṛe nikal jaate hain। - adhik garam chijen n khaaen। - jayaada kaṛak barisal vaale barash se dnt saaph n karen। - mmsaahaari khaana khaane ke baad kulala jaroor karen। isase dntom men phnse reshe bhi nikal jaaenge aur gndh bhi। - dnton men takaliph n ho, tab bhi saal men ek baar dnton ka chekaap jaroor karaaen। - kuchh bhi khaane-pine ke baad saaph paani se kulala karen। - jayaada puraana barash masooṛon aur dnton ko nukasaam pahuncha sakata hai, isalie har tin mahine men barash badal len। Home Remedies: saphed aur chamakate dnt kisi ki bhi parasaneliti mem mikhaar la sakate hain। bahut se log pile dnton ke kaaran logon ke saamane hnsane se bachate hain ya munh par haath rakhakar hnsate hain। dnt jayaadaatar umar ke kaarana, dnton ki thik se saphaai n hone ke kaarana, bahut jayaada chaay ya kaॉphi pine ke kaaran athava tmbaakoo aur sigaret pine ke kaaran pile ho jaate hain। kabhi kabhi kisi bimaari ke kaaran bhi dnt pile ho jaate haim। haalnki pile dnton ko saphed banaama koi mushakil kaam nahin hai। thodi si mehamat se aap pile dnton ko saphed bana sakate hain। aaie aapako kuchh ghareloo nusakhe bataate haim jo aapake dnto ki saphedi aur chamak ko bamaae rakhenge। 1. beking sodaa- (Baking Soda) beking soda dnton ko saphed banaane ka sabase aasaan tarika hai। yah dnton se palaak ko khatam karake dnton ki saphedi aur chamak banaae rakhata hai। kaise upayog karen - roj barash karate samay apane pesat men thoda sa beking paaudar daalem aur barash karen। dnton ki saphedi laut aaegi। - ek kap paami men beking soda aur haaidarojam par ऑkasaaid (hydrogen peroxide) milaakar maauth vaॉsh (mouthwash) ki tarah bhi isatemaal kiya ja sakata hai। 2. sntare ka chhilakaa- (Peel of Orange) sntare ke chhilake se roj dntom ki saphaai karane se kuchh hi dinon men pile dnt chamakane lagenge। kaise upayog karen - roj raat ko sote samay sntare ke chhilake ko dnton par ragaden। sntare ke chhilake men vitaamin si (vitamin c) aur kailashiyam ke saath maaikaroऑragenijam (micro organism) hota hai jo dnton ki majabooti aur chamak banaae rakhata hai। 3. sataraॉberi- (Strawberry) sataraॉberi men bhi vitaamin si parachur maatara men hota hai jo ki dnton ko saphed banaane men sahaayak hai। kaise upayog karen - sataraॉberi ke kuchh tukadon ko pisakara, is lep ko dntom par lagaakar masaaj karen। ise din men do baar karane se kuchh hi dinon men pile dnt saphed hone lagate hain। - beking soda aur sataraॉberi ke palap ko milaakar bhi dmton par ragadne se dnton ka pilaapan khatam hota hai। 4. ninboo- (Lemon) minboo ke paraakaृtik baliching (natural bleach) ke gun dnton par bhi asar dikhaate haim। pile dnton ke lie minboo ke chhilake ko dnton par ragada ja sakata hai, ya nimboo ke paani se garaare bhi kie ja sakate hain। kaise upayog karen - ninboo ke saath namak milaakar dnton ki masaaj karem। - do haphaton tak rojaana do baar karane se dnt chamakane lagemge। 5. namaka- (Salt) namak ko puraame samay se hi dnto ki saphaai ke lie isatemaal kiya jaata raha hai। yah dnton ke khoe minaralas lautaata hai jisase dmton ka saphed rng bana rahata hai। kaise upayog karen - rojaana subah toothapesat ki tarah mamak ko dnton ki saphaai ke lie isatemaal kiya ja sakata hai। mamak ko chaarakol men milaakar bhi dnton ki saphaai ki ja sakati hai jisase dnt saphed hote hain। - namak aur beking paaudar milaakar bhi mnjan taiyaar kiya ja sakata hai। 6. tulasi- (Basil) tulasi mem bhi dnton ko saphed bamaane ka gun hota hai। isake saath hi tulasi paayariya aadi se bhi dntom ki rakasha karati hai। kaise upayog karen - tulasi ke pataton ko sukhaakar paaudar bana len। is paaudar ko rojaana isatemaal karane vaale toothapesat men milaakar dnton ki saphaai karen। - tulasi ke pataton ka pesat banaakar usamen sarason ka tel (mustard oil) milaaen। is pesat se dntom ki saphaai karane par bhi bahut phaayada hota hai। 7. seba- (Apple) seb ko daait men shaamil karane se bhi dnton ki saphedi lautaai ja sakati hai। seb ki karnchines dnton ko paraakaृtik taur par sakarab karati hai। rojaana ek ya do seb jaroor khaaen aur khoob chaba chaba kar khaaen। isi tarah gaajar aur khira bhi kachacha khaane se dnt saphed tatha majaboot banate hain। Disease: ti. bi. (Tuberculosis) Description: tayoobarakayulosis (Tuberculosis) maayakobekatiriyam tayoobarakayulosis naamak jivaamu ke kaaran hota hai। ti.bi. rog ko anay kai naam se jaama jaata hai, jaise tapedika, kashay rog tatha yakashamaa। Symptoms: - agar aapaka vajana, bagair koshish kiye huye, pichhale 2 mahinon men, 5 kilogaraam se adhik ghat gaya hai - agar aapako khmsi men khoon aata hai - agar aapako khnsi men balagam aata hai - agar aapako tin haphate se adhik se khnsi hai - agar aapako bhookh kam lagati hai - agar aapako raat men adhik pasina aata hai - agar aapane apane balagam ka kabhi ti bi ka jnch karavaaya hai, jise pozitiv kaha gaya ho Reasons: tibi kai kaaranon se phailata hai lekin isake paramukh kaaranon men aparayaapat v apaushatik bhojama, kam jagah men adhik logon ka rahanaa, gmdagi, gaay ka kachacha doodh pina aadi hain। isake anay kaaran niman haim: tibi ke kaaran (Causes of Tuberculosis) - ti bi ke marij ke jahn-jahn thookane se isake vishaanu savasath vayakati ke sharir men paravesh karake use rogi bama dete hain। - kapada mil men kaam karane vaale sharamik ya reshe-roe ke snparak mem rahane vaale loga, - bunakara, dhool ke snparak mem rahane vaale log tatha ndheri kothariyon ya chaalon mem rahane vaale log bhi is rog ka shikaar ho jaate hain। - madiraapaana, dhoomarapaan tatha rogagarasat pashu ka mns khaame vaale log bhi tibi ka shikaar ho sakate hain। - asaavadhaanivash rogi ka khoon anay kisi rog ke sharir men charhaane se vah vayakati rogagarasat ho jaata hai। Treatments: tibi ka upachaar (Treatment of Tuberculosis in Hindi) - yadi tin athava adhik sapataah se khnsi ho rahi ho to kaf ki do baar jnch karaaen। ye jmch sarakaari kaf sookashamadarashi kenadaron par ni:shulak ki jaati hai। - sabhi davaaon ko niyamit roop se, bataai gai poori avadhi tak len। - khnsate ya chhinkate samay roomaal ka parayog karen। Home Remedies: tibi yaani tayoobarakulosis (Tuberculosis), ek parakaar ka inphekasham hota hai jo ki maayakoikatiriyam tayoobarakulosis (mycobacterium tuberculosis) baikatiriya ke kaaran phailata hai। tibi adhikatar phephephadon men hoti hai lekim yah sharir ke kisi bhi hisase men ho sakati hai। tibi ke marij ke kaph men khoon aana tibi ka aam lakashan hai isake alaava smson ka tej chalanaa, vajan ka kam honaa, bukhaar honaa, kidani aur sine men darad hona aadi bhi tayoobarakulosis ke lakashan hain। vaise to tibi se poori tarah nijaat ke lie chikitasak se paraamarash aavashayak hai lekin kuchh ghareloo upachaaron ke davaara bhi tibi ko thik karane ki parakariya tej ki ja sakati hai। aaie aapako bataate hain tibi ke upachaar ke lie kuchh ghareloo nusakhe- 1. lahasun (Garlic)- lahasun men salaphayoorik esid (sulphuric acid) parachur maatara men hota hai jo ki tibi ke kitaanuon ko maarane men sakasham hai। isake saath hi lahasun men elisin (allicin) aur ejoini (agoeni) bhi hote hain jo ki tibi ke panapane vaale kitaanuon ka khatam karane ka kaam karate hain। itana hi nahin lahasun ke emtibaikatiriyal gun imayoomiti ko bhi barhaate hain। kaise karem upayog aadhi chamamach lahasuna, ek kap doodh aur chaar kap paani ko ek saath milaakar ubaalen। ise tab tak ubaalen jab tak yah misharan ek chauthaai rah jaae। is misharan ko din men tin baar pien। garam doodh men lahasun ka ras milaakar bhi piya ja sakata hai। isake baad paani n pien। garam doodh men lahasun ko ubaalem। isake baad lahasun ko chabaakar bache hue doodh ko pi lem। 2. kela (Banana)- kela poshak tatavon aur kailashiyam ka bahut achachha satarot hai। yah tibi ke marij ka imayoon sisatam badhaa़ne men sahaayak hai। isake saath hi bukhaar aur kaph se bhi raahat deta hai। kaise karen upayog ek pake hue kele ko ek kap maariyal ke paani men masalakar milaaen। isake baad isamen dahi aur shahad milaaen। ise din men do baar khaaen। kachache kele ka joos banaakar rojaana pien। kele ke tane ka joos banaakar bhi piya ja sakata hai। 3. nvala (Amla)- nvala men entiphalemetari (anti inflammatory) aur entibaikatiriyal (antibacterial) gun hote hain। jo sharir ka imayoon sisatam majaboot karake sharir ko uraja paradaan karate hain। kaise karen upayog nvala ke bij nikaalakara, joos banaaen aur isamen ek chamamach shahad milaakar subah subah piem। 4. sntara (Orange)- sntare men bhi jaroori minaralas (minerals) aur knpaaund (compound) hote hain। sntare men maujood salaaim (salain) sharir ko inphekashan se bachaata hai saath hi imayoon sisatam ko majaboot karata hai। kaise karen upayog taaja sntare ke ras men thoda sa namak aur shahad milaakar rojaana subah shaam pien। smtare ko chhilakar usaki salaais par bhi namak chhidk kar khaaya ja sakata hai। 5. sharipha (Custard apple)- tibi ke upachaar ke lie sharipha bhi behad phaayademnd hai। shariphe ka palap nikaalakar ise khaana chaahie। kaise karen upayog do shariphon ka palap nikaalakar use paani men ubaal len, isake saath pachachis kishamish (kishmish) ko bhi ubaal len। jab paani ek tihaai rah jaae tab ise chhaamakar isamem paaudar shugar milaaen। is pey men ilaayachi aur daalachini milaakar din men do baar pien। 6. kaali mirach (Black pepper)- kaali mirach phephadon (lungs) ki saphaai ka kaam karati hai। jisase tibi ke dauraan hone vaale sine ke darad se raahat milati hai। isake saath hi yah tibi ke kitaamuon ko maarane ka kaam bhi karati hai। kaise karen upayog makakhan mem aath se das kaali mirach pharaai karem। isamen ek chutaki himg milaaen aur paaudar bana len। is misharan ko tin baraabar bhaagon men bnt lem। kuchh kuchh ghmte ke ntaraal par isaki ek ek doj khaaen। 7. akharot (Walnut)- akharot tibi ke marijon ko taakat deta hai, umaki imayooniti barhaata hai aur jaladi thik home men bhi madad karata hai। kaise karem upayog akharot ke paaudar men kuchh kali lahasun ki milaakar kuchal len। isamen kaleriphaaid makakhan (clarified butter) milaakar khaaen। akharot ko yoon bhi khaaya ja sakata hai ya isake paaudar ko salaad men daalakar khaaen। 8. pudima (Mint)- pudina men maujood entibaikatiriyal (antibacterial) gunon ke kaaran isamem bhi tibi ke rog ko thik karane ka adabhut gun hota hai। kaise karen upayog ek chamamach pudine ke ras mem do chamamach shahad milaaen, isake saath hi is ghol men maalat vinegar (malt vinegar) aur aadha kap gaajar ka joos milaaen। is ghol ko kuchh kuchh ghnton par poore din pien। Disease: pharozan sholadar (Frozen Shoulder) Description: kndhe ka darad ek bahut hi aam shikaayat hai। aisa maana jaata hai ki kndhon ke aasapaas joṛom men soojan aane ke kaaran yah darad hota hai। aise darad men kabhi-kabhaar kndhe sunan bhi paṛ jaate hain। yah sathiti kai baar mahinon tak rah jaati hai। Symptoms: - kndhom ka suman paṛ jaana - kmdhon ko ghumaane men asamarathata mahasoos hona - raat men kndhon men tivar darad hona Reasons: - daayabitij ke marijon men, haृday samasaya se garasit logon men paarakisan bimaari ke marijom men ho sakati hai। - garadan men hone vaali saravaaikal disak ki samasaya bhi aise darad ka kaaran ho sakati hai। - vo marija, jinahen kndhon par kisi parakaar ki chot lagi ho ya kmdhon ki kisi parakaar ki sarajari hui hai, umamem pharojan sholadar ki aashnka adhik hoti hai। Treatments: kndhon ki jakadn men akasar maalish ya senk se aaraam milata hai। agar isase aaraam nahin milata hai to niman upaay apanaame chaahie: - darad ko anadekha n karen। yah lagaataar ho to daॉkatar ko dikhaaem। - saamaamay kndhon ke darad men darad nivaarak davaaom se hi raahat mil jaati hai। aisa darad kmdhon mem soojan ke kaaran hota hai, isalie soojan kam karame vaali davaaen bhi raahat pahuncha sakati hain। lekin darad ki davaaon ka parayog keval aapaat sathiti men hi karen। - kndhon ko garam ya thnda sek den। - darad se jalad aaraam ke lie ekayoopnkachar chikitasa ka sahaara le sakate hain। - pharojan sholadar ki chikitasa ka sabase achachha upaay phijiyotherepi (Physiotherapy) maana jaata hai। phijiyotherepi men kndhon mem khinchaav utapanan kar kndhon ko dobaara gatimaan banaama hota hai। aisa karane ke lie kndhon ke vibhinan binduon ko vayaayaam davaara dhire-dhire saamaamay sathiti men laane ka parayaas kiya jaata hai। - pharojan sholadar (Frozen Shoulder) ki chikitasa samay par nahin ki gai to marij ko poora jivan is samasaya ke saath bitaana paṛ sakata hai। Disease: saravaaikal sapaॉnadilaaitis (Cervical Sypondolysis) Description: umar ke saath hadadiyon men ghisaav v badalaav a jaata hai। yah garadan ki hadadiyom mem bhi hota hai। hadadiyon men ghisaava, amatar ho jaane ya inake jod vaale bhaag ki mmsapeshiyon mem soojan se garadan ka darad yaani saravaaikal sapndaailosis (Cervical Spondolysis) hota hai। yah sab garadan ki us hadadi mem hota hai jise saravaaikal sapaain kahate hain। rirh ki hadadi ka garadan vaala yah bhaag merudanad (Spine) ki saat kasherookaaom (Vertebrae) evn unake madhay ki disak se banata hai। garadan ki 85 paratishat gatividhiyn upar ki do kasherookaaon ke kaaran hoti hai। garadan ke darad se hone vaali pareshaani isamen baadha pahunchaati hain। saravaaikal sapndaailosis pahale 40 varash se adhik aayu ke logon ko hota tha kinatu varatamaan samay ki jivanacharaya evn aajivika ne bachache aur badon sabhi ko garadan men darad ka marij bana diya hai। Symptoms: - garadan men akaṛana, - garadan ghumaame men chat ki aavaaj aana - garadam ghumaane men dikakat - chakakar aana - darad v bhaaripan - nasom men khinchaav se haathon men knpan aadi lakashan dikhate hai - sir ke pichhe bhaag men darad - haathon ka suman pad jaanaa, jaan n rahana Reasons: - sote samay mote takie ka upayog isaka ek kaaran hai। - baithane ki galat sathiti ke kaarana, lnbe samay tak ek jaisi sathiti men baithanaa। knpayootar par jayaada der tak kaam karane vaale vayakati, dnt chikitasaka, vaahan chaalaka, helamet dhaarak aadi ko yah anay logon ki apekasha jayaada hota hai। - vidayaarathi evn aise vayakati jo bhaari baig pith ya kmdhe par latakaae rahate hain, ve isase pidit hote hain। - kisi chot ya pharaikachar ke kaaran yah darad hota hai। - kuchh anay rogon men bhi yah darad parakat hota hai। - ek jaisi sathiti men lagaataar tivi, knpayootara, vidiyo gem aadi ke upayog se hota hai। Treatments: - garadan evn kmdhe ka vayaayaam niyamit karem। - sahi sathiti men baithen। - pair jamin par evn pith kurasi ke paृshath bhaag par sidhi rakhen। - jhukakar ya ek jaisi sathiti men lagaataar kaam n karen। - bicha-bich men kndhe, garadan ko ghumaaen। - mote takie v masanad ka upayog kam ya bnd kar den। - garadan ke darad vaale bhaag ki garam kapade se sikaai karane ya baraph ghisane se darad thik ho jaata hai, phir bhi darad bama rahe to hadadi rog visheshajaञ se milen aur upachaar laabh len। Home Remedies: saravaaikal sapndalaaitis (cervical spondylosis) ko garadam ki gathiya (meck arthritis) ke naam se bhi jaana jaata hai। is rog men garadan ke jod mem darad ki shikaayat rahati hai। yah jod kaaratileja, utak aur saravaaikal sapaain men jude rahate hain। saravaaikal sapndalaaitis adhikatar umar barhane ke saath hone lagata hai lekin kai dapha garadan par dabaav padme, baithane-uthane ke galat poshachar se, dhoomarapaan karane, vajan ke bahut jayaada hone, jenetik kaaranon aur aalasi raham sahan se bhi shuroo ho sakata hai। haalnki kuchh ghareloo upaay apanaakar saravaaikal saponadiloyasis ka upachaar snbhav hai। aaie jaanate hain kuchh aise hi upachaaron ke baare men- 1. niyamit vayaayaam (Daily excersise)- niyamit vayaayaam n karana bhi saravaaikal sapndalaaitis hone ka bada kaaran hai। niyamit vayaayaam se garadan ke darad ko kam kiya ja sakata hai। (yadi kisi bhi tarah ke vayaayaam se darad barh jaae to vayaayaam ko chhod den) 2. garam aur thmdi sikaai (Hot and cold fomentation)- garadan darad se nijaat ke lie garadan ki garam aur thndi sikaai karame se bhi bahut aaraam milata hai। garam sikaai karane se rakat snchaar behatar hota hai vahin thndi sikaai se soojan aur chubhan kam hoti hai। kaise karen upachaara- garam sikaai ke lie garam paani ki botal ko tauliya men lapet kar garadan ki sikaai karem। thndi sikaai karane ke lie baraph (ice) ke tukadon ko tauliya men lapetakara, us tauliya se sikaai karen। sikaai karate vakat kam se kam do se tin minat tak garadan ki lagaataar sikaai honi chaahie। 15 se 20 minat men dobaara doharaaen। is vidhi ko aaraam hone tak din men do baar karen। 3. lahasun (Garlic)- yadi saravaaikal sapndalaaitis ke lakashan najar aaem to lahasun ka isatemaal behad achachhe parinaam de sakata hai। isake aushadhiy gun garadan ke darada, soojan aur jalan ko thik karate hain। kaise karen upachaara- lahasun ki do kali har subah khaali pet paani ke saath khaaen। khaana bamaane vaale kisi bhi tel mem lahasun ki kuchh kaliyn daal kar bhoon len। is tel ko gumaguna hone tak thnda karen aur parabhaavit hisase ki maalish karem। is vidhi ko din men do baar kiya ja sakata hai। 4. haladi (Haldi)- haladi ke aushadhiy gun kisi se chhipe nahin hai lekin achachhi baat yah bhi hai ki yah saravaaikal sapndalaaitis ke darad mem bhi utani hi parabhaavi hai। haladi rakat snchaar tej karake garadan ke darad se aaraam deti hai aur garadan ki akadm ko bhi kam karati hai। kaise karen upachaara- ek chamamach haladi ko doodh men daalakar ubaalem aur thmda hone par isamen shahad milaaen, ise din men do baar pien। 5. til (sesame seed)- saravaaikal sapndalaaitis ke upachaar ke lie aayuraved ki besat aushadhi hai tila। isamen kailashiyama, maiganishiyama, maiganija, kaॉpara, jimka, phaॉsaphoras aur vitaamin ke (vitamin k) tatha di (vitamin d) parachur maatara men paae jaate hain। isi kaaran yah hadadiyon ke saath saath poore sharir ke lie phaayademnd hai। kaise karem upachaara- til ke tel ko gumaguna karake lagabhag 10 minat parabhaavit hisase ki masaaj karen। is kariya ko dinabhar men tin se chaar baar karen। garam sisam ke tel men kuchh boonde levendar ke tel ki daalakar bhi masaaj ki ja sakati hai। til ko halaka sa bhoonakar roj subah chabaaen। isake alaava garam doodh men bhune hue til daalakar bhi piya ja sakata hai। ek din men lagabhag do gilaas doodh pien। 6. adarak (Ginger)- saravaaikal sapndalaaitis ke ilaaj ke lie adarak bhi behatarin parabhaav dikhaata hai। yah rakat snchaar (blood circulation) ko tej karata hai jisase garadan ke darad se raahat milati hai। kaise karen upachaara- ek din mem lagabhag tin kap adarak ki chaay pien। adarak ki chaay banaane ke lie paani men adarak ubaalen aur thmda karake isamen shahad milaaen। is pey ko pien। parabhaavit hisase ki adarak ke tel se masaaj bhi ki ja sakati hai। 7. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar)- seb saaidar siraka bhi saravaaikal sapndalaaitis se raahat dene men bahut achachha asar dikhaati hai। yah garadan ke darad aur soojam se raahat deta hai। kaise karem upachaara- kisi kapade ko se saaidar siraka men bhigokar parabhaavit sathaan par lapetem aur kuchh ghnton ke lie chhod den। din mem do baar is vidhi ko karen। do kap seb ke sirake ko gumagune paani men daalakar nahaaya bhi ja sakata hai। ek gilaas paani mem kachacha seb ka siraka aur shahad milaakar pine se bhi laabh hota hai। Disease: vaakavikaar (Dyslexia) Description: disalekasiya koi bimaari nahin hai aur n hi yah koi maanasik ayogayata hai। disalekasiya (Dyslexia) paṛhane-likhane se snbndhi ek vikaar hai, jisamem bachachon ko shabadon ko pahachaanane, paṛhane, yaad karane aur bolane men pareshaani aati hai। ve kuchh akasharon aur shabadon ko ulata paṛhate hain aur kuchh akasharon ka uchachaaran bhi nahin kar paate। unaki parhane ki raphataar aur bachachon ki apekasha kaaphi kam hoti hai । Symptoms: - agar aapaka bachacha inamen se ek ya do pareshaaniyon se gujar raha hai aur vo sathaayi samasaya nahin hon to thoṛi madad se hi bachache ko raahat mil sakati hai, chaahe vo ghar par ki gai madad ho ya kakasha men - uchachaaran saaph nahin hona - utatejit rahama - kavita vaale shabadon men dikakat - kaaphi thaka hona ya ekaagarata (ek chiz par dhayaan lagaane) men kami - ginati, shabada, din aur mahimon ke naam samajhane men dikakat - daaen aur bme men mtar samajhane men dikakat hona - disha aur niradesh samajhane men pareshaami - doosare bachachon ke mukaabale der se bolana shuru karana - nmbaron ke karam aur ganit ke chinahom men ulajhan - nai chijen sikhame men deri - paṛhaai ke dauraan shabadon ki galatiyn lagaataar karana - paraaimari paṛhaai ke dauraan lakashan paṛhane - baatachit karane mem dikakat - bina soch vichaar ke kaaray karana ya kisi kaaray ko karane yojana nahin banaana - yadi ghar par aap apane bachache ke vayavahaar ke baare men satarak hain to shikashakon se jaanakaari lijie ki kaya sakool men bhi vo aisa hi vayavahaar karata hai. - logon se bolachaal karane men dikakata, apane aasapaas ki chijon ke parati asnvedanashilata jisake kaaran duraghatana ki snbhaavana bami rahati hai - varanamaala aur snkhaya ko sikhane men dikakat hona - shabadon aur dhavani ke mel ko kaaphi der se samajhana - shabadon ka matalab samajhane men deri, jayaadaatar sahi shabadon ko nahin pakaṛ paana - shabadon ki pahachaan men dikakat jaise (b/d), ulate (m/w), milate julate (felt/left) aur vaikalapik (house/home) shabad - samay ke baare men yaad rakhane ki kami - sakool se pahale ke lakasham Reasons: - vnshaanugat (Herediatary), yah tntarika tntar (Nervous System) ki samasaya hai, jo janam poorav kaarakon par nirabhar karati hain। - maata ke sntulit aahaar ki kami, dhoomarapaan ka sevan bhi isake kaaran ho sakate hain। - bachachon men kuposham bhi isaka ek baṛa kaaram hai। Treatments: - kuchh kes men bachache ke janam se pahale hi disalekasiya ka ndaaja lagaaya ja sakata hai। aise men daॉkatar un garabhavati mahilaaon ko paushatik aahaar lene ki salaah ke saath saath kuchh vishesh davaaom se snbndhit salaah dete haim। - jin maamalom men janam ke baad disalekasiya ka pata lagata hai, um bachachon ko jayaada samay dekar snbhaala ja sakata hai। in bachachon ki samajh dhimi hoti hai, isalie inahem jayaada samay dene ki aavashayakata hoti hai। - disalekasiya se pidit bachachon ke saath apana paṛhane ka apana tarika badalen, chijon ko aasaan karake bataaen, toṛa-toṛakar samajhaaen। chitaron aur kahaaniyon ka sahaara len। jin akasharon ko pahachaanane aur likhane men samasaya hoti hai, unahen baara-baar likhavaae। - vokeshanal tarenimg karaaem। Disease: pitataashay ki pathari (Gallstomes) Description: pitataashay (Gall Bladder) pitat (Bile) bhndaaran ke lie ek chhoti si thaili hai (pitat jigar davaara utapaadit ek paachak ras hai jo khaane men maujood vasa ke tootane men parayog kiya jaata hai)। pitataashay men vasaayukat khaaday padaarathon ki maatar adhik hone se pitataashay ki pathari (kolesataraॉla, pitat varamak aur kailashiyam lavam se bana chhota sa patathara) ka niramaan hota hai। Symptoms: - darad chhaati, kndhe, garadan men bhi phail sakata hai - pet aur pith men achaanak darad uthana - vasaayukat bhojan khaame ke baad pet ke darad men teji aanaa, piliyaa, bukhaar Reasons: - pitat men kolesataraॉl ki atayadhikata (Over Saturation) - pitat men lesithin - aur pitat lavan ki kam aapoorati (Undersupply)। Treatments: pitataashay ki pathari kisi bhi samasayaaon ka kaaran nahin hai lekim yadi pitataashay ki pathari snkaraman paida kar raha hai to aapareshan jaroori hai। Home Remedies: asasi phisadi pitat ki thaili ki pathari kolesataraॉl (cholestrol) ke jamane ya sakhat hone ke kaaran hoti hai। pitat ki pathari ke kaaran pet men asahaniy darad hota hai, kai baar ulati (vomit) bhi ho sakati hai। rogi ka khaana pachane men dikakat hone lagati hai jisase pet men apach (indigestiom) aur bhaaripan rahata hai। pitat ki thaili men pathari hone ke baare men yahi kaha jaata hai ki bina ऑpareshan ke ise nikaalana mushakil hai। aise men yadi aapako gaॉl baledar saton ki shikaayat hai to jaahir hai aapane bhi ऑparesham ka vichaar banaaya hogaa, lekim ऑpareshan se pahale kuchh ghareloo upaay apanaakar dekhen, snbhav hai ki pathari gal jaae। kuchh ghareloo upaay n keval pathari ko gala demge balaki paachan ko duroosat karake darad ko bhi thik kar denge। aaie jaanate hain, aise hi ghareloo upaayon ke baare men। 1. seb ka joos aur seb ka siraka (Apple and Apple cider vimegar)- seb men pitat ki pathari ko galaame ka gun hota hai, lekin ise joos ke roop men seb ke sirake ke saath lene par yah jayaada asarakaari hota hai। seb men maujood mailik esid (mallic acid) pathari ko galaane men madad karata hai tatha seb ka siraka livar men kolesataraॉl nahin banane detaa, jo pathari banane ke lie jimamedaar hota hai। yah ghol n keval pathari ko galaata hai balaki dobaara banane se bhi rokata hai aur darad se bhi raahat deta hai। upachaar ke lie- ek gilaas seb ke joos mem, ek chamamach seb ka siraka milaaen। is joos ko rojaana din bhar men do baar pien। 2. naashapaati ka joos (Pear juice)- naashapaati ke aakaar ki pitat ki thaili ko naashapaati davaara hi saaph kiya jaana snbhav hai। naashapaati mem maujood paikatin (pectene) kolesataraॉl (cholesterol) ko banane aur jamane se rokata hai। yoon bhi naashapaati gunon ki khaan hai jisake kai savaasathay laabh hain। upachaara- ek gilaas garam paani men, ek gilaas naashapaati ka joos aur do chamamach shahad (honey) milaakar pien। is joos ko ek din men tin baar pina chaahie। 3. chukndara, khira aur gaajar ka joos (Beetroot, Cucumber and carrot juice)- joos therepi ko pitat ki thaili ke ilaaj ke lie ghareloo upachaaron men sabase jayaada isatemaal kiya jaata hai। chukndar n keval sharir ka majabooti deta hai balaki gaॉl baledar ko saaph bhi karata hai saath hi livar ke kolon (colon) ko bhi saaph karata hai। khira men maujood jayaada paani ki maatara livar aur gaॉl baledar donon ko ditaॉkasiphaai (detoxify) karati hai। gaajar men bhi vitaamin si aur uchach poshak tatav (high nutrient) hone ke kaaran yahi gun hote hain। upachaara- ek chukndara, ek khira aur chaar gaajar ko lekar joos taiyaar karem। is joos ko paratidin do baar pima hai। joos men paratayek saamagari ki maatara baraabar honi chaahie, isalie sabaji ya phal ke saaij ke hisaab se maatara ghataai ya barhaai ja sakati hai। 4. pudina (Mint)- pudina ko paachan ke lie sabase achachhi ghareloo aushadhi (home remedy) maana jaata hai jo pitat vaahika tatha paachan se snbndhit anay rason ko barhaata hai। pudina men taarapin (terpenes) bhi hota hai jo ki pathari ko galaane men sahaayak maana jaata hai। pudine ki patatiyon se bani chaay gaॉl baledar saton se raahat de sakati hai। upachaara- paani ko garam karen, isamen taaji ya sookhi pudine ke patatiyon ko ubaalen। halaka gunaguna rahane par paani ko chhaanakar isamen shahad milaaen aur pi len। is chaay ko din men do baar piya ja sakata hai। 5. khaana-paan aur dinacharaya men badalaav (Chamges im diet and daily activity) rojaana 8 se 10 gilaas paani jaroor pien। chaahe payaas n bhi lagi ho। vasaayukat ya tej masaale vaale khaane se bachen। paratidin kaॉphi jaroor pien। bahut jayaada bhi nahin lekin din men ek se do kap kaaphi hain। kaॉphi bhi pitat vaahika ko barhaati hai jisase pitat ki thaili mem pathari nahin hoti। apane khaane men vitaamin si ki maatara badhaaen। dinabhar men jitana jayaada snbhav ho vitaamin si se bharapoor chijen khaaen। haladi, sauntha, kaali mirach aur hing ko khaame men jaroor shaamil karen। Disease: rebij (Rabies) Descriptiom: rebiz ek nayooro inavesiv (Neuro-Invasive) vaayaral bimaari hai। rebiz ka vaayaras tntarika tntar yaani sentaral naravas sisatam (Cemtral Nervous System) par ataik karata hai, jisase pidit vayakati saamaanay nahim rah paataa। Symptoms: - gale ki mns peshiyon men khinchaav paida ho jaata hai - pidit vayakati kutate ki tarah bhaunkane bhi lagata hai - bechaini, nshik pakashaaghaata, bharama, anidara aur nigalane men kathinaai aadi kuchh anay lakasham hain - rebij ka shikaar bane jaanavaron ka dimaagi sntulan bigadne lagata hai - rebij ho jaane par marij paani se darane lagata hai Reasons: rebij pashuon ke kaatane ke kaaran hota hai। paalatoo jaanavara, kutate, bilali ya chamakaadad ke kaatane se sabase adhik rebiz hota hai। Treatments: rebij se bachaav ke lie jaroori hai isake baaren men jaanakaari honaa। rebiz (Rabies) akasar pashuon ke kaatane ke kaaran hota hai, saath hi aise men is baat ka dhayaan rakhana chaahie ki yah siraph kaatane hi nahin chhilane ke kaaran bhi hota hai। rebiz hone par niman baaton ka dhayaam rakhana chaahie: - pashuon ke kaatame par kaate gae sathaan ko paani v saabun se achachhi tarah dho dema chaahie। - dhone ke baad kaate gae sathaan par achachhi tarah se tinchar ya povodim aayodin lagaana chaahie। aisa karane se kutate ya anay pashuon ki laar men paae jaane vaale kitaanu sirotaaipavan laayasa vaayaras ki gayaalakoparotin ki paraten ghul jaati hain। isase rog ki maar ek bade had tak kam ho jaati hai, jo rogi ke bachaav mem sahaayak hoti hai। - isake turnt baad rogi ko titenas ka injekashan lagavaakar chikitasaalay men le jaana chaahie। yahn chikitasak ki salaah se kaate gae sathaan par kaarabolik esid lagaaya jaata hai, jisase adhikatam kitaanu nashat ho jaate hain। - isake baad chikitasak ki salaah par aavashayakataanusaar injekashan lagaae jaate haim, jo tin ya das din ki avadhi ke hote hain। - tatapashachaat aavashayakataanusaar nishachit dinon par busatar doj bhi die jaane ka paraavadhaan hai, jo chikitasak ke vivek v kaate gae hai। yadi raibij ke lakashan ubharane se pahale isaka ilaaj n kiya jaae to vayakati ki maut bhi ho sakati hai। aise jaanavar jo is vaayaras se aphekated (affected) hote hain, unake salaaiva (salaiva) aane par aapako lagata hai ki raibij inphekated thaa, to sabase pahale parabhaavit hisase ko paani aur phir saabun se achachhi tarah dhoen। yadi jaanavar ne kaata ho ya aapake jakham par kharoncha ho to bilakul bhi laaparavaahi n karen। saabun aur paani se dhone ke baad turnt chikitasak se milen। 2. akharot (walnut) akharot men kutate davaara hone vaali raibij ke jahar ko maarane ki kashamata hoti hai। upachaar ke lie akharota, payaaj aur namak ki baraabar maatara lekar pis len। is mitaran men thodaa़ shahad milaaen। parabhaavit hisase ya ghaav par yah lep lagaaen। 3. levendar (lavander) jaanavar ke kaatane ke sathaan par ya raibij parabhaavit hisase par levendar ko pis kar lep lagaane se bhi imphekashan se bacha ja sakata hai। 4. lahasun (garlic) lahasun men paraakaृtik taur par entibaayetik (antibiotic) gun hote hain। raibij ke ghaav ko jaladi bharane ke lie din men tin baar lahasun ki kali chabaaen। 5. jira (cumin) kutate ke kaatane se phailame vaali raibij par jira bhi kaaphi asar dikhaata hai। do bade chamamach jira ko pisakar usamen bis kaali mirach pisakar milaaen। donon paaudar men paani milaakar lep banaaem aur parabhaavit hisase par lagaaen। isase bhi ghaav jaladi bharane men madad milegi। 6. vitaamim si (vitamin c) yadi aap raibij se inphekated hain to apame aahaar men vitaamin si ki maatara barhaaen। isake lie amarood (guawa), laal mirach (red pepper), kivi (kiwi), phool gobhi (cauli flower), sntara aur ninboo aadi lem। vitaamin si sapaliment bhi le sakate hain। 7. vitaamin bi (vitamim b) raibij ke imphekashan se bachane ko vitaamin bi bhi bahut laabhakaari hai। raibij ke upachaar ke lie apane aahaar men aise bhojan ko shaamil karen jisamen vitaamin bi parachur maatara men ho। aise khaaday padaarathon ke lie aap bndagobhi (cabbage), tamaatara, rasapabairi, tarabooja, amaanaas (pime apple) aur paalak aadi le sakate haim। isake alaava vitaamin bi ke sapaliment lena bhi phaayademnd hota hai। nota- yah sabhi upachaar ghareloo hain। inamen se kuchh upachaar jaanavar ke kaatane ke turnt baad daॉkatar ke paas pahunchame ki deri ki avasatha men pahale kie ja sakate hain, taaki inphekashan jayaada n barhe ya avasatha ghaatak n ho। saath hi kuchh upachaar ilaaj ke dauraan lagaataar kie ja sakate hain। lekin raibij hone ki sathiti men chikitasak ke paas jaana jaroori hai, ghareloo upachaar atirikat laabh ke lie hain। Disease: jukaam (Common Cold) Description: jukaam vishaanuon (vaayarasa) davaara phailaaya jaane vaale snkaramam hai jo khaasakar hamaare sns paramaali ke aage vaale hisase ko parabhaavit karata hai। jukaam sharir ki roga-paratirodhak kashamata ka parichaayak hai। Symptoms: - nkh se paani bahana - kaan men darad hona - gale men darad hona - naak se paani bahana - saradarad hona - haraarat mahasoos hona Reasons: - hava men maujood baikatiriya ya vaayaras jab kabhi sns ke jarie sharir men paravesh karate hain, to elaraji ho jaati hai। natija yah hota hai ki paani ya balagam naak se baahar aane lagate haim। - hamaare gale men do tarah ke baikatiriya maujood hote hain - kuchh achachhe aur kuchh bure। kabhi-kabhi saradi-garami baṛhane, ekadam thndaa-garam khaane, thnde se garam v garam se thnde maahaul men jaane, thnda paani jayaada pine ya baarish men bhigane se gale ke bure baikatiriya sakariy ho jaate hain। ye baikatiriya hi gale men inaphekashan kar dete hain aur jukaam (Jukam) ki vajah bamate hain। Treatmemts: jukaam ek savabhaavik kariya maami jaati hai। agar kuchhek din men yah apane aap thik ho jaae to ise bimaari nahin maana jaata lekin adhik din rahane par isaka upachaar karaana jaroori hota hai। jukaam ke kuchh khaas upaay niman hain: - saadhaaran jukaam apane aap pnch din men thik ho jaata hai। - agar balagam saphed ho to yah elaraji ki nishaani hai। yah saadhaaran jukaam hota hai। - jukaam ko pnch din se jayaada ho jaaen ya saath men khnsi, balagama, badan darad v bukhaar bhi ho, to samajhama chaahie ki aam jukaam nahin hai। - agar balagam pila ho ho v sns ki dikakat ke saath bukhaar bhi ho to baikatiriyal inphekashan hota hai। - aise men daॉkatar ke paas jaana chaahie। - agar kaf ke saath khoon bhi aae to chintaajanak baat hai। yah ti.bi. ka lakashan ho sakata hai। aise men turanat daॉkatar se paraamarash len। Home Remedies: jukaam snkaraman (Infection) ka ek parakaar hai jo ki vaayaras ke vibhinan parakaar ke kaaranon se ho sakata hai। sir darada, naak bahanaa, khnsi, tej bukhaara, nkhon men jalana, gale men kharaash (Sore throat) aur sharir men darad (Body pain) aadi saamaanay jukaam ke kuchh lakasham hain। jukaam se raahat ke lie kai ghareloo upachaar hain jo ki jukaam ki samasaya se raahat de sakate haim। yah ghareloo upachaar kisi bhi dushaparabhaav ke bima saradi ke vibhinan lakashanon se parabhaavi raahat paradaan karate hain। 1. lahasun (Garlic) - lahasun ka jivaamurodhi aur emtivaayaral (antiviral) gun saradi ke lakashanon se chhutakaara paraapat karane men bahut sahaayak hota hai। lahasun paratirakasha paranaali (immunity) ke lie achachha hai aur shavasan maarag (respiratory process) ko kholane men madad karata hai। kaise karen upayog - ek kap paani men lahasun ki kali, do chamamach ninboo ka rasa, ek chamamach shahada, aur aadha chamamach laal mirach ya laal mirach paaudar milaaen। ise tab tak roj khaaen jab tak saradi jukaam se aaraam na ho। - ek kap paani men 4-5 kate hue lahasun ki kali ubaal len aur ek chamamach shahad daalen। ise din men do se tin baar sevan karen। 2. shahad (Honey) - shahad men maujood enjaaim (enzyme) men, uchach maatara men baikatiriya aur vaayaras ko maarane ke gun hote hain। shahad se gale ka sookhaapan door hota hai aur jukaam jaladi thik ho jaata hai। kaise karen upayog - sabase saral upaay ghar par ek chamamach ninboo ka ras aur do chamamach shahad milaaen। thmdak aur gale men kharaash se raahat paane ke lie har do ghnte men len। yadi aap chaahem, to ek chamamach kachacha shahad bhi kha sakate hain। 3. masaala chaay (Masal chai) - kichan men rakhe masaalon se bani chaay jukaam men bahut jaladi raahat deti hai। kaise karen upayog - ek chauthaai kap sookha bhune hue dhaniya bij pisakar isamen aadha chamamach jira aur saunph ke bij aur ek chauthaai chamamach methi ke bij milaaen। ab ek kap paani ubaal len aur isamen aadha chamamach taiyaar masaala aur aadha chamamach mishari daalen। tin se chaar minat ubaalen। isake baad doodh daalem aur garam garam pien। 4. adarak (ginger) - adarak apame entivaayarala, esapekataremat (expectorant) gunon ke kaaran saradi se raahat deta hai। kaise karen upayog - kachacha adarak khaane ya ek din men adarak ki chaay kai baar pine se laabh hota hai। adarak ki chaay ke parabhaav ko baṛhaane ke lie, chaay men ninboo ka ras aur shahad milaaen। - adaraka, laung aur namak ka ek pesat taiyaar karen। aadha chamamach kha sakate hain। - naak bah rahi ho to baraabar maatar men sookha adarak paaudar (Dry ginger powder) makakhan ya ghi aur guṛ (jaggary) milaakar chhoti chhoti goli banaaen। subah rojaana khaali pet ek goli khaaen। 5. laal payaaj ka sirap (Syrup of red onion) - ghar ke bane laal payaaj sirap se bhi saradi se piṛit logon ko raahat milati hai। kaise karem upayog - 2-3 laal payaaj ko baarik gol tukadon mem kaat len। ek baratan men payaaj ka ek tukaṛa rakhen aur kachacha shahad milaaen। jab tak baratan bhar n jaae tab tak parakariya ko doharaaen। katore ko dhak kar rakhen aur 12 se 15 ghnte ke lie chhoṛ den। payaaj sirap ki tarah moti parat mem jam jaaegaa। 6. chikan ka soop (Chicken soup) - chikan soop kai men kai aavashayak poshak tatav vitaamin hain jo aam saradi ke lakashanon ke upachaar men madad karate haim। chikan soop ke uchach entiऑkasident gun jukaam ko thik karane ki parakariya men teji laate hain। saravotatam parinaamon ke lie, jaivik sabajiyon aur chikan ka upayog kara, ghar ka bana chikan soop taiyaar karem। Disease: bukhaar (Fever) Description: bukhaar aana ek behad aam bimaari hoti hai। vijaञaan ke anusaar yah bukhaar rog nahin balaki rog ka lakashan hota hai। jaanien bukhaar ke baaren men visataar se: Reasons: - shavasan snsathaam vaale bukhaar jaise ki jukaama, phaloo, gale ki soojana, shavaasanali shotha, nayoomoniyaa, ti.bi. aadi। - tavacha ke snkaraman (Imfectiom) se hone vaale bukhaar jaise ki jakham men pip honaa, phode ya daane vaale bukhaara। - machachhar ya pisasoo se hone vaale bukhaar jaise ki maleriya (Malari Fever), phaayaleriya (Flaria), dengoo (Dengue), chikunagumaya (Chickengunia), masatishak javar (Memingitis), paleg (Plague), aadi। in sabhi bukhaaron men pahale knpaknpi hoti hai। - paachan snsathaan ke bukhaar jaise dasat ya pechisha, piliyaa, taayaphaॉid aadi। pechish men khoon aur balagam girata hai। taayaphaaid khoon ke jaॉnch se hi pata chalata hai। - parajanan aur mootar smsathaan ke bukhaar - isamen peshaab ke samay jalan hoti hai। - anay snkaraamak bukhaar jaise ki baruselaॉsisa, edasa, tapedik ke kuchh parakaara, jodon ka bukhaara। asnkaraamak bukhaaron men jaise loo lagana aur ऍlaraji se hone vaale bukhaara। Treatments: bukhaar aane par rogi ke sharir ka taapamaan dekhana chaahie aur agar taapamaan adhik ho to daॉkatar ki salaah leni chaahie। bukhaar (Bukhar) aame ke dauraan rogi ko niman saamaamay upachaar bhi diya ja sakata hai: - rogi ko khoob saara savachachh evn ubala hua paani pilaaen, sharir ko parayaapat kailori dene ke lie galookoja, phalom ka ras aadi den। - aasaani se pachane vaala khaana jaise chaaval ki knji, saaboodaane ki khir ya khichadi, jau ka paami aadi dena chaahiye। - rogi ko achachhe havaadaar kamare men rakhama chaahiye। - savachachh evn mulaayam vasatar pahanaaen। - yadi javar 39.5 digari se. ya 103.0 phairenahaait se adhik ho ya phir 48 ghmton se adhik samay ho gaya ho to daॉkatar se paraamarash len। Home Remedies: jab bhi sharir ka taapamaan saamaanay se jayaada hota hai to yah bukhaar kahalaata hai। kai baar mausam men parivaratan ya snkaraman ke kaaran bukhaar ho jaata hai। bachachon men imayooniti kamajor hone, kaan men inphekashan hone ya peshaab men inphekashan hone par bhi bukhaar hota hai । itana hi mahin saapha- saphaai ka abhaav home se bhi bukhaar hone ki snbhaavana rahati hai। bukhaar ke saamaanay lakashamom men sir darad (Headache), mnsapeshiyon men darad (Muscle pain) , dihaadareshan (Dehydration) , kai dapha knpakapi (Shivring) to kai baar pasina aana aur kamajori ho sakate hain। yoon to bukhaar kuchh din men thik ho jaata hai lekin phir bhi kuchh ghareloo upaayon ka apanaakar aap jaladi thik ho sakate hain। ghareloo upaayon ke baad bhi yadi bukhaar n utar raha ho ya barh raha ho to turnt chikitasak ki salaah leni chaahie। bukhaar ke lie ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies for Fever) thnda paani (Cold Water) kisi kapade ko thnde paani men bhigokar sharir ko ponchhe। isake alaava thnde paani ki patatiyn sir par rakhane se bhi laabh hota he aur sharir ka taapamaan kam hota hai। kapade ko samaya-samay par badalate rahana chaahie। saamaanay bukhaar ke lie yah behad achachhi parakariya hai jo taapamaan ko barhane nahin deti। tulasi (Basil) tulasi bukhaar men sharir ke taapamaan ko kam karame men bahut sahaayak hai। yah harab baajaar men maujood amay emtibaayotikas (Antibiotics) ki tarah hi kaaray karati hai aur parabhaavi bhi hai। bukhaar ko thik karane ke lie tulasi ki bis patati aur ek chamamach kasa hua adarak lekar ek kap paani men ubaalen। thnda karake isamen shahad milaaen aur pi len। is vidhi ko din men do baar karen। tulasi ki patati aur kaali mirach paaudar ko milaakar bhi chaay banaai ja sakati hai jisase sharir ka taapamaan kam hota hai। is chaay ko din men do se tin baar pi sakate hain। seb saaidar siraka (Apple Cider Vinegar) seb saaidar siraka bhi bukhaar ke lie behad sasati aur parabhaavi dava hai। seb saaidar siraka bukhaar ko teji se kam karata hai kayonki isamen maujood esid garamaahat ko sharir ki tavacha se baahar kar deta hai। saath hi isamen maujood minaral sharir ko bukhaar se door bhi rakhate hain। kisi kapade ko ek bhaag siraka aur do bhaag paani lekar usamen bhigoen। atirikat paani ko nichod den aur is patati ko maathe aur pet par rakhen। ek patati pair ke talavon par bhi rakhi ja sakati hai। jaise hi kapada garam ho jaae, dobaara solayooshan men dubaaen aur parakariya ko doharaaen। lahasun (Garlic) lahasun ki garam taasir bhi sharir men pasina laakara, sharir ka taapamaan kam kar sakati hai। yah sharir se haamikaarak vishaakat padaarathon ko bhi baahar nikaalane men sahaayak hai। itana hi nahin lahasun entiphngal (antifungal) aur entibaikatiriyal gunom se bhara hai jo sharir ko imayooniti (Immunity) deta hai। lahasun ki ek kali ko pisakar garam paani men milaaen। 10 minat dhak kar rakhen। paani ko chhaan len aur ghoonta-ghoont karake dhire-dhire piem। ek din men is pey ko do baar pien। agale hi din aap bukhaar se raahat mahasoos karenge। do chamamach oeliv ऑyal (Olive Oil) men do kali lahasun ki daalakar bhoonen। is tel ko thmda karake pair ke talavon men lagaaem। kishamish (Raisin) kishamish sharir ke inphekasham se ladne aur bukhaar se raahat dene ki kashamata rakhati hai। kishamish mem phinolik saayetonayootariyent (Phemolic Phytonutriemts) aur entiऑkasident (Antioxident) gun hote hain। aadhe kap paani men ek ghnte ke lie 25 kishamish bhigaaen, jab tak ki kishamish naram ho jaaen। kishamish ko paani ke ndar hi masal den aur paani ko chhaanakar alag kar len। is joos men aadhe ninboo ka ras milaaen। mitaran ko ek din men do baar pien। adarak (Ginger) adarak men sharir ke taapamaam ko niyntarit karane ke gum hote hain। yoon bhi adarak paraakaृtik roop se enti vaayaral (Anti Viral) aur entibaikatiriyal (Anti Becterial) ejemt se bharapoor hota hai। paani men adarak daalakar ubaalen aur use thnda karake chhaamakar usamen, shahad milaakar pi len। is tarah se bani chaay ko din men tin se chaar baar piya ja sakata hai। derh chamamach adarak ka rasa, ek chamamach ninboo ka ras (Lemon Juice) aur ek badi chamamach shahad milaakar is mikasachar ko pien। is mitaran ko bhi din men tim se chaar bar liya ja sakata hai। Disease: gale men kharaash (Sore Throat) Description: mausam badalate hi gale men kharaash homa aam baat hai। saamaanay shabadon men gale mem kharaasha, gale ka snkaraman (Infection) hai। aamataur par gale ka smkaraman (Infection) vaayaras ya baikatiriya ke kaaran hota hai। Symptoms: - 100.5 darigi F ya 38 darigi selasiyas se adhik bukhaar hona - garadan men soojan hona - gale men darad hona - nigalane men kathinaai hona - pet men darad hona - bhookh n lagana hona - mitali ya ulati hona - sharir men pida hona - sns lene men kathinaai hona Reasons: - badalata mausam men akasar kharaash ki samasaya ka saamana karama padta hai। - kabhi kabhi khaane pine ki chizom ke viparit parabhaav ke kaaran bhi gale men snkaramam ho sakata hai। - isake alaava gale men kharaash ki samasaya anuvnshik bhi ho sakati hai। - thnde, khatate, evn tale hue khaaday padaarathon ko khaane ke kaaran bhi gale men sakaraman ho sakata hai। Treatments: gale ki kharaash ka ilaaj (Treatment of Sore Throat) - namak ke gunagune paani se garaare karen। isase gale mem aaraam milegaa। - adaraka, ilaayachi aur kaali mirach vaali chaay gale ki kharaash (Sore Throat) men aaraam pahunchaati hai। - kam masaale vaala bhojan len। - pharij ka thnda paani n pien, n hi anay thndi chijen khaaen। Home Remedies: saamaanayath gale ki mdarooni parat men snkaraman ke kaaran gale mem kharaash hoti hai। isake alaava kabhi kabhi mausam mem achaanak badalaav hone ki vajah se gale mem kharaash hoti hai aur kai baar tomsil (tonsil) ya gale men kisi tarah ke inphekashan ke kaaran bhi kharaash ho sakati hai। vaise to gale ki kharaash tin chaar din men thik ho jaati hai, lekin kuchh ghareloo upaayon se gale ki kharaash men jaladi raahat milati hai। aaie jaanen gale ki kharaash door karane ke ghareloo upaay 1. garam paani aur namak ke garaare (Gargle of warm water and salt)- jab gale men kharaash hoti hai to shaleshama jhilali (mucous membrane) ki koshikaaon men soojan ho jaati hai। namak is soojan (swellimg) ko kam karata hai jisase darad men raahat milati hai। upachaar ke lie ek gilaas gunagune paani men ek bada chamamach mamak milaakar ghol len aur is paani se garaare karen। is parakariya ko din men tin baar karem। 2. lahasun (Garlic)- lahasun inphekashan (infection) paida karane vaale jivaanuon ko maar deta hai। isalie gale ki kharaash men lahasun behad phaayademnd hai। lahasun men maujood elisim (allicin) jivaanuon ko maarane ke saath hi gale ki soojam aur darad ko bhi kam karata hai। upachaar ke lie gaalon ke donon taraph lahasum ki ek ek kali rakhakar dhire dhire choosate rahen। jaise jaise lahasun ka ras gale men jaaega vaise vaise aaraam milata rahegaa। lahasum ka ras nikaalane ke lie bich bich men dnton se kuchalate rahen। 3. bhaap lena (Steaming)- kai baar gale ke sookhane ke kaaran bhi gale men imphekashan ki shikaayat hoti hai। aise men kisi bade baratan men garam paani karake tauliya se munh dhakakar bhaap len। aisa karane se bhi gale ki sikaai hogi aur gale ka inphekashan bhi khatam hogaa। is kariya ko din men do baar kiya ja sakata hai। 4. laal mirach (Red chilli)- gale ki kharaash ko thik karane ke lie laal mirach bhi behad phaayademnd hai। upachaar ke lie ek kap garam paani mem ek chamamach laal mirach aur ek chamamach shahad milaakar pien। 5. beking soda (Baking soda)- gale ki kharaash door karane ke lie beking soda ki chaay behad phaayademnd hai। kaarana, beking soda men enti baikatiriyal (antibacterial) gun hote hain jo ki jivaanuom ko nashat kar dete hain। isake lie ek gilaas garam paani men beking soda aur namak milaakar din men tin baar garaare karen। 6. laung (Laung or Clove)- laung ka isatemaal upachaar ke lie sadiyon se hota a raha hai। gale ki kharaash ke upachaar ke lie laung ko munh men rakhakar dhire dhire chabaana chaahie। laung entibaikatiriyal gunon se bharapoor hoti hai jo gale ke inphekashan aur soojan ko door karati hai। 7. adarak (Ginger)- adarak bhi gale ki kharaash ki behad achachhi dava hai। adarak men maujood entibaikatiriyal gun gale ke inphekashan aur darad se raahat dete hain। gale ki kharaash ke upachaar ke lie ek kap paani men adarak daal kar ubaalen। isake baad ise halaka gunaguna karake isamem shahad milaaen। is pey ko din men do se tin baar pien। gale ki kharaash se aaraam milegaa। 8. masaala chaay (Masal Chay)- launga, tulasi (basil), adarak aur kaali mirach (black pepper) ko paani men daalakar ubaalen, isake baad isamen chaay patati daalakar chaay banaaen। is chaay ko garam garam hi pien। yah bhi gale ke lie behad laabhadaayak upaay hai jisase gale men turnt aaraam milata hai। Disease: ubakaai (Nausea) Description: ubakaai aama ulati hone ka ehasaas maatar hai। kuchh logom ko mitali jayaada aati hai। visheshakar yaatara ke samay kuchh logon ko ubakaai ki samasaya hoti hai। ise mosham sikames (Motion Sickness) bhi kahate hain। yah gaadi se yaatara ke dauraan ya ya naav se yaatara ke dauraan (Se Sickness) vishesh roop se mahasoos kiya jaata hai। Symptoms: - dil ki dhaṛakan baṛh jaati hai - pasina aane lagata hai - pet men gaṛabaṛi ka ehasaas hone lagata hai Reasons: yaatara ke dauraan mitali aana behad saamaanay baat hai lekin kai vajahon se yah agar lagaataar aae to ek samasaya ho sakati hai। mitali niman kaaranon se bhi aati hai: mitali aur ulati ke saamaamay kaaran (Reasom of Nausea) - ainti baayotik (Anti Biotic) davaaiyom ke kaaran akasar pet men gaṛabaṛi ho jaati hai jo mitali ya ulati ka kaaram ban jaata hai। - kuchh logon ko yaatara ke dauraan mitali, ulati ka anubhav hota hai। isake liye isaki davaॉne aadha ghnta poorav lekar hi chale। - badahajami se, amalata (Acidity), sharaab aadi se bhi mitali ki samasaya ho sakati hai। - garabhaavasatha men pahale timaahi men mitali ya ulati ki samasaya (nause during pregnancy) hoti hai। yah apane aap ruk jaati hai। mitali aur ulati ki samasaya garabhadhaaran ke samay sharir men haaramonal badalaav ke kaaran hota hai। sharir men vitaamin bi6 ki kami se bhi garabhavati mahila ko ulati hone ki samasaya ho sakati hai। - phood elaraji aur phood asahishamuta (Food Intolerance) - maaigaren men sir ke bhitar kisi bhi parakaar ke dabaav se seribaro-sapaainal phalooid (Cerebro-Spinal Fluid) parabhaavit hota hai jisake kaaran mitali ya ulati ki samasaya utapanan hoti hai। - pitataashay (Gall Bladder) aur paachak garnthi (Pancreas) men soojan hone par pet ke upari bhaag men darad hota hai aur mitali aur ulati home lagati hai। - kabhi kabhi ऍkasident ya gndagi badaboo ke kaaran bhi mitali a sakati hai। - tanaava, bhay aur bechaini ke kaaran sharir ki kariya men asntulan paida ho jaata nahin kar paate hain, himolaayatis ki sathiti kai kaaranon se paida ho sakati hain, kaaran aanuvnshik aur reda-balad selas ka ati niramaan ho sakata hai isake alaava kai avasatha men saamaamay
