maatara sharir ke vajan ke mutaabik 3 se 5 garaam hoti hai। yadi yah maatara is smkhaya se kam ho jaati hai to sharir men himogalobin banana kam ho jaata hai aur sharir men khoon ki kami ho jaati hai। isaka ek mukasaan yah bhi hai ki sharir ki koshikaaon men ऑkasijan ki aavaajaahi (Oxygen circulation) kam ho jaati hai jisase sharir ka parayaapat uraja nahin mil paati aur vayakati enimiya se garasat ho jaata hai। isake saath hi yadi sharir men pholik esid aur vitaamim bi 12 ki kami hai tab bhi vayakati enimiya se garasat ho sakata hai। purooshon ki tulana men mahilaaen jayaada enimik paai jaati hain। sharir ka jaladi thakanaa, chakakar aanaa, tavacha mem pilaapana, lagaataar rahane vaala sir darad aadi kuchh enimiya ke lakashamom mem shaamil haim। aaie aapako bataate hain, enimiya se raahat paane ke ghareloo upaay (Home remedies for anemia) 1. paalak (Spinach) paalak men bharapoor lauh tatha vitaamin bi 12 hota hai। isake saath hi paalak pholik esid (Folic Acid) ka bhi uchach satarot hai। aise men paalak khaane se khoon ki kami poori hoti hai। upachaar ke lie paalak ka soop banaakara, ya paalak ka saag aadi ko apane roj ke khaane men shaamil karana chaahie। 2. anaar (Pomegranate) anaar sharir men himogalobin (Haemoglobin) ko bahut teji se barhaata hai। anaar men parotin aur kaarabohaaidaret ki uchach maatara hoti hai। isamen aayaram aur kailashiyam bhi hota hai। yah khoon men himogalobim ki maatara ko teji se barhaakar rakat snchaar ko thik rakhata hai। enimiya ke upachaar ke lie subah khaali pet anaar khaaen aur rojaana anaar ka joos pien। 3. chukndar aur seb ka ras (Beetroot and Apple Juice) chukndar men pholik esid uchach maatara men hota hai jabaki seb men lauh tatav hote hain, aise men donon hi enimiya ki kami ko door karate haim। upachaar ke lie ek kap chukndar ke ras aur ek kap seb ke ras men ek se do chamamach shahad milaakar din men do baar pien। 4. tamaatar (Tomato) sharir ke lie bahut jayaada aayaran ki maatara lene ke saath hi yah bhi jaroori hai ki aayaran ko aapaka sharir sokhe। isamen tamaatar aham bhoomika mibhaata hai। rojaana ek se do kachache tamaatar jaroor khaaem। ek gilaas tamaatar ka ras bhi roj pien aur khaana banaane aur salaad men bhi tamaatar ka bharapoor upayog karen। 5. khajoor (Dates) khajoor bhi aayaran bahut achachha satarot hai। sau garaam khajoor men 90 miligaraam aayaran ki maatara hoti hai। do khajoor ko ek kap doodh men raat bhar ke lie chhod den। in khajoor ko subah khaali pet chaba chabaakar khaaen। bache hue doodh ko bhi pi len। khajoor ko garam paani men do ya tin ghmton ke lie bhigaakar us paami ko pina bhi phaayademnd hota hai। jim logon ko lekatoj (lectose) se elaraji hai aur doodh mahin le sakate, unake lie yah behatar tarika hai। 6. kishamish (Kishmish) kishamish bhi enimiya ki behad achachhi ghareloo dava hai। kishamish men aayarama, parotina, phaaibara, sodiyam jaise uchach poshak tatav hote hain। upachaar ke lie ek kap paani men 10 se 15 kishamish raatabhar ke lie bhiga dem। subah im kishamish ko shahad milaakar kha lem aur bache hue paani ko pi lem। 7. shahad (Honey) shahad bhi lauh aur vitaamin bi 12 ka uchach satarot hai। shahad ko rojaana khaane se bhi sharir men emimiya ki kami poori hoti hai। shahad ko phalon men milaakara, doodh men daalakar ya chini ki jagah shahad isatemaal karake bhi rakat ki kami poori ki ja sakati hai। Disease: dimenshiya (Dementia) Description: dimenshiya (Dementia) vayakati ke masatishak ko parabhaavit karane vaali bimaari hoti hai। alajaaimaras ki bimaari (Alziehmers Disease) aur vasakayular dimenshiya (Vascular Dementia) isake sabase aam parakaar (Common Type) haim। Symptoms: - apane aap men gumasum rahanaa, mela-jol bnd kar demaa, chupapi saadhama - kapade ulate pahananaa, saaf-suthara n rah paana - kisi baat ko ya parashan ko doharaanaa, jidad karanaa, tarak n samajh paama - kisi vasatu ka chitar dekhakar yah n samajh paana ki yah kaya hai - kuchh kaam shuroo karanaa, phir bhool jaana ki kaya karana chaahate the, aur bahut koshish ke baad bhi yaad m kar paana - chizon ko galata, anuchit jagah par rakh chhodana (jaise ki ghadi ko, ya ऑphis phaail ko pharij men rakh denaa) - chhoti chhoti samasayaaon ko bhi n sulajha paana - chhoti-chhoti baat para, ya bina kaaran hi baukhala jaanaa, chilalaanaa, ronaa, itayaadi - dimenshiya se parabhaavit vayakati men, rog ke barhane ke saath jayaada aur adhik gmbhir lakashan nazar aate hain। (yaad rakhen ki har vayakati men alag alag lakashan mazar aate hain) - nnbar jodne aur ghataane men dikakata, ginati karane men dikakat - bolate ya likhate hue galat shabad ka parayog karanaa, ya shabadon ke arath n samajh paana - badi rakam ko phaalatoo ki sakim men daal denaa, paise se samabndhit ajib niranay lenaa, laaparavaahi ya gairajimamedaari dikhaana - yah bhool jaana ki taarikh kaya hai, kaunasa mahina hai, saal kaunasa hai, vayakati kis ghar mem hain, kis shahar men hain, kis desh men Reasons: ​dimenshiya kai kaaranon se ho sakata hai lekin isaka mukhay kaaran aanuvnshik hi maana jaata hai। saath hi barhati umar men is bimaari se pidit hone ki smbhaavana bhi barh jaati hai। isake aham kaarak nimam hain: dimenshiya ke paramukh kaaran (Causes of Dementi ​in Hindi) - aanuvnshika: agar parivaar men koi bhi is bimaari se piṛit ho, to khatare ki snbhaavana ba़dh jaati hai - barhati umar men is bimaari ke khatare barh jaate hain। - uchach rakatachaap se pidit rogiyon ko dimenshiya ke parati sachet rahana chaahie। - madhumeh aur motaape ko bhi isaka mukhay kaaran maana jaata hai। - zayaada jnk phood khaane se aur aadhunik jivanashaili se sharir se jaroori poshak tatav mahin mil paate jis kaaran dimenshiya (Dementia) hone ki snbhaavana barh jaati hai। Treatments: dimenshiya se bachaav aur isaka ilaaj donon hi snbhav hai। jaroori hai to keval sahi samay par isaki jaanakaari honaa। dimenshiya ke dauraan niman baaton ka dhayaan rakhana jaroori hai: - dimenshiya ka vayakati aur parivaar par kaya asar padegaa, yah samajhen aur savikaarem। - dekhabhaal kai varashon tak chal sakati hai, isalie yah jaanana jaroori hai ki rogi ki dekhabhaal ke alaava aur kaya kaya jimamedaariyn nibhaani haim aur dekhabhaal ke lie samay aur paise ka intajaam kis parakaar karenge। - isalie apami jindagi men usi parakaar se badalaav laaen taaki rogi ki dekhabhaal ke saath saath aap apani anay jimamedaariyn bhi nibha saken। isake lie jo bhi sikhana hai, vah sikhen, aur khushi khushi apane karatavay ka niravaah karen। Home Remedies: dimenshiya ya yaadadaashat ka jaana sabhi ke lie chinta ka kaaran ho sakata hai। ham sabhi apane dimaag ko savasath rakhana chaahate hain। dimemshiya ke marij ki yaadadaashat (memmory) jaane ke saath hi usake vayavahaar men bhi parivaratan hota hai jisase n keval marij balaki parivaar ke anay sadasay bhi parabhaavit hote hain। aaie jaanen dimenshiya se bachane ke lie kuchh ghareloo upachaara- 1. chini ko avaॉid karen (Avoid sugar) sabase pahale apane khaane se mitha (sweet), kaarabohaaidaret (carbohydrate) tatha riphaaind kaarabohaaidaret (refimed carbohydrate) sabhi ko alag kar den। jab tak ki aapaka vajan niyntarit nahin ho jaata hai, kaarabohaaidat vaali chijon ko khaane se bachen। bahut adhik chini kho se bhi dimaagi utak (brain membrane) kamajor hote haim jisaka asar yaadadaashat (memmory) par padta hai। 2. haladi (Haldi) haladi men maujood tatav karakayoomin (curcumin) dimemshiya se surakasha paradaan karata hai। haladi men emtiऑkasident (antioxidant) tatav bhi hote hain jo dimaagi vikaas ke lie jaroori hain। aise men bhojan mem haladi ka isatemaal jaroor karen। 3. naariyal tel (Coconut oil) naariyal tel men khaana banaane se bhi dimenshiya ka upachaar snbhav hai। maariyal tel men vasa ki maatara bahut jayaada nahin hoti aur yah dimaag ko bhi tej karata hai। 4. salaman machhali aur nda (Salmon fish and egg) thnde paani (cold water) men rahane vaali machhali salamam aur nde ki jaradi (egg yolk) donom hi dimaag ko tej bamaati hain। aise men bhojan men donon ko shaamil kiya jaana behad jaroori hai। ek din men do nde jaroor khaaen। 5. adarak (Ginger) adarak bhi dimenshiya se bachaav ke lie behad phaayademnd hai। adarak ki chaay (ginger tea), khaane mem adarak ka parayog ya sookha adarak (dry ginger), kisi bhi roop men adarak khaana dimenshiya men behad laabhadaayak hai। 6. garin ti (Green tea) garin ti bhi achachhe savaasathay v achachhe dimaagi vikaas ke lie behad jaroori hai। garim ti pine se sharir men ऑkasijan (Oxygen) ka snchaar hota hai aur jami hui vasa (Saturated fat) door hoti hai। isase yaadadaashat barhati hai aur bhoolane ki samasaya door hoti hai। 7. baadaam (Almond) baadaam bhi tej dimaag ke lie phaayademmd hota hai। baadaam ke tel men vasa hoti hai jise khaane se charabi nahin barhati aur dimaag ko anay poshak tatav (nutrient) bhi milate hain, jisase n keval sharir balaki dimaag bhi savasath hota hai। Disease: taaiphaaid (Typhoid) Description: taaiphaaid ya nt javar ek gnbhir bimaari hai। is bimaari men rogi ko tej bukhaar ke saath ulati aur dasat aadi ki samasaya hoti hai। taaiphaaid (Typhoid) ek jaanaleva bimaari maani jaati hai। aaien jaanen isake vishay men adhik jaanakaari। Symptoms: - kabaj ya dasat homa - kabhi-kabhi shauch men khoon ka aama - bukhaar shuroo men halakaa, par dhire-dhire tej hota jaata hai - bhookh kam lagana aur ulatiym aana - rog ki gnbhir sathiti men behoshi bhi a sakati hai - sira-darad aur badana-darad - sookhi khmsi aana aur pet men darad Reasons: maana jaata hai ki taaiphaaid adhikaatar gndagi ke kaaran phailata hai। shauch ke baad snkaramit vayakati davaara haath thik se n dhona aur bhojam banaama ya bhojan ko chhoona bhi rog phaila sakata hai। kuchh anay kaaran niman haim: - un kashetaron men kaam karana ya yaatara karana jahn yah bimaari hai। - galat jivana-shaili ke kaaran sharir ke rog paratirodhak tntar ka kamajor honaa। - pine ke paani ka jivaanu se paradooshit honaa। - shauch ke baad saapha-saphaai ka dhayaan na rakhanaa। Treatments: taaiphaaid ka upachaar (Treatment of Typhoid in Hindi) - daॉkatar ke paraamarash se balad tesat ke baad hi daॉkatar ke paraamarash ke anusaar hi chikitasa karaaem। - taaiphaaid ki dava ko bich men n chhoden। bukhaar men peraasitaamol ka isatemaal karen। - rogi ke sharir men paani ki kami n hone paae, isake lie rogi ko paani aur amay taral padaarath parayaapat maatara men den। - rogi ke aasapaas saapha-saphaai ka vishesh dhayaan rakhen। Home Remedies: taaiphaaid ka bukhaar paachan tntar aur baladasatarim (blood stream) men baikatiriya ke inphekasham ke kaaran hota hai। salomomela taaiphi (salomomel typhi) naam ka yah baikatiriya (bacteria) paani, kisi pey ya khaane ke saath hamaare sharir ke ndar paravesh karata hai aur paachan tntar mem jaakar yah baikatiriya barh jaate hain। yah baikatiriya sharir ke bhitar ek jagah se doosari jagah jaise, livara, sapalina, gaॉlabaledar aadi jagahon par ghoomate rahate hain। taaiphaaid ka bukhaar adhiknshat dooshit paani (polluted water) pine se hota hai। taaiphaaid ke lakashanon men sir men darad (headache), pet men darad (pain in stomach) aur bukhaar ka hona hai lekin taaiphaaid ke bigadne par ulati (Vomiting), daayariya (diarrhea), mal men khoon aana (blood in stool), livar ka barhana (enlargement of liver) aadi bhi ho sakate hain। taaiphaaid men laaparavaahi nahin baratani chaahie tatha isaka koras poora kiya jaana bhi jaroori hai kayonki isake dobaara hone ke chnses bhi rahate hai। taaiphaaid se nijaat ke lie yahn ham aapako kuchh ghareloo musakhon ke baare men bataaemge jinahen apanaakar aap taaiphaaid se raahat pa sakate hain। 1. thnda paani (Cold water) kisi kapade ko thnde paani men bhigokar sharir ko ponchhe। isake alaava thnde paami ki patatiyn sir par rakhane se bhi laabh hota he aur sharir ka taapamaan kam hota hai। kapade ko samay samay par badalate rahana chaahie। saamaanay bukhaar ke lie yah behad achachhi parakariya hai jo taapamaan ko barhane nahim deti। nota- isake lie baraph ya baraph ke paani ki isatemaal n karake, taaje paani ka isatemaal karen। 2. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vinegar) seb ka siraka bhi bukhaar ke lie behad sasati aur parabhaavi dava hai। isase bukhaar ko teji se door hota hai kayonki isamen maujood esid garamaahat ko sharir ki tavacha se baahar kar deta hai। saath hi isamen maujood minaral sharir ko bukhaar se door bhi rakhate hain। kaise karen upayog kisi kapade ko ek bhaag siraka aur do bhaag paani lekar usamen bhigoen। atirikat paani ko nichod den aur is patati ko maathe aur pet par rakhen। ek patati pair ke talavon par bhi rakhi ja sakati hai। jaise hi kapada garam ho jaae, dobaara ghol men dubaaen aur parakariya ko doharaaen। 4. lahasun (Garlic) lahasun ki garam taasir bhi sharir men pasina laakara, sharir ka taapamaan kam kar sakati hai। yah sharir se haamikaarak vishaakat padaarathon ko bhi baahar nikaalane mem sahaayak hai। itana hi nahim lahasun entiphngal (antifungal) aur entibaikatiriyal (Antibacterial) gunon se bhara hai jo sharir ko imayooniti (Immunity) deta hai। kaise karen upayog lahasun ki ek kali ko pisakar garam paani men milaaen। 10 minat dhak kar rakhen। paani ko chhaan len aur ghoont ghoont karake dhire dhire pien। ek din men is pey ko do baar pien। agale hi din aap bukhaar se raahat mahasoos karenge। do chamamach ऑliv ऑyal (olive oil) men do kali lahasun ki daalakar bhoonem। is tel ko thnda karake pair ke talavon (sole of feet) men lagaaen। 5. tulasi (Basil) tulasi bhi taaiphaaid ke bukhaar ke lie utatam aushadhi hai। isake entibaikatiriyal (Antibacterial) aur entibaayotik (Antibiotic) gun baikatiriya ko khatam karate hai, jisase bukhaar jaladi bhi thik hota hai। kaise karen upayog pudine ki bis patatiyon men ek chhoti chamamach adarak (Ginger) ko kadadookas karake ek kap paani mem ubaal len। is paami ko gumaguna rahane tak intajaar karen। isake baad ise chhaanakar isamen shahad milaakar piem। is pey ko dim do se tin baar le sakate hain। 6. laung (Laung or clove) laung men taaiphaaid ko thik karane ke gun hote hain। laumg ke tel men entibaikatiriyal (Antibacterial) gun hote hain jo ki baikatiriya ko maar dete hain। kaise karen upayog aath kap paani men 5 se 7 laung daalakar ubaal len। jab paani aadha rah jaae ise chhaan len। is paani ko poora din piem। is upachaar ko ek haphate lagaataar karen। Disease: joon (Lice) Descriptiom: joon (Head Lice) til ke aakaar ki ek chhoti parajivi hai jo manushay ke sharir men paida ho jaati hain। saamaanayata: yah baalon men paaye jaate hain। ye baṛi teji se chal sakati hain। is kaaran baalon ke bich inahen khojana kathin ho jaata hai। ye sabhi umar tatha parajaatiyon ke logom ko snkaramit karati haim। Symptoms: - sir men khujali hona Reasons: juen teji se, ek vayakati se doosare vayakati tak phail sakati haim। yah behad teji se chalati hain। juon ke phailane ke kuchh kaaran niman hain: juen phailane ke kaaram (Cause of Head Lices in Hindi) - haita, sakaarapha, knghi, barasha, heyar kalip athava baireta, heyar bainda, helamet athava kapaṛon, ka adala-badalakar isatemaal karate hain। - ek hi bisatara, palng athava kaalin ka parayog karate/karati hain। - bahut nikat rahakar khelate hain। - aise alamaari athava laॉkar men rakhi gai, vasatuon ka parayog karate hain, jin men juen athava unake nde maujood hote hain। Treatments: kaise roke joon ko phailane se (Treatment of Head Lice in Hindi) - saamaanay shaimapoo se baal saaph karen। kndishanar ka parayog n karen। isake kaaran juon ki dava ka parabhaav samaapat ho sakata hai। - garam paani se baal dhokar unahen tauliye se sukha len। is tauliye ka dubaara parayog tab tak m karen, jab tak yah dho n liya jaae। - baalom par saphed siraka lagaaen - yah us ‘gonda’ ko dhila karame men sahaayak hota hai, jo ‘likhon’ ko baalon se chipakaae hue hai। - baalon ko mahin knghi se saaph karen, jisase ye nde nikal aaen। baalom ko idhara-udhar karake knghi karana upayogi ho sakata hai। - sabhi ndon ka hataaya jaama aavashayak hai। isamen 2 athava 3 ghmte ya adhik samay lag sakata hain, tatha yadi knghi kaam nahim karati hai to aapako haathon sm mde chumane paṛ sakate hain। - parivaar men jitane logon ko joonen hain sab ka upachaar ek saath ho। - kapade bisatar aadi dhoop men rakhen ya garam paani men dhoen। - roosi - roosi - baalon ka jhadna Home Remedies: joon ek chhota parajivi (parasite) hai jo baalon ki jadon aur baalom ke nichale hisase par chipake rahate hain, jahn yah sir ki tavacha se khoon ko pikar jinda rahate hain। bachachom men joon hone ki samasaya aam hai। yadi aap joon vaale kisi vayakati ke snparak men aate hain to yah aapako bhi ho sakate hain। saath hi inphekated vayakati ka saamaam jaise knghi aur kapade aadi isatemaal karane se bhi joon hone ki snbhaavana rahati hai। sir men joon hone ka sabase aam lakashan hai sir mem khujali hona aur sir ki tavacha par laal chakatate padnaa। yah bahut teji se barhate hain isalie inahen jaladi khatam karana bahut mushakil hota hai। kuchh ghareloo upachaar ke davaara joon se nijaat paai ja sakati hai। aaie aapako bataaen aise hi kuchh ghareloo upachaar ke baare men- 1. lahasun (Garlic)- lahasun ki tej mahak juon ka dam ghotati hai aur unahen maar deti hai। kaise karem upayog aath se das lahasun ki kaliyon ko pisakar isamen nimboo ka ras milaaen aur baalon ki jadon mem lagaaen। aadhe ghnte baad baalon ko garam paani se dho len। lahasun ki kaliyom ko pisakara, usamen khaane vaala tel milaaen। isake baad isamen shainpoo ya kndishanar men milaakar baalom men lagaaen। aadhe ghnte ke lie baalon ko yoon hi chhod den aur dho den। 2. bebi ऑyal (Baby oil)- bebi ऑyal men kapade dhone vaala ditarajent aur kuchh siraka milaakar baalon men lagaane se bhi joon ka ilaaj snbhav hai। bebi ऑyal bhi joon ka dam ghont deta hai jisase vah mar jaati hain। kaise karen upayog bebi ऑyal ko baalon men lagaakara, patale dnton vaali knghi se baal kaarhen। joon girani shuroo ho jaaengi। isake baad baalon ko ditarajent aur garam paani se dho len। sone jaane se pahale baalon men siraka lagaaen aur baalon ko shaavar kaip se dhak lem aur poori raat yoon hi chhod dem। subah saamaanay shainpoo se baal dho len। shaimpoo ke baad kmdishanar karen। 3. ऑliv ऑyal (Olive oil)- ऑliv ऑyal bhi joon maarane men bahut parabhaavi hai। kaise karen upayog baalon men kisi bhi parakaar ka ऑliv ऑyal sone se pahale lagaaen। shaavar kaip lagaakar raat bhar tel ko baalon men yoon hi chhod den। subah men baalon ko knghi karen, joon baahar nikal aaengi। isake baad baalon ko shaimpoo kar len। aadha kap ऑliv ऑyal men aadha kap kmdishanar milaakar isamen kuchh likavid saabun milaaen। ise baalon ki jadon men lagaakar ek ghmta chhod den aur baal dho len aur knghi karake joon baahar nikaal den। ise ek haphate baad dobaara doharaaen। 4. namak (Salt)- namak bhi joon mikaalane men behad asarakaari hai। kaise karen upayog ek chauthaai kap namak men itana hi siraka milaakar is ghol ko baalon men sapare karen। sapare kie hue gile baalon par shaavar kaip pahanen aur do ghnte yoon hi chhod den। isake baad baal dho len aur baalon par kndishanar karen। har tisare din is parakariya ko doharaaen। 5. petaroliyam jeli (Petrolium jelly)- petaroliyam jeli rengane vaale (roaming around) juon ko turnt maar deti hai। kaise karen upayog sone se pahale baalon ki jadon mem petaroliyam jeli lagaaen। isake baad kapade se baalon ko bndh kar so jaaen। subah bebi ऑyal se jeli hataaem aur knghi karake joon ko baahar nikaalen। 6. naariyal ka tel (Coconut oil) naariyal ka tel rengane vaale juon par asar dikhaata hai saath hi inaki snkhaya ko barhane se rokata hai। kaise karen upayog sabase pahale baalon ko seb ke sirake (Apple cider vinegar) se dhoen। baalon ko poori rah sukhaakar jadon men naariyal ka tel lagaaen। chhah se aath ghnton ke lie baalon ko yoon hi chhod den। isake baad baalon ko shainpoo karake knghi karem aur joon nikaalen। 7. saphed siraka (White vinegar) saphed sirake men maujood esitik esid joom ko maarata hai। yah joon ko maarane ka surakashit aur sasata tarika hai। kisi tel men saphed siraka milaakar baalon men lagaakar kuchh ghmte chhod den aur phir shainpoo karen। Disease: kabaj (Constipation) Description: kabaj ek behad aam bimaari ban chuki hai। mal tayaag ek paraakaृtik kariya hai। lekin jab mal tayaag karane men agar pareshaani aati hai to us samasaya ko kabaj (Kabj) kahate hain। aniyamit khaanapaan aur galat jivanashaili ke kaaran yah bimaari lagaataar barhati ja rahi hai। Symptoms: - ainthan ho, darad ho, pet phool jaae ya matali ho - aisa mahasoos ho ki aapaki ntadiyn poori tarah se khaali nahin hui ho - mal tayaag ke lie zor lagaana pade Reasons: - aise aahaar jinamen charabi aur shakakar jayaada hom aur reshe kam hon। - kaaphi maatara men taral padaarath m lenaa। - mishakariy rahanaa। - jab aap ko mal tayaag ki ichachha ho tab shauchaalay n jaanaa। Treatments: kaise door karen kabaz (Treatment of Constipation in Hindi) - din men kam se kam 8-10 gilaas paani pina chaahie। gunagune ya garam paami se aapaki nton ko aasaani se kaam karane men madad mil sakati hai। - barain siriyala, hol garen bareda, kachachi sabajiyn, taaje ya sukhaaye hue phala, sookha meva aur paॉpakaॉran jaisi adhik reshe vaali chijen khaaie। reshe sharir se mal ko nikalane mem madad karate hain। - chiza, chaॉkalet aur anakaden aadi kam khaana chaahie kayonki inase kabaj (Kabj) barh sakati hai। - mal ko maram karane ke lie aaloo bukhaare ya seb ka ras pijie। - apani nton ko thik se kaam karane men madad karane ke lie kasarat kijie। - kabaj men paidal chalane se laabh hota hai। - jab aap ko mal tayaag karane ki ichachha ho, shauchaalay jaaen। - enima ka upayog karane se pahale apane chikitasak ki salaah len। Home Remedies: - ek chutaki kaala namak gunagune paani men daalem aur use subah khaali pet pikar 15 minat tak chahalakadami karen, kabaz men avashay hi raahat milegi। - apame bhojam men mote anaaj (Bran) ka samaavesh karen। mausam ke anusaar upalabadh salaad ko shaamil karane se kabaj aur pet ki doosari tamaam samasayaaon se sathaai roop se chhutakaara paaya ja sakata hai। - alasi ke bij (Flaxseed) ka sevan bhi kabaz se aaraam dilaata hai। alasi ke bij ko subah kaॉranaphalekas (Cornflax) ke saath milaakar kha sakate hain ya phir mutathi bhar alasi ke bij ko garam paani ke saath subah kha sakate hain। - kishamish phaaibara(Fiber) se bharapoor hoti hai aur paraakaृtik julaab ki tarah kaam karati hai। १०-१२-kishamish ko raat men paani men bhigokar rakh den aur subah khaali pet khaaen। garabhaavasatha (Pregnamcy) men mahilaao ko akasar kabaz ki shikaayat rahati hai, garabhavati mahilaaon (Pregnant Females)ke lie yah bahut laabhakaari upaay hai। - amarood (Gauva) bhi kabaz men bahut raahat pahunchaata hai। isake goode aur bij men phaaibar ki uchit maatara hota hai। isake sevan se khaana jaladi pach jaata hai aur esiditi (Acidity) se bhi raahat milati hai, saath hi pet bhi saaph ho jaata hai। - ek gilaas gunagune paami men ninboo (Lime) aur namak (Salt) milaakar subah khaali pet pine se bhi kabaz men kaaphi aaraam milata hai। Disease: uchach rakatachaap (High Blood Pressure) Description: haai balad pareshar ya uchach rakatachaap ki samasaya aajakal behad aam hoti ja rahi hai। uchach rakatachaap ke dauraan marij ke sharir men rakat ka paravaah behad tej ho jaata hai। is sathiti men aapake haृday ko adhik kaam karana padta hai। aaiye jaanen isase judi anay baaten: Symptoms: - ulati hone ki shikaayat aur chidachidaapan - kam mehamat karane par sns phoolanaa, thakaavat rahana - chakakar aama - tngon men darad - tamaav homa - naak se khoom aana - nimd m aana - lagaataar siradarad honaa, sir chakaraana - sms lene men kathinaai - sir ke pichhe v garadan men darad - haृday ki dhaṛakan tej rahana - haृday kashetar men piṛa mahasoos karana Reasons: uchach rakatachaap ke hone men bahut saare phaikataras aham bhoomika nibhaate hain jinamen se sabase mahatavapooram hai aasim jivanashaili। shaaririk sharam ki kami ke kaaran bhi kai baar yah bimaari logon ko pareshaam karati hai। uchach rakatachaap ke kai anay kaaran niman hain: uchach rakatachaap ke kaaran (Reason for High Blood Pressure) - dhoomarapaan - motaapa - nishakariyata - namak ka jayaada sevan - sharaab pina - tanaav - barhati umar - aamuvnshikata - paarivaarik itihaas - puraani kidani ki bimaari - thaairoid disaऑradar Treatments: rakatachaap (Blood Pressure) barhane par kis tarah apana dhayaan rakhana isaki jaanakaari hona behad jaroori hai। saath hi samaya-samay par daॉkatari jnch is bimaari se bachaane men bahut kaaragar hoti hai। uchach rakatachaap se bachane ke kuchh paramukh upaay nimam hain: - paratidin ek ghmta halaka ya tej kisi parakaar ka vayaayaam jaroor karen। - khaane men haai phaaibar vaale chijen leni chaahie। - khud ko ekativ rakhane ka adhik se adhik parayaas karana chaahie। - samaya-samay par daॉkatar ki salaah leni chaahie। Home Remedies: uchach rakatachaap (High Blood Pressure) yoon to jivanashaili se snbndhit ek saamaanay bimaari hai lekin yahi kai anay badi bimaariyon ki shuroovaat ya vajah bhi hai। kai baar uchach rakatachaap se vayakati ki maृtayu tak snbhav hai। dil ki bimaariyn (Heart Disease), enajaaina (Engina) aur satarok (Stroke) aadi sabhi samasayaaen uchach rakatachaap ke kaaran hoti hain yahn tak ki kai baar shugar ke lie bhi uchach rakatachaap jimamedaar hota hai। haalnki yadi apane savaasathay ka dhayaan rakha jaae to kai ghareloo upaayon se bhi uchach rakatachaap ko thik kiya jaana snbhav hai। aaie jaanate hain kuchh aise hi ghareloo upachaaron ke baare men। uchach rakatachaap ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for High Blood Pressure) lahasun (Garlic) lahasun ko khaali pet subah kachacha hi khaaen। lahasum men rakat ko patala karane ke gun hote hain jo ki rakat ka thakaka jamane se bhi rokata hai। chikitasak se paraamarash lekar lahasun kar parayog shuroo kar sakate hain। shahajan ki phali (Drum Sticks) shahajan men parotina, vitaamin aur anay poshak tatav maujood hote hain jo ki shaaririk savaasathay ki daृshati se behad jaroori hain। shahajan ka upayog karane ka aasaan tarika hai ki isaki phaliyon ko daal ke saath banaakar khaaya jaae। isase bhi uchach rakatachaap naॉramal hota hai। nvala (Indian Gooseberry) mvala men vitaamin si ki uchach maatara hoti hai jo ki sharir se kolesataraॉl (cholesterol) ki maatara ko kam karati hai। isase dil savasath rahata hai aur uchach rakat chaap niyntarita। mooli (Radish) rasoighar men parayog hone vaali aam sabaji hai mooli, lekin isamen uchach rakatachaap ko niyntarit karane ke gun hote hain। mooli ko salaad ke roop mem kachacha ya dahi ke saath milaakar khaaya ja sakata hai। til (Sesame) til daayasatolik aur sisatolik (Diastolic and Systolic) , donom tarah ke rakatachaap ko niyntarit karata hai। til ke tel men sisamin (Sesamin) aur sisaminaॉl (Sesaminol) donon hote hain jo ki sharir ke tanaav ko kam karane men aham bhoomika mibhaate hain। til ka khaane men parayog karane se uchach rakatachaap ko niyntarit kiya ja sakata hai। til ke ladadoo ya til ka paaudar salaad ya daal sabaji mem upar se chhiṛakakar khaane se laabh hota hai। alasi ke bij (Flex Seed) alasi ke bij omegaa-3 phaiti esid men se ek hai jisase isamen alapha linolenik esid (Alf Linolenic Acid) naamak yaugik ki uchach maatara hoti hai। yah uchach rakatachaap ko niyntarit karane ke saath hi kelaॉsataraॉl ki maatara bhi ghataata hai jisase haृday bhi savasath banata hai। Disease: dnt ka darad (Toothache) Description: dnt hamaare sharir ka mahatavapooram hisasa hain। baat musakuraane ki ho ya kuchh khaane ki bina dnt sab bekaar hai। lekin kisi bhi kaaran yadi dnton men darad ho jaae to vayakati baichen ho jaata hai। dnton ka darad yoon to ek aam samasaya hai, lekim isaka darad asahaniy hota hai। Symptoms: - chabaane men darad hona - bukhaara, siradarad - sns lene men kathinaai Reasons: dmton men darad ke kai kaaran ho sakate hain। dmton ki thik se saphaai n karanaa, dmton men kaiviti hona ya atayadhik mitha khaanaa। isake saath hi chaay kaaphi jayaada pinaa। isake saath hi kuchh amay kaaran bhi hain jaise: dnton men darad ka kaaram (Causes of Tooth Pain) 1. masoodon men inphekashana- yadi kisi bhi kaaran se masoodon mem inphekashan hai to yah dnt darad ka kaaran ho sakata hai। isake kaaran tooth inemal (Tooth Enamel) ki samasaya bhi hoti hai। isase dnton men thnda garam laganaa, munh ka savaad bigadnaa, garadan ki galaind men soojan aanaa, masoodon men soojan aanaaaadi samasayaaen a sakati hain। 2. kaivitija- isake kaaran dnton ki upari parat nashat ho jaati hai। kaॉrabohaaidaret vaala khaana jisamen bareda, soda kek ya kaindi aadi dnton par chipak jaae aur achachhi tarah se saaph n ho to kaiviti (Cavity) ho sakati hai jisaka parinaam hota hai dntom men darada। 3. dnt men kidaa- isase dnt poori tarah khokhala ho jaata hai aur unamen khaana bhar jaata hai। jo ki darad ka kaaran banata hai। darad ke kaaran dnt kaam mahin karata aur um par ek parakaar ki gndagi jamame lagati hai। 4. toote dnta- kuchh khaate vakat ya kisi anay kaaran se yadi dnt toot gae hain to aise dnton men darad ki shikaayat akasar rahati hai। aise dnton ke inemal kamajor ho jaati hai jisase ye sensitiv ho jaate hain। 5. philinga- yadi dntom men philing (Tooth Filling) karaai gai ho to yah bhi kai baar yah dnt darad ka kaaran ho sakati hai। Treatments: ​dnt darad hone par thnde paani se kulala karama phaayademnd hota hai lekin agar isase pooran aaraam nahin mil paae to niman upaay karane chaahie: - koi penakilar lem। - aais paik ya taॉvel men aais lapetakar use gaalom par kuchh der ke lie rakhen। agar gaalon men soozan a jaae aur darad ho to pharozen piz ko aaisapaik ki jagah lagaaen। ye chehare ke aakaar ke anusaar badal sakate hain। - agar do dinon men darad nahin jaata to denatisat (Dentist) ke paas jaaen। ho sakata hain zayaada kaॅviti ya karaik ki vajah se darad ho। - dnt ka daॉkatar aapake munh ki jnch karega aur ekasa-re legaa। phir dnt ka daॉkatar dnt ko thik karega ya nikaal degaa। aapako darad nivaarak davaaen ya entibaayotik lene ke lie kaha ja sakata hai। daॉkatar ki bataai gai davaaen len। Home Remedies: dnton ka darad vaise to ek saamaanay samasaya hai, lekin isaka darad asahaniy hota hai। yadi aapako bhi kabhi dnt men darad ho to ghabaraaen nahin, kuchh ghareloo upaay apanaakar aap is takaliph se bach sakate haim। 1. launga- yadi dnt men darad ho to laung ka tel rooi men bhigokar dnt par lagaaie। koshish kijie ki tel masoodon par n lage kayonki isase halaki jalan mahasoos ho sakati hai। 2. elakohala- ji hn aapane thik parha elakohala। ek sip elakohal se kulala karane par bhi darad men aaraam milata hai। isase darad vaala hisasa sunan ho jaata hai। lekin sathaai yah ilaaj nahin hai। 3. vikasa- vikas ko apane chehare ke us hisase ki taraph lagaaie jis taraph dnt men darad ho। isake baad chehare ko dhnk len। isase darad men aaraam milata hai। 4. aaisa- baraph ke tukade se sikaai karane par bhi dnt darad men behad aaraam milata hai। 5. kaali miracha- kaali mirach ke paaudar ko masoodon par ragadne se bhi darad ka hisasa sunan ho jaata hai aur darad men aaraam milata hai। 6. kachachi payaaja- kachachi payaaj ko 3 minat tak darad vaale hisase par ragaden, isase bhi darad men bahut aaraam milata hai। 7. lahasuna- lahasun ki kali ko chabaakar usake ras ko laar ke saath milakaar kulala karen। kuchh hi sekend men darad men aaraam milegaa। 8. vanila araka- vanila arak ki kuchh boonde rooi men lekar darad vaale hisase par lagaaen। dnt darad men aaraam milegaa। 9. gehoon ke paudhe ka rasa- nkurit gehoon ke paudhe ka ras bhi kulale ke roop men parayog kar dnt darad se bacha ja sakata hai। yah masoodon ke visham padaarathon ko nikaalakar jivaanuon ki vaृdadhi ko rokata hai। 10. pairaॉkasaaida- dmton men darad hone par pairaॉkasaaid se kulala karem। lekin dhayaan rahe ise kabhi migalen nahin। isase bhi dnt darad mem aaraam milata hai। Disease: demgoo (Dengue) Description: dengoo, maada edij (Female Aedes) machachhar ke kaatane se hota hai। ye machachhar din men, khaasakar subah kaatate hain। marij men agar jatil tarah ke dengoo ka ek bhi lakashan dikhaai de to use jaladi - se - jaladi daॉkatar ke paas le jaaen। diechaeph ( DHF - Dengue Hemorrhagic Fever) aur diesaes (DSS - Dengue Shock Syndrome) bukhaar dengoo ke do parakaar hain jinamen paletaletas (Platelets) kaaphi kam ho jaate hain, jisake kaaram sharir ke jaroori ngon par bura asar paṛ sakata hai। Symptoms: - ulati v sharir par laala-laal daane nikal aate hain - kamajori ho jaati hai aur chakakar aate hain - dengoo bukhaar ke lakashan aam bukhaar se thoṛe alag hote hain - demgoo shaॉk simdarom (DSS) ke marijon men saadhaaran dengoo bukhaar aur dengoo haimarejik bukhaar ke lakashanen ke saatha-saath bechaini mahasoos ho - dengoo hemorejik bukhaar men uparokat lakashanon ke alaava paletaletas ki kami se sharir men kahin se bhi khoon bahana shuroo ho sakata hai, jaise naak se, dnton v masoodon se, khoon ki ulati v mal men khoon aana aadi - thakaavat v kamajori hai - naaṛi kabhi tej aur kabhi dhire chalanelagati hai aur rakat chaap (Blood Pressure) ekadam kam ho jaata hai - bukhaar bahut tej hota hai - siradarada, kamar v jodon men darad hota hai - halaki khnsi v gale men kharaash mahasoos hoti hai Reasoms: - khaali baratanon ko ulata karake rakhen। - pakashiyon ke khaame- pine ke baratanon ko har roj saaph karen। - agar ghar mem koolar hai to usaka paani do ya tin din baad avashay badalen। - ghar men sathit haudiyon, tainkaron men paani ko saaph rakhane ke lie usamen kalorin ki do chaar goliyn daal den। - ghar ke aasa- paas ya chhat par pade bekaar taayara, tayooba, toote hue matake, khaali dibabon aadi men barasaat ka paani ikathatha n home den। - paarak men jaate samay ya aisi jagah jaate samay jahn machachharom ke kaatane ka khatara ho, vahn poori baajoo ke kapade pahanane chaahie taaki machachhar na kaaten। - poora aaraam karane den। use har chhah ghnte men pairaasitaamol (Paracetamol) den aur baara- baar paani aur taral chijen ( miboo paani, chhaachha, naariyal paani aadi ) pilaaen। - bachachon ka khaas khayaal rakhen। - bukhaar kam hone ke baad bhi eka-do din men ek baar paletaletas kaaunt tesat jaroor karaaen। dengoo men marij ke rakatachaapa, khaasakar upar aur miche ke rakatachaap ke ntar par lagaataar nigaraani ( dim mem 3-4 baar ) rakhana jaroori hai। donon rakatachaap ke bich ka pharak 20 digari ya usase kam ho jaae to sathiti khataranaak ho sakati hai। rakatachaap girane se marij behosh ho sakata hai। - bachache naajuk hote hain aur umaka imayoon sisatam (Immune System of Kids) kamajor hota hai isalie bimaari unahen jaladi pakad leti hai। aise men unaki bimaari ko najarndaaj n karen। - bachache khule mem jayaada rahate hain isalie inaphekashan hone aur machachharon se kaate jaane ka khatara unamen jayaada hota hai। - bachachom ghar se baahar poore kapaṛe pahanaakar bhejen। - machachharon ke mausam men bachachon ko nikar v ti - sharat n pahanaaen। - raat men machachhar bhagaane ki karim lagaaem। - agar bachacha bahut jayaada ro raha ho, lagaataar soe ja raha ho, bechain ho, use tej bukhaar ho, sharir par raishej hon, ulati ho ya inamen se koi bhi lakasham ho to phauran daॉkatar ko dikhaaen। - aamataur par chhote bachachom ko bukhaar hone par unake haath - pnv to karaana chaahie kayonki bachachon men paletaletas jaladi girate hain aur unamen dihaaidareshan (paani ki kami) bhi jaladi hota hai। Home Remedies: dengoo edij machachhar (Adeej Mosquito) davaara phailane vaali bimaari hai jo ki haal ke samay men teji se barh rahi hai। dengoo ke baare men sabase khaas baat yah hai ki isake machachhar din ke samay kaatate hain tatha yah machachhar saaph paani (Cleam Water) mem panapate hain। dengoo ke dauraan rogi ke jodon men tej darad (Pain im Joints) hota hai tatha sir men bhi darad (Headache) kaaphi tej hota hai। badon ke mukaabale yah bachachon men hai jisase kai baar ndarooni rakatasataraav (Internal Bleedimg) hone ki snbhaavana bhi rahati hai। dengoo se bachaav ke lie kuchh ghareloo upaay bhi hain jinahen apanaakar dengoo se bachaav snbhav hai। aaie aapako bhi bataate hain ki kaun se ghareloo upaay aapako dengoo se bacha sakate hain- dengoo ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Dengue) dhaniya patati (Coriander Leaves) dengoo ke jisase ki sharir men ebajaॉrab karane ki kashamata barhati hai। isase sharir jayaada lauh tatav ebajaॉrab kar paata hai jo ki dengoo ke bukhaar ko thik karane ke lie jaroori hai। tulasi (Basil) tulasi ke pataton ko garam paani men ubaalakar chhaanakara, rogi ko pine ko den। tulasi ki yah chaay dengoo rogi ko behad aaraam pahunchaati hai। yah chaay dinabhar mem tin se chaar baar li ja sakati hai। papite ki patati (Papay Leaves) papite ki patatiyn, dengoo ke bukhaar ke lie sabase asarakaari dava kahi jaati hai। papite ki patatiyon men maujood papen enjaaim (papain enjymes) sharir ki paachan shakati ko thik karata hai, saath hi sharir men paraatin ko gholane ka kaam karata hai। dengoo ke upachaar ke lie papite ki patatiyon ka joos nikaal kar ek ek chamamach karake rogi ko den। is joos se paletaletas ki maatara teji se barhati hai। bakari ka doodh (Goat Milk) dengoo bukhaar ke lie ek aur buhat parabhaavashaali dava hai bakari ka doodha। bahut kam hochuki paletaletas ko bhi bakari ka doodh turnt barhaane ki kashamata rakhata hai। dengoo ke upachaar ke lie rogi ko bakari ka kachacha doodh thodaa-thoda karake pilaaen, isase paletaletas barhenge aur jodon ke darad men bhi aaraam milegaa। chiraayata (Chirayta) chiraayata men bukhaar ko thik karane ke gun hote hain। dengoo ke bukhaar ko bhi chiraayata ke isatemaal se thik kiya ja sakata hai। dhatoora (Dhatura) dhatoore ki patatiyon men dengoo ke bukhaar ko thik karane ke gun hote hain, lekin isaki khuraak 2 desigaraam se adhik nahin honi chaahie। methi ke patate (Fenugreek Leaves) methi ke patate bhi demgoo ke bukhaar ko thik kar sakate hain। methi ke pataton ko paani men ubaalakar harabal chaay ke roop men isaka payog kiya ja sakata hai। methi se sharir ke vishaakat padaarath baahar nikal jaate hain jisase dengoo ke vaayaras bhi khatam hote hain। anaar aur kaale ngoor (Pomegranate and Black Grapes) dengoo bukhaar men rakat ki kami ko poora karame aur paletaletas ke satar ko barhaane ke lie anaar aur kaale ngoor ka ras pina chaahie। sntare ka joos (Orange juice) vitaamin si se bharapoor sntaraa, paachan shakati ko barhaava deta hai saath hi sharir ka imayooniti bhi barhaata hai। aise men dengoo rogi ko jalad se jalad savasath hone ke lie sntare ke ras ka sevan karama chaahie। Disease: maleriya (Malaria) Description: maleriya bukhaar ke kaaran parativarash ki kai log apani jaan gnva dete haim। gnde paani men panapane vaale machachharon ke kaatane se phailani vaali is bimaari ke vishay men jaanakaari behad kaaragar hai। aaie jaanen maleriya ke baaren men: Symptoms: - ulati aana hona - enimiya hona - thnd lagakar bukhaar chadhaऩa - darad aur ainthan hona - pasina aana - maleriya bukhaar 10-15 din rahata hai - ye bukhaar chaṛhataa-utarata rahata hai Reasons: - aasapaan maujood paani ko samay par na badalana - rahane ke sathaan ke aasapaas gndagi hona - paani ka jamaav hona - machachharon ke ndom ka jama hona Treatments: maleriya ka paraathamik upachaar (Treatment of Malari in Hindi) - maleriya men kalorokavin jaisi enti-maleriyal dava (Chloroquine- Anti malarial medicine) di jaati hai। in davaaon ke saaid - iphekatas ho sakate hain, isalie inahen daॉkatar ki salaah ke bina n len। - marij ko poora aaraam karane den। use har chhah ghnte men pairaasitaamol (Paracetamol in Malaria) den aur baara- baar paani aur taral chijen ( niboo paani , chhaachh , naariyal paani aadi ) pilaaen। - maleriya bukhaar ke dauraan bachachon ka khaas khayaal rakhen। - bachache naajuk hote hain aur unaka imayoon sisatam kamajor hota hai isalie bimaari unahen jaladi pakad leti hai। aise men unaki bimaari ko najarndaaj m karen। - bachache khule men jayaada rahate hain isalie inaphekashan hone aur machachharon se kaate jaame ka khatara unamen jayaada hota hai। - bachachon ghar se baahar poore kapaṛe pahanaakar bhejen। - machachharon ke mausam men bachachon ko nikar v ti - sharat n pahanaaen। - raat men machachhar bhagaane ki karim lagaaen। - agar bachacha bahut jayaada ro raha ho , lagaataar soe ja raha ho , bechain ho , use tej bukhaar ho , sharir par chakatate (Rashes) hon, ulati ho ya inamem se koi bhi lakashan ho to phauran daॉkatar ko dikhaaen। - aamataur par chhote bachachom ko bukhaar hone par umake haath - pnv to thmde rahate hain lekin maatha aur pet garam rahate hain isalie unake pet ko chhookar aur rekatal temaparechar lekar unaka bukhaar chek kiya jaata hai। bagal se taapamaam lena sahi tarika nahin hai , khaasakar bachachon men। agar bagal se taapamaan lena hi hai to jo riding aae, usamem 1 digari joṛ den। use hi sahi riding maana jaaegaa। Home Remedies: maleriya bukhaar ke dauraan tej sir darad (Headache), jor ki thnd ke saath knp knpi (Shivring) honaa, mnsapeshiyon me bhaynkar darad hona (Muscle pain) aur behad kamajori jaise lakasham mahasoos hote hain। bukhaar utarate samay pasina hota hai। sharir ka taapamaan 104 digari se bhi jayaada ho sakata hai। ji ghabaraana aur pitat ki kadvi ulati hona aur paratidin nishachit samay par bukhaar charhana bhi maleriya ka paramukh lakasham hai। jaanie maleriya se raahat ke ghareloo upaay (Home Remedies for Malaria) 1. choona (Chuma)- tin garaam choona len, ise 60 mili paani men gholen। ek ninboo isamen nichoden। maleriya bukhaar ki snbhaavana home par yah misharan pien। yah nusakha paratidin lene se bukhaar se raahat milati hai। 2. chiraayataa- (Chirata)- chiraayata maleriya bukhaar ki sabase asaradaayak aushadhi maami gai hai। ek paav garam paani men 15 garaam chiraayata milaaen, kuchh laung aur daalachini bhi mila den। is paani ke isatemaal se bhi maleriya bukhaar utarame lagata hai। 3. nimboo (Lemon)- garam paani men ninboo ka ras milaakar pine se bukhaar ki tivarata ghatane lagati hai। 4. phitakari (Alum)- thodi si fitakari tave par bhoonakar chooran bama len। aadha chamamach paaudar bukhaar aane ke 3 ghnte pahale paani se pien। baad men har doosare ghnte par yah dava lete rahane se bukhaar khatam hota hai। 5. tulasi patata (Basil leaves)- jab bukhaar n ho, 10 garaam tulasi ke pataton ke ras mem aadha chamamach kaali mirach ka paaudar milaakar chaat len। isase maleriya bukhaar khatam ho jaata hai। 6. shahad (Honey)- ek gilaas paani len। isamen ek chamamach daalachini, ek chamamach shahad aur aadha chamamach kaali mirach ka paaudar milaakar garam karen। thmda hone par pien, yah ataynt laabhakaari nusakha hai। 7. dhatoora (Dhatoora)- dhatoora ki nai kopal 2 mag lekar gud ke saath achachhi tarah milaakar isaki goli bama len। imahen din men 2 baar lene se maleriya khatam ho jaata hai। 8. anan n khaaen (Avoid solid food)- maleriya hone par aman n khaaen। keval phal aur paani lete rahen। aisa karane se bukhaar se jaladi laabh milata hai। 9. adarak (Ginger)- ek gilaas paani mem 10 garaam adarak aur 10 garaam mumakaka daalakar itama ubaalen ki aadha rah jaaya। thnda hone par pien। 10. amarood (Guava)- ek bada amarud garam raakh men bhoon len। yah amarood khaana bhi, maleriya rogi ke lie laabhakaari hai। 11. thndi patati rakhen (Cold compress)- tej bukhaar ki haalat men maathe par thnde paani ki patati rakhane se taapamaan niche a jaata hai। thmde paani men gila kiya taavel saare sharir par lapetane se turnt laabh milata hai। 12. payaaj ka ras (Onion juice)- payaaj ka ras maleriya men laabhakaari hai। 5 mili ras men 4 kaali mirach ka paaudar milaakar din men 3 baar pime se laabh hota hai। 13. jaamun (Black berry)- jaamun ke ped ki chhaal sukhaakar pis len। 5 garaam choorana, gud ke saath din men 3 baar lene se maleriya se raahat milati hai। Disease: chhinkana (Sneezing) Description: chhink ko ek saamaanay kariya maana jaata hai। chhink paraayh tab aati hai jab hamaari naak ke ndar ki jhilali kisi baahari padaarath ke ghus jaane se pareshaani mahasoos karati hai। hamaari maak men mayookas jhilali hoti hai jisake utatak hai, ji hn tej dhoop se chhink ki nasem sakariy ho jaati haim jisase bina mausam ke dhoop men chalate vakat bhi chhink a jaati hai। - sekas bhi chhimkane ka kaaran ho sakata hai। sekas ke dauraan dhoola-mitati, sabaji ka tej chhaunk ya kisi chij ki tej gndha। isake alaava thnd ke mausam men, nami ya taapamaan men giraavata, kisi khaame se elaraji ya kisi dava se riekashana। vajah chaahen jo bhi ho, ek do ya tin chhink aana to saamaanay hai lekin yadi aapako ek saath kai chhinken aati hain, itani ki aap pareshaan ho jaate hain aur yah roj ki hi baat hai, to phir is baare men aapako saavadhaani ki khaas jaroorat hai। chhimkane ki samasaya se nijaat ke lie ham aapako kuchh ghareloo upaay bataane ja rahe hain jisase aapako chhinkane se raahat milegi। chhinkane ki samasaya se raahat takariban das minat paani ko kavar karake rakh den aur usake baad chhaanakar pien। is tarah ki chaay ko din men do baar pien। kaali mirach (Black Pepper) gunagune paami men aadha chamamach kaali sakata hai। tanaav se door rahen (Avoid Stress) yadi aap thaayaraॉid snbndhi kisi bhi pareshaani se garasit hain to tanaav bilakul n len। aisa koi bhi kaaray n karen, jo aapako iritet karata ho aur maatara bhi ghataaen, jisase haayapothaayaraॉidijam men aaraam ho। Disease: ऑsatiyoporosis (Osteoporosis) Description: ऑsatiyoporosis (Osteoporosis) ek aisi shmt parakaृti ki bimaari hai jisake ke minaral se milakar bami hoti hain, jo ki umar ke saath kam hone lagate haim। kai baar to hadadiyn itani kamajor ho jaati hain ki maamooli si chot se bhi toot jaati hain। ऑsatiyoporosis parotina, pauteshiyam bhi shaamil hote hain। aise men roj ek gilaas baadaam vaala doodh niyamit roop se pien। til ke bij (Sesame Seeds) apane bhojan men til ke bij shaamil karane se hadadiyon ki kamajori door hoti hai। til men bhi kailashiyam ki uchach maatara hoti hai, jo ki hadadiyon ke savaasathay ke lie sabase jaroori poshak tatav hai। isake saath hi til men maiganishiyama, phaॉsaphorasa, mainganija, tnba (Copper), jasata (Zinc) aur vitaamin di bhi hota hai। upachaar ke lie ek mutathi bhume hue til chaba kar doodh pien। isake alaava khaane banaane men bhi bhume hue tilon ko upar se daalakar khaaya ja sakata hai। anaanaas (Pine Apple) anaanaas men ऑsatiyoporosis ko rokane ke lie jaroori mainganij shaamil hai। mainganij ki kami se hadadiyon ka ghanatav kam aur hadadiyn patali ho sakati hain, aise men anaanaas khaame se mainganij ki kami poori hoti hai। upachaar ke lie har roj khaana khaane se pahale ek kap amaanaas ko khaaen। isake saath hi anaanaas ka joos bhi piya ja sakata hai। dhaniya ke bij (Coriander Seed) dhaniya ke patate aur bij donon men hi maiganishiyama, aayarama, kailashiyama, poteshiyam aur maingamij aadi poshak tatav hote hain। dhaniya ke bijon ko garam paani men ubaalakar kuchh der dhak kar rakhen usake baad gunaguna rahane par usame shahad milaakar pien। khaane ke chhaunk men bhi dhaniya ke bijon ka isatemaal kiya ja sakata hai। hare dhaniya ka isatemaal bhi khaana banaane aur chatami ke roop men karana chaahie। Disease: baresat kainsar (Breast Camcer) Description: maanav sharir ke avayav aur utak koshikaaon (sela) se bane hote hain। kainsar in koshikaaon ka ek rog hai। baresat kainsar duniya men teji se phailane vaali khataranaak bimaariyon men se ek hai। baresat kaimsar (Breast Cancer) ya satan kainsar ki adhikatar rogi mahilaaen hoti hain। purushon ko bhi satan kainsar ho sakata hai, lekin isaki snbhaavana bahut kam hoti hai। Symptoms: - satanom ke baare men jaan lene ka saral tarika hai T L C yaani T - TOUCH Your Breasts (apane satanom ko chhuem) kaya aapako kuchh asaamaanay lagata hai? kaya aap satan men, chhaati ke upari hisase men, ya bagalo men koi gnth (Lump) mahasoos karati hain? kaya aapako satanon ke upar koi parat mahasoos hoti hai jo hatati nahin? kaya satanon men saadhaaran sa darad hai। L - LOOK for chamges (kuchh badalaav to nahi lagataa) kaya satanon ke aakar ya banaavat ( shape or texture) men koi badalaav hai? kaya satanon ke aakar ya aakaृti (size or shape) men koi badalaav hai (koi ek satan doosare ke mukaabale chhota ya bada hain)? satanon ki tavacha ki banaavat men koi badalaav jaise fti fti si ya koi gadada sa pad jaanaa? rng men badalaav jaise ki nipapalas ke aasapaas surakh laal rmga.ho jaanaa? kaya nipapal ki disha sahi hai, kahin vah ndar ki taraph to nahi mud gaya hai? kisi bhi nipapal se taral padaaradh ka risanaa? nipapal ke aas paas kisi paradaarath ka risana ya papadi ka jamanaa? C - CHECK any unusual findings with your doctor (kuchh asaamaanay sa mahasoos ho to turnt hi daॉkatar se salaah len) kaya aapako kuchh asaamaanay ya alag sa mahasoos ho raha hai? agar aisa hai to turnt hi daॉkatar se salaah len। samay samay par apane satanon ki jnch savayn karate rahen aisa karane se aap uname saamaanay taur par aane vaale badalaavon aur asaamaanay badalaav ke baare men jaan jaayenge, akasar maasik dharam (Menses) ke samay satanon mem kuchh badalaav avashay aata hai। lakashanon ke ubharane ka intazaar n karen, niyamit roop se satamon ki jnch karavaaen। yah saravavidit hai ki rokathaam ilaaz se behatar hai Reasons: baresat kainsar ke kaaran (Reasom for Breast Cancer) kai log maanate hain ki baresat kainsar anuvnshik hota hai jo poori tarah sahi tathay mahin hai। satam ya baresat kainsar ke kuchh aham kaaran nimam hain: - aayu-satan kainsar hone ka jokhim aayu ke saath baṛhata hai। - yadi aapako pahale kainsar ya satan ka koi anay rog hua ho। - paarivaarik itihaas - keval 5–10% satan kainsar hi amuvnshik roop se paraapat jin ke kaaran hote hain। satan kaimsar ka khatara kin mahilaaon ko jayaada hota hai? - adhik umar ki mahilaaen। - jin mahilaaon ki mn, bahan ya beti ko satan kainsar hua ho - janam ke samay se hi karomozom (gunasootaro) men badalaav ho। - mahila jise bachache na hue hon, ya 30 saal ki umar ke baad bachache hue hon। - jise 12 saal ki umar se pahale hi piriyadas shuru ho gae hon। - jis mahila ko 50 saal ki umar ke baad menopaॉj (rajonivaृtati) hui ho। - jis mahila ki satan ke utak kaaphi ghane hon। aapaki memogaraaphi karake daॉkatar ye jaanakaari de sakate hai। - jo mahila garabh nirodhak goliyon ka lnbe arase se isatemaal kar rahi ho। - jo mahila din men 2 se 5 baar sharaab ka sevam karati ho। - jis mahila ko menopaॉj ke baad jayaada motaapa a gaya ho। - jis mahila ne haaramon ripalesament therepi isatemaal ki ho। - jo mahilaaen apane bachachon ko satanapaan nahin karavaatin। haaramom snbndhi kaarak esatarojan aur parojesatarojan maamak haaramon se lnbe samay tak samaparak mem aane se aapaka satan kainsar ka jokhim barh sakata hai। jivanashaili snbndhi kaarak lamabe samay tak paratidin do peg se jayaada sharaab pina tatha dhoomarapaan se aapaka satan kaimsar ka jokhim barh sakata hai| vajan jayaada homa bhi satam kainsar ka kaaran ban sakata hai। Treatments: - agar aapako thoda sa bhi snshay ho to turnt daॉkatar ki salaah lijiye। - chhote satan Home Remedies: satan kainsar (Breast cancer), sabase aam kainsar men se ek hai। satan kainsar ek knpalekas bimaari (Complex disease) hai jisake home ke lie kai phaikatara, jaise aanuvnshik (Heredity), khaana-paan aur jivan shaili jimamedaar hote hain। chikitasa visheshajaञom ki maanen to aane vaale samay men satan kainsar se pidit rogiyon ki snkhaya aur bhi teji se barhagi। haalnki jivan shaili men badalaav karake satam kainsar se kaaphi had tak bacha ja sakata hai। jaanie satan kainsar se bachaav ke ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies for Breast Cancer): 1. garin ti (Green tea)- ek gilaas paani men harabal garin ti ko aadha hone tak ubaalen aur phir use pien। yah phaayademnd hoti hai aur isase satan kainsar ka khatara kaaphi kam ho jaata hai। 2. ngoor aur anaar ka joos (Grapes and pomegranate juice)- rojaana ngoor ya anaar ka joos pine se satan kainsar se bacha ja sakata hai। in donon phalon ke joos men kainsar ke selas ko maarane ki kashamata hoti hai, jisase satan kainsar ka khatara kam ho jaata hai। 3. lahasun (Garlic)- lahasun men phalevomas (flavons) aur phalevonolas (flavonols) jaise enti baikatiriyal tatav hote hain। roj lahasun ka sevan karane se satan kainsar ki snbhaavama ko roka ja sakata hai। 4. haladi (Turmeric)- haladi men karakayoomin (curcumin) maam ka tatav hota hai jo ki vibhinam tarah ke kainsar ko thik karane men sakasham hai। haladi ke sevan se kainsar sel barhane ki snbhaavana kam hoti hai tatha kainsar thik hota hai। 5. tamaatar (Tomato)- tamaatar khaane se bhi mahilaaen satan kaimsar se bachi rah sakati hain। tamaatar men laayakopin (lycopene) hota hai jo ki ek shakatishaali entiऑkasident hai aur kainsar ko barhane se rokata hai। 6. paalak (Spinach)- paalak men entiऑkasidemt layootin (lutin) hota hai jo kainsar se bachaane men sahaayak hai। haphate men do se tin baar paalak khaama chaahie jisase satan kainsar se bacha ja sakata hai। 7. barokali (Broccoli)- barokali men kainsar se ladne vaale tatava, indola-3-kaarabinol (indole-3-carbinol) hota hai jo ki satan kainsar ke selas ki garoth ko kam kar dete haim। barokali ke niyamit sevan se kainsar se bacha ja sakata hai। barokali ke saath patata gobhi aur gobhi ko milaakar khaana chaahie। 8. akharot (Wallnut)- akharot men bahut se poshak tatav hote haim jo satan kainsar ki garoth ko kam kar dete hain isalie akharot ka rojaana sevan karana chaahie। 9. balooberi (Blueberries)- balooberi vitaamin aur minaral se bharapoor hoti hain। inamen entiऑkasident elejik bhi hote hain jo satan kainsar se bachaav karate hain। baloobairi ke saath sataraॉberi aur balaikaberi bhi behad phaayademnd hoti hai। Disease: siradarad (Headache) Description: siradarad ek aam samasaya hai। sir ke kisi bhi hisase mem darad ho sakata hai aur yah darad keval lakashan hota hai jo ki sir ki kisi bimaari ko darashaata hai। kai baar bahut jayaada tanaav leme, thakaavat hone, bhookhe rahane, garami tej hone ya kisi aam shaaririk samasaya jaise ki bukhaar ya jukaam ke kaaran bhi sir darad ho sakata hai। Symptoms: - uchach rakat chaap homa - kabaj ya dasat hona - jayaada sharaab pina - tanaavagarasat hona - pet thik n hona Reasons: sir darad ke kaarana- (Cause of Headache) sir ka darada, dimaag men rakat koshikaaon (blood vessels) aur shiraaon (nerves) ke aapas men takaraane se hota hai। darad ke samay rakat koshika ki ek nishachit sira aur sir ki mnsapeshiyn sakariy hoti hain aur dimaag ko darad ka siganal bhejati haim। jisase sir darad mahasoos hota hai। sir darad ke anay kaaran (Other Reasons of headache) 1. jab vayakati kisi chij ko lekar khud par dabaav mahasoos karata hai ya kisi sathiti ya parisathiti ko lekar asamnjas men hota hai। aise men usaka man ashnt ho jaata hai aur dimaag par jayaada gahara parabhaav padta hai jisake kaaram tanaav hota hai aur sir darad hone lagata hai। 2. dimaag ki rakat vaahiniyom mem badalaav hone se hone vaale darad ko maaigaren ka darad kaha jaata hai। is tarah ke sir darad men sir ke kisi ek hisase men chubhan bhara darad hota hai aur darad ke saath ji michalaane, gais aur ulati jaisi samasayaaen bhi hoti haim। itana hi nahim vayakati photophobiya (roshani se pareshaani) aur phomophobiya (shor se pareshaani) se bhi pareshaani mahasoos karata hai। parayaapat nind n leme, bhookhe rahane ya kam paani pine se maaigaren ho sakata hai। 3. kuchh mahilaaen haaramom men badalaav ke dauraan gmbhir sir darad mahasoos karati hain। yah sathiti monopoja, maasik sataraava, ovelayoosham aadi ke dauraan bhi ho sakati hai। maasik sataraav men utaara charhaav se bhi is tarah ka sir darad bana rah sakata hai। 4. kuchh khaas tarah ki davaaiyon ka jayaada din tak lene ke kaaran ribaaund siradarad ki samasaya ho ho sakati hai। kai bimaariyn aisi hoti hain jinamen davaaiyn lnbe samay tak chalati hain, aise men yah masatishak ko parabhaavit kar sakati hain। is tarah ka sir darad davaaen bnd hone ke saath khud hi bnd ho jaata hai। 5. dmt darad se bhi sir ki nasen parabhaavit hoti haim। dnt aur sir ki masen jabade par jaakar milati hain jisase dnt aur sir ek doosaren ko kamekat karate hain। jisase dnt men kisi bhi tarah ki takaliph hone se sir men darad hone lagata hai। 6. chaay aur kaॉphi ke aadi logon ko yadi samay par chaay n mile to bhi unahen sir darad ki shikaayat ho sakati hai। 7. kuchh logon ko subah uthate hi siradarad ki shikaayat hoti hai jabaki kuchh der baad yah apane aap thik ho jaata hai। kai baar raat men achachhi nimd n lene ya bhookhe pet sone ke kaaran subah subah sir darad ho sakata hai। 8. nkhon mem kisi tarah ki samasaya hone, nkh kamajor hone, chashama m pahamane ya kmtekat lains men gadbadi home se sir darad ho sakata hai। aisi koi bhi samasaya jisase nkhon par tanaav padta ho, sir darad hone ki vajah ho sakata hai। aise men yadi koi vayakati sir darad se pareshaan hai to use apani nkhon ko bhi jaroor chaik karaana chaahie। 9. kuchh logon ko aaisakarim ya bahut thndi chijon ko khaane se bhi sir darad ki shikaayat ho sakati hai। aaisakarim ya bahut thndi chijen khaane ke baad maathe ke bich men bhaaripan mahasoos hota hai jisase sir darad shuroo ho jaata hai। is tarah ka darad aaisakarim khaane ke turnt baar shuroo ho jaata hai। Treatments: sir darad se raahat ke lie tipasa- (Tips to Prevent Headache) Home Remedies: aajakal ki tej bhaagati jindagi aur vayasat jivanashaili men tanaav aur saradarad ek aam bimaari ho gai hai। saradarad ke kai kaaran hote hain। sir men rakat pahunchaane vaali naaṛiyon men snkuchana, sanaayu tntar ki asamaamay gatividhi, jayaada dhoomarapaan karanaa, jayaada alakohal lenaa, sharir men paani ki kami, jayaada der tak bevajah sonaa, darad nivaarak davaaon ka jayaada sevan karanaa, saradi-jukaama, bukhaar samet aise kai vajah hain, jisase saradarad hoti hai। yahn yah jaanana jaruri hai ki saamaanay saradarad aur maaigaren ke saradarad mem ntar hai। maaigaren men saradarad kaaphi pareshaani vaala hota hai aur yah ek gnbhir bimaari bhi hai। saradarad ya kisi bhi tarah ke saradarad mem jaladi elopaithik darad nivaarak dava khaama sehat ke lie nukasaanadeh hota hai, kayonki jayaada pen kilar khaane se kidani aur livar daimej hote hain। elopaithik davaaon se behatar hai ki ham aise kuchh ghareloo upachaar ko aajamaaem, jisase saradarad men n siraph aaraam milata hai balaki yah jaṛ se khatam bhi hota hai, bina koi saaid iphekata। saradarad ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Headache) sarason tel (Mustard Oil) saradarad men sarason tel kaaphi asaradaar hota hai। maathe ke jis hisase men darad ho raha ho us taraph vaale naak men sarason ke tel ki kuchh boonden daal dijie aur usake baad jor se snson ko upar ki taraph khinchie। isase saradarad se kaaphi raahat milegi। dhayaan rahe saradarad hone par bisatar par letakar darad vaale hisase ko bed ke niche lataka kar maak men tel lena chaahie। daalachini (Cinamon) daalachini ko paani ke saath mahin pisakar maathe par patala lep lagaane se saradarad men kaaphi raahat milati hai। lep sookh jaane par use hata lijie। tina-chaar baar lep lagaane par saradarad hona bnd ho jaata hai। pushakar mool (Pushkar Mool) pushakar mool ek kudarati jaṛi booti hai। ise chndan ki tarah ghisakar lep bana len aur sir par lagaaen। isake lep ko maathe par lagaane se saradarad men kaaphi raahat milata hai। mulethi (Mulethi) mulethi saradarad men kaaphi kaam karata hai। mulethi ko pisakar chooran bana lijie। is chooran ko naak ke paas le jaakar soonghen। isase saradarad chhoo-mntar ho jaaegi। saunpha-pipala-mulethi (Saunf, Peepal and Mulethi) pipal ke patate, sontha, mulaithi aur saunph sabako pisakar chooran bana lijie। usake baad is chooran men ek chamamuch paani milaakar gaadha lep bana bana lijie। is lep ko maathe par lagaaie। saradarad khatam ho jaaegaa। masaaledaar chaay (Spicy Tea) masaaledaar chaay saradarad ke lie ek raamabaan ki tarah kaam karata hai। ise ghar mem bhi aasaani se banaaya ja sakata hai। yah ek uta‍tejak pey padaarath hai jo dimaag ko sachet karata hai। chaay men thoṛi adarakha, laumg aur ilaaichi mila kar ubaal den। ho gaya garamaagaram masaaledaar chaay taiyaara। masaaledaar chaay ko garamaagaram hi pima chaahie। isase aapaka saradarad to gaayab hoga hi saath men aap tarotaaza bhi mahasoos karenge। tel maalish (Oil massage) saradarad mem tel ki maalish bahut asaradaar hoti hai। maalish se sir ki rakat dhamaniyon men rakat paravaah sahi se home lagata hai aur saradarad turnt chhoo-mntar ho jaati hai। dhayaan rahe sir ki maalish harabal tel se hi karem aur saradarad hone par tel ko halaka garam kar lena chaahie taaki yah jaladi asar kare। ninboo paani (Lemon Water) kaaphi maatara men sharaab pine se akasar logom ko haingaovar ho jaata hai। haimgaovar men kaaphi tej saradarad hota hai। aisi sathiti men ninboo paani kaaphi kaam karata hai। sharaab jayaada pine se sharir men paami ki kami ho jaati hai aur ninboo paani pine se sharir mem paani ki kami bhi door hoti hai aur saradarad bhi thik hota hai। Disease: baronkaaitis (Bronchitis) Description: jab shavaasanali tatha isaki shaakhaaon men snkaraman ya elaraji ke kaaran soojan aane ke kaaran shavaas snbndhi samasaya hoti hai to us sathiti ko baronkaaitis (Bromchitis) kahate haim। yah saradiyon ki ek aam samasaya hai। Symptoms: - khnsi ke saath bahut gaaṛha v hare rng ka balagam aana - naak bahana ya bmd hona - badan darad hona - baara-baar chhaati men jalan - bukhaar ya thnd lagama - lagaataar kaaphi der hona - sns phoolama - sns lete samay chhaati men gharagharaahat ki aavaaj hona Reasons: - sine men sathit shavns nali aur usaki shaakhaaon men baara-baar hone vaala inphekashana। - mayoomoniya bhi baronkaaitis ka mukhay kaaran hoti hai। - ti.bi. ka inphekashan bhi isaka ek paramukh kaaran hota hai। agar shuruaat men hi ti.bi. inphekasham ka samuchit ilaaj ho jaae to baromkaaitis se bacha ja sakata hai। - kuchh logon men yah rog janamajaat hota hai। - isake alaava aintitaripasin naamak enjaaim ki kami, rayoometaaid ऑratharaaitis aur anay aatoimayoon bimaariyn bhi baronkaaitis ka kaaran banati hain। - baikatiriya ya vishaanu ka snkaraman bhi baronkaaitis ka kaaran ho sakata hain। - dhoomarapaan aur vaayu paradooshan ke kaaran bhi yah bimaari ho sakati hai। - vaayu men kisi chij se elaraji jaise paraag kan itayaadi bhi baronkaaitis ka kaaram ho sakate hain। Treatments: baronkaaitis se bachaav ke lie sharir ko thndi se bachaana chaahie। saath hi niman baaton ka bhi khayaal rakhana chaahie: - dhoomarapaan chhoṛ dem। - vaayu paradooshana, v dhool se bachen। - saradi aur phaloo se karen bachaava। - balagam patala rakhane ke lie khoob paani pien। - sote samay sir bisatar se uncha rakhane ke lie takie ka parayog karem। - yadi bukhaar baṛh jaae aur thnd lagane lage to turnt kisi chikitasak se snparak karem। Home Remedies: baronkaaitis naak aur phephaṛe ke bich sns lene vaali nali men soojan ke vajah se hoti hai। yah paraay vaairal inphekashan se hota hai। gale men khichakhicha, knto jaisi chubhan aur darad homa isake lakashan hain। mausam men badalaav aur elaraji se bhi baronkaaitis ki shikaayat hoti hai। isamen kabhi-kabhi bukhaar ki bhi shikaayat hoti hai। baronkaaitis men kharaash ya darad hone se khaana khaane, paani pine ya thook nigalane tak men takaliph hoti hai। isase nijaat paane ke lie daॉkatar ki madad lene se behatar hai ki kuchh ghareloo ilaaj kie jaane chaahie jo kaaphi asaradaar bhi hota hai। baronkaaitis men kharaash ke ghareloo ilaaja(Home remedies for Bronchitis) shahad (Honey) shahad men emti vaayaral aur enti baikatiriyal gun hota hai। gale men kharaash hone par shahad ya shahad vaali chaay pine se soojan kam hoti hai aur gale ko kaaphi aaraam milati hai। gale men kharaash men yah kaaphi phaayademnd hota hai। adarak (Ginger) saradi, kaph aur gale ki kharaash men adarak gale ko kaaphi aaraam pahunchaata hai। adarak men enti imphalaametari gun hota hai। adarak ka rasa, adarak ki chaay pine ya adarak choosane se gale ki soojana, kharaash men kaaphi aaraam milata hai। harabal chaay (Herbal Tea) kaali miracha, tulasi v laung se bani chaay pine se gale men kharaash se nijaat milati hai। in kudarati jaṛi-bootiyon se bani garam chaay ki chusakiyon se gale ko kaaphi raahat milati hai। vaise harabal chaay kai bimaariyon mem bhi kaam aata hai। haladi (Turmeric) thoṛi si haladi daalakar doodh men ubaal len। doodh tab tak ubaalen jab tak haladi pak na jaaen. phir ise kap men lekar chaay ki chusakiyn lete hue pien। isase gale ke darad men aur kharaash men kaaphi raahat milegi। garaara (Gargil) gale men kharaash ki shikaayat hone par garam paani men namak daalakar garaare karen। namak mila garam paani aapake gale mem inphekashan ki vajah se aai soojan ko kam karata hai aur aaraam pahunchaata hai। behatar hoga ki jaladi raahat ke lie aap har tin ghnte men garaare karen। taral padaarath (Liquid) aap thoṛi-thoṛi der men kuchh garam taral padaarath lete rahen। kuchh bhi nahin to aap thoṛi-thoṛi der men garam paani pite rahen। isase aapake gale ki sikaai hogi aur aapako aaraam milegaa। lahasun (Garlic) lahasun men emti-baayotik aur enti vaayaral gum hote hain। gale ki soojan aur kharaash men yah kaaphi asaradaar hota hai। lahasun ke do-tin tukaṛe ko paani ke saath chaba kar subah khaaen ya phir doodh men ubaal kar bhi pi sakate haim। yookilipatas tel (Eucalyptus Oil) gale ki kharaash men bhaap lena kaaphi phaayademnd hota hai। garam paani men agar yookilipatas ke tel ko mila kar bhaap len to yah kaaphi asaradaar hota hai। gale ki soojan aur kharaash ko kam karata hai। Disease: ibola vishaanu rog (EVD) (Ebola) Description: ibola vaayaras rog ya ibola hemoraahaijik bukhaar ibola vishaanu ke kaaran hota hai। ibola vishaanu rog (EVD) ya ibola hemoraahaijik bukhaar (EHF) men sharir men nason se khoon baahar aana shuroo ho jaata hai, jisase sharir ke ndar rakatasaraav shuroo ho jaata hai aur isase 90% rogiyon ki maृtayu ho jaati hai। Symptoms: - aarnbhik lakashan men javara, phumasi, sar darada, michali, ulati aur pet mem darada, poore sharir men gathiya ka darada, gale men darada, dasat sakata hai - is rog ka inkayoobeshan piriyad (Incubation Period) ek haphate ka hota hai। usake baad rogi mem aarnbhik lakashan najar aate hain - jananng men soojan hoti hai - tavacha mem darad ka anubhav hota hai - netarashaleshamalaashoth (knjengavaaitisa) hai - poore sharir par phunshiyon najar aane lagati hain - munh ka taalu laal ho jaata hai - munha, kaana, maak se rakatasaraav hota hai - rog ke vikasit avasatha men yah lakashan bhi najar aate hai Reasons: ibola se bachaav ka sabase behatar aur ekamaatar upaay hai isase parabhaavit rogi ke samaparak men aane se bachamaa। kisi rogi ke snparak men aame se yah rog aur teji se phailata hai। Treatments: ​ibola ka abhi tak koi thos ilaaj nahin mila hai। bachaav hi is bimaari ka sabase behatarin upaay maana jaata hai। abhi tak ibola se piditon ke kes men nimam kadam uthaae jaate hain: - is bimaari ke lie koi vishishat upachaar nahin hai; snkaramit logon ki sahaayata ki koshishom men unahen oral rihaaidareshan therepi (pine ke lie thoṛaa-sa mitha aur namakin paani demaa) ya intaraavemas phaludas dena shaamil hai। - akasar is vaayaras ke snkaramit hone vaale 50% se 90% tak log maut ke shikaar ho jaate hain। - isake lie tika vikasit karane ke parayaas jaari hain; haalnki abhi tak aisa koi tika maujood nahin hai। Disease: loo lagana (Heat Stroke) Description: garami men sabase badi samasaya hoti hai loo laganaa। ngareji bhaasha mem ise hit satarok (Heat Stroke) aur sanasatarok (Sun Stroke) bhi kahate hain। garami men uchach taapamaan men jayaada der tak rahane se ya garam hava ke jhonkon se snparak men aane par loo (Loo) lagane ka siraph ndarooni vasatar rakhen। sharir par halaka sa garam paani chhidken। - gili chaadar men lapetakar taapamaan kam karane ka parayaas karen। - haath pair ki maalish karen jisase rakat sncharam parabhaavit hota hai। - snbhav ho to baraph ke tukade kapade men lapetakar garadana, bagalom aur jnghon par rakhe। isase garami jaladi nikalati hai। - dhoop men ghar se baahar mikalen to chhatari ka isatemaal karen। nnge badan aur nnge pair dhoop men na khaṛe hon। - ninboo paani, aam panaa, chhaachha, lasasi, naariyal paani, bel ya ninboo ka sharabata, khas ka sharabat jaise taral padaarath pite sabajiyon ka sevan adhik karen। - khiraa, kakaṛi, lauki, tauri jaroor khaaen। - thmde vaataanukoolit kamare men rahen। - imali ke goode ko haath pairon par malen। - sharir ka taapamaan tej hone par (Unripe mango juice) kachache aam ka joos raamabaan hai loo se bachaav men। kachache aam ko ubaal kar ya paka kar usaka gooda mikaal liya jaata hai aur phir paani ke saath guṛa, saumpha, pudina aur rog hai, jisamen vayakati achaanak jamin par gir kar paraayh aradadh moorachhitaavasatha men rahata hai। rogi ko isaka pooravaabhaas bhi nahin hotaa, ki use miragi (Epilepsy) ka daura padne vaala hai। Symptoms: - inahen tin avasathaaon men bnta ja sakata hai। paratham avasathaa-saara sharir tan jaata hai। yah avasatha 30 seknd se adhik nahim hoti, marij apani jibh ko dnton se chaba sakata hai। kai marijon ko kapadon men peshaab ya paakhaana bhi ho jaata hai। davitiy avasathaa- yah adhik ugar hoti hai, do se pmch minaton tak bani rahane vaali is avasatha ke dauraan marij ko tel jhatake aate hain। usake munh se jhaag mikalakar baahar bahane lagata hai, honth aur chehara nile pade jaate hain। taृtiy avasathaa-jhatake aana bnd ho jaata hai। marij ya to hosh men a jaata hai ya vah phir aisi avasatha men rahata hai। Reasons: miragi ke daure mukhayata: dimaagi kamajori ke kaaran aate hain। yah kamajori anuvnshik ya kisi amay kaaran se bhi ho sakati hai। miragi ke daure (Mirgi ke Daure) padne ke kuchh aham kaaran niman hain: miragi ke dauron ka kaaran (Reason for Epilepsy in Hindi) - yah rog saamaanayata: masatishak ki kamajori ke kaaran hota hai। - masatishak men rakatasaraav hona ya khoon ka thakaka jam jaane (sataroka) ke kaaran bhi miragi ke daure aate hain। - sir men chot lagane ya masatishak snkaramam ke kaaran - garabhaavasatha ki jatilataaom ki vajah se maata ko bhi daindaraph shuroo ho jaata hai। 4. ऑyal galaimd ka bnd honaa- kai baar kisi bimaari ya haaramomal asntulam ke kaaran ऑyal galaind bnd ho jaate hain jisase roosi hone lagati hai। 5. snkaramana- baalon ki sataailing ke lie kemikal ka parayoga, heyar kalar ka isatemaala, baalon ko nechural roop se n sookhame demaa, gile baalom ko hi bndh lena aadi kuchh aise kaaran hain jisase daimdaraph (Rusi) hone lagata hai। isase baalon men khujali shuroo hoti hai aur dhire dhire samasaya barhati jaati hai। 6. heyar kalara- heyar kalar men amoniya hota hai jo ki sakailap par roosi ko janam deta hai। heyar kalar ka isatemaal ekasaparat se raay lekar hi karana chaahie aur achachhe kisam ke heyar kalar ka isatemaal karama chaahie। 7. pasina aur dhoola- garamiyon ke dinon men sir ki tavacha par jama pasina jab dhool ke snparak men aata hai to sakailap par gndagi jama homa shuroo ho jaati hai। jo ki dhire dhire daimdaraph ka kaaran ban jaati hai। 8. elaraji- kai baar ham jo tela, shainpoo, heyar sataailing paraॉdakat ya heyar kalar isatemaal kar rahe hote haim vah hamen soot nahin karataa, natija elaraji ho jaati hai jo daindaraph hone ka bada kaaran hai। Disease: haarat ataik (Heart Attack) Description: haarat ataik ya haृday aaghaat haal ke saalon men saravaadhik hone vaali laaiphasataail bimaari hai। haृday men balaॉkej ke kaaran hone vaali is bimaari se dumiyaabhar men kai log pidit hain aur kai jaan gnva chuke hain। haarat ataik (Heart Attack) ke pachaas paratishat marijon ki asapataal pahunchane se pahale hi maृtayu ho jaati hai। har saal bhaarat men 30 laakh logon ki lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Pimples) baraph (Ice) baraph munhaason ki soojam aur laalima ko jalad se jalad thik karane ka gun rakhati hai। baraph parabhaavit kashetar men rakat milaakar bhi chehare par lagaaya ja sakata hai। Disease: gnjaapan (Baldness) Description: purushon men gnjaapan (Baldness) ek aam samasaya hai। daraasal gmjaapan ek parisathiti hai jisamen purushon ke jisase gnjaapan ko kaaphi had tak kam kiya ja sakata hai। 1. arndi ka tel (Castor Oil) arndi ka tel gnjaapan ko door karane ka sabase kaaragar dava hai। yah ek aadararak yaani maॉsacharaaijing ejent ki daal bhi besat hai। arahar ki daal ko pis kar pesat bama len। is pesat ko sir ke parabhaavit kashetar men lagaaen, jalad hi asar dikhane lagegaa। 3. ailovera jel (Aloe Ver Gel) ailo vera ek harabal aur baikatiriya ko bhi maaregaa। 10. dahi (Curd) baalon ke lie dahi kndishanar ka kaam karata hai। yah baalon ke gnjepan ko door karane men kaaphi kaam karata hai। baalon ko jhaṛane-girane se bhi rokata hai। baalon men dahi ka maasak lagaaem kaaphi behatar natije aaemge। Disease: dihaaidareshan (Dehydration) Descriptiom: dihaaidaresham yaani mirajalikarana। manushay sharir men paani ke kam ho jaane ki avasatha ko dihaaidareshan (Dehydration) kahate hain। vaijaञaanik bhaasha men dihaaidareshan ko haaipohaaidaraisham (Hypohydration) kahate hain। sharir men paani ki kami (Pani ki Kami) ke kaaran sharir se khanij padaarath jaise ki namak aur shakakar kam ho jaate hain। dihaaidareshan ke dauraana, sharir ki koshikaaon se paani sookhata rahata hai jisake kaaran sharir ke kaaray karane ka sntulan asaamaanay ho jaata hai। Symptoms: - ghabaraahat ya knpaknpi - kabaj - chakakar aana - munh ka baar baar sookh jaana - sookhi tavacha - payaas ma bujhana - sir men darad - susati - mnsapeshiyon mem ainthan - kamazori Reasons: - sharir men paani ki gnbhir samasaya kai baar jaanaleva bhi ho sakati hai। - sharir se pnch paratishat darav khatam hone par kamazori, payaasa, ubakaai, chiṛachiṛaapan hota hai। - sharir se das paratishat darav khatam hone par sir darada, chakakar aur mgon men sanasanaahat paida ho sakati hai। sharir ki tavacha nili paṛane lagati hai aur sharir kamazor ho jaata hai। - sharir se pndarah paratishat darav khatam hone par dekhane aur suname ki shakati par asar paṛata hai। jibh men soojan ho jaati hai aur khaana nigalane men dikakat hoti hai। - sharir se pndarah paratishat se jayaada darav khatam hone par insaan ki maृtayu bhi ho sakati hai। - dasat ke kaaram sharir men hue dihaaidareshan se manushay ki maृtayu ke aasaar jayaada hote haim। gnbhir dihaaidareshan (Pani ki Kami) ki vajah se manushay ka baren daimej yaani usake masatishak ko haani bhi pahumch sakati hai। saath hi haaipovolemik shaॉk ka khatara bhi rahata hai jisamen sharir ke kai ngon ko haami pahunch sakati hai। - yadi aapako chakakar a rahe hain, ya aap kisi bhi kaaray ko karane men khud ko asamarath pa rahe hain to aise samay men daॉkatar ko dikhaama behad aavashayak hota hai। do din se jayaada kabaj ya bukhaar rahane par turnt daॉkatar se samaparak karen। Treatments: dihaaidaresham ke upaay (Treatment for Dehydration) - jitana ho sake jayaada se jayaada paani mem kam se kam ek baar soop jaroor pien। ninboo paani (Lemon water) ninboo paani n siraph sharir ko haaiderat rakhata hai balaki sharir ke taॉkasin bhi baahar nikaalata hai। ninboo paami pine se hai। upachaar ke lie 4 kap paani men ek kap jau bhiga dem। usake baad is paani ko lagabhag 45 minat dhakakar ubaalen। jab achachhi tarah ubal jaae to is paani ko chhaanakar gunaguna rahane tak thnda karen aur isamen shahad milaakar pien। savaad barhaane ke lie ninboo ka ras bhi milaaya ja sakata hai। Disease: ghamauriyn (Prickly Heat) Description: ghamauriyon ko ngareji men parikali hit (Prickly Heat) kahate hain। garamiyon ke mausam men ghamauriyn hona aam baat hai। garami ke mausam men sharir se pasina adhik maatara men bahata hai। yadi samay rahate is pasine ko saaf na kiya jaae to yah sharir ki tavacha men hi sookh jaata hai jisake kaaran pasine ki garnthiyn bnd ho jaati hain aur sharir men ghamauri hone lagati hain। Symptoms: - sharir men khujali hona - sharir mem jalan ya knte si halaki soojan aur chubhan mahasoos hone lagati hai। ghamauri ke daane dhoop ke sidhe snparak men aane se baṛh jaate hain। aamataur par ghamauri kuchh dinon men apane aap sahi ho jaati hai lekin kuchh logom men yah haphaton aur mahinon tak ke lie ho sakati hai। isalie ek haphate tak ghamauri ke thik na hone par daॉkatar se jaroor paraamarash lena chaahie। ghamauri (Prickly Heat) ke kaaran logon men samaya, hasatamaithun ke dauraan ya sekas ke baare men sochane par hota hai to ye maanasik kaaranon ki vajah se ho sakata hai। dhayaan rahe ki tanaav ke kaaran sharir men kai haaramonas ka satar baṛh bahaav men kami aati hai to vah thik se sakhat mahin ho paata aur irekataail disaphnkashan jaisi samasayaaen shuroo ho jaati hain। * nayooraॉlaji se juṛi samasayaaen (naravas sisatam men aai kisi kami) bhi irekataail disaphmkashan ka kaaran ho sakati hain। Treatments: irekataail disaphnkashan ka upachaar (Treatment of Erectile Dysfunctions) Home Remedies: yoon to is samasaya ke upachaar ki shuruaat khaana-paan mem sudhaar v vayaayaama, dhayaan v yog aadi karane se ki jaati hai, lekin yadi isase koi laabh najar n aae to isake chikitasakiy upachaar kiye jaate hain। taritament daॉkatar idi ka upachaar karane se pahale is samasaya ke kaaran ka pata lagaata hai। isake lie kai tarah ke tesat bhi kie jaate hain। aur phir niman upachaar maadhayamon ki madad li ja sakati hai - haॉramon taritament ka koi khaas saaid iphekat bhi nahin hota hai। balad sapalaai (Blood Supply) ling men dhamaniyon men kisi parakaar ki rukaavat ki vajah se rakat ke paravaah men kami a jaati hai, to aiese jivan mem sudhaar karake is samasaya se bach sakata hai। balad pareshar ya haृday samasayaaon se bachaav (Blood Pressure and Heart Problems) ling ke sakhat hone ka mukhay kaaran usamen rakat ka thik ijaikuleshan (Premature Ejaculation) Description: parimecha‍yor ijaikulesham (Premature Ejaculation) arathaat shigharapatan purushon ko hone vaali ek parakaar ki yaun samasaya hai। is samasaya men sa‍vabhaav men chiṛachiṛa ho jaata hai, use siradarad v tanaav jaisi shaa‍ririk samasa‍yaaen bhi ho sakati hain। kai baar dekha jaata hai ki shigharapatan se garasit vayakati ki kuchh samay ke baad ja sakata hai। saath hi yoorin aur rakat ki jnch davaara bhi bimaari aur usamen ho rahe sudhaar ka pata lagaaya ja sakata hai। Disease: ghengha (Goiter) Descriptiom: ghengha yaani goitar (Goiter) rog ebamaॉramal tarike se barh rahi hai। ghengha rog ke vishay men anay mahatavapooran jaanakaari niman hai: ghengha ke vishay mem jaanakaari (Information of Goiters in Hindi) * khaane men aayodin ki kami Goiter im Hindi) 1. namaka- khaane men hamesha aayodin vaala namak khaane se ghengha rog mem bahut laabh milata hai। 2. karajani- goonja ya karajani ki jad aur bij se nikaala hua tel lagaane se aur naak men daalane se galagarnthi aur gale ki gnth men laabh hota hai। 3. aparaajitaa- saphed aparaajita ki jad ke ek se do garaam chooram ko ghi men misharit kar pine se athava katu phal ke chooran ko gale ke anadar gharashan karame se ghengha rog shnt hota hai। 4. pipala- pipal aur thoohar ka lep karane se medaj ghengha (motaape ki vajah se gale ki gmthe) thik ho jaati hain। 5. devadaaroo- devadaaroo aur inadaraayan ko ek saath pisakar lep karane se kaphaj ghengha thik ho jaati hai। 6. arndi- arndi ki jad ko pisakar chaaval ke paani men milaakar subaha-shaam lep karame se ghengha rog thik ho jaata hai। 7. samudaraphala- samudaraphala, sahajan ke bij aur dashamool ki saari aushadhiyon ko sil par pisakar halakaa-halaka garam lep karane se vaataj galagnd yaani ghengha (gais ki vajah se gale ki gnthe) rog thik ho jaata hai। 8. amalataasa- amalataas ki jad ko baarik pisakar paani men milaakar galagnd (ghenghaa) tatha gndamaala (gale ki gmthe) par lep karane se domon rog thik ho jaate hain। 9. lauki- lauki ke pake hue phal men paani bharakar ek sapataah tak rakhe rahame den। usake baad pine se ghengha rog samaapat ho jaata hai। 10. laal arndi- laal arndi ki jad ko pisakar chaavalon ke paani men milaakar lep karane se ghengha rog thik ho jaata hai। 11. soorajamukhi- soorajamukhi ki jad aur lahasun donon ko pisakara, tikiya banaakar gale par bndhane se ghengha phoot jaata hai aur bahakar saaph ho jaata hai magar isase darad bahut hota hai। Disease: motaapa (Obesity) Description: sharir ke ndar asaamaanay roop se jama vasa hi obesiti (Obesity) hai। saamaanayataur khujali se mijaat ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home remedies for Itching) 1. naariyal ka tel (Coconut oil)- tavacha ke shushak hone ya kisi kide ke kaatane se, khujali kisi bhi kaaran se ho, naariyal ka tel petaroliyam jaili (Petroleum jelly)- yadi tavacha behad snvedanashil (sensitive skim) hai to khujali se nijaat ke lie petaroliyam jaili behad achachha upaay hai। isamen koi bhi rasaayan nahin hota aur tavacha par ninboo ke ras ko rooi ki sahaayata se lagaaya ja sakata hai। 4. beking soda (Baking soda)- tin hisase beking soda men ek hisasa paani milaakar ek pesat banaayem। is pesat ko parabhaavit
