hai। Disease: gale men darad (Throat Ache) Description: gale men darad (Throat ache) saamaanay saradi ka snket bhi ho sakata hai aur vokal korad men inphekashan ya satarep tharot (strep throat) jaisi barasaaitis - ऑsatiyokondaraaitis - kaaratilej ka phatana - kaaratilej ka ghis jaana Treatments: jodon ke darad se raahat ke lie tipas (Tips to prevent joint pain) 1. gatishil rahen (Keep moving) jodom ke darad se raahat ke lie gatishil rahen, yaani jodon ki moovament hoti rahani chaahie। lnbe samay tak ek hi sathiti men rahane se bhi jodon men kathorata mahasoos hoti hai। 2. jodon ko chot se bachaaen (Prevemt joints from injury) jodon par lagi chota, hadadi ko tod bhi sakati hai, isalie jodon ko chot se bachaakar rakhen। jab bhi koi aisa khel khelen jisamen jodon par chot lagane ka dar ho, to javaaint sephati pedas (Joint safety pads) pahanen। tenis aur golaph khelate samay bhi bareses (braces) pahanen। 3. vajam ko niyntarit rakhen (Maintain your weight) yadi aapaka vajan niyntaran men rahega to aapake jod bhi savaasathay rahemge। sharir ka jayaada vajan ghutanon aur kamar par adhik dabaav daalata hai, jisase kaaratilej (cartilage) ke tootane ka dar rahata hai। aise men vajan ko niyntaran men rakhana behad jaroori hai। 4. satareching jayaada n karem (Do mot stretch more) vayaayaam karate samay satareching karane ki bhi salaah di jaati hai, lekin satareching keval haphate men tin baar karen। satareching ko ekadam shuroo karane ki jagaha, isase pahale vaaram ap vayaayaam (warm up exercise) karen। 5. doodh pien (Drink milk) jodon ko majaboot rakhane ke lie doodh jaroor pien। doodh se hadadiyon ko kailashayim aur vitaamin di milata hai jisase hadadiyn majaboot banati hain। yadi doodh pasmd n ho to doodh se bane anay khaaday padaarath jaise panira, dahi aadi bhi khaae ja sakate hain। 6. sahi poshachar banaae rakhen (Maintain right posture) jodom ke darad se raahat ke lie sahi poshachar men uthamaa, baithana aur chalana behad jaroori hai। sahi poshachar garadan se lekar ghutanon tak ke jodon ki rakasha karata hai। 7. vayaayaam (Exercise) jodon ke savaasathay ke lie vayaayaam ko dainik dinacharaya ka hisasa bamaaen। tairaaki (swimming) bhi jodon ke darad se raahat ke lie achachha vayaayaam hoti hai। Home Remedies: jodon ka darad (Joint Pain) sharir ke kisi bhi bhaag men ho sakata hai, ghutane, kndhe ya kamara। kai baar gathiya jodon ke darad ka kaaran hota hai jo kai baar tanaav lene, parabhaavit hisason par jayaada dabaav padne, moch aane ya kisi anay parakaar ki chot lagane ke kaaram bhi aisa ho sakata hai। jodom ke darad mem parabhaavit hisasa laal ho sakata hai aur vahn soojan bhi a sakati hai। aaie ham aapako bataate hain ki kaun se ghareloo upaay apanaakar aap jodon ke darad men raahat pa sakate hain। jodon ke darad ke lie ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies for Joint Pain) maalish (Massage) maalish se sharir ke darad men behad aaraam milata hai, yahi parakariya jodon ke darad men bhi laagoo hoti hai। naariyala, jaitoona, sarasom ya lahasun ke tel se parabhaavit hisase ki maalish karem। halake haathon se dabaav dete hue darad vaale hisase ko malen। aisa karane se darad se raahat milegi। garam aur thndi sikaai (Cold and Hot Compress) jodon ke darad se nijaat ke lie garam aur thndi sikaai karane se bhi bahut aaraam milata hai। garam sikaai karane se rakat snchaar behatar hota hai vahin thmdi sikaai se soojan aur chubham sikaai karen। sikaai karate vakat kam se kam do se tin minat tak garadan ki lagaataar sikaai honi chaahie। yah poori parakariya 15 se 20 minat men doharaaen। is vidhi ko aaraam home tak din men do baar karen। lahasum (Garlic) yadi jodon men darad hai to lahasun ka isatemaal behad achachhe parinaam de sakata hai। isake aushadhiy gun garadan ke darada, soojan aur jalan ko thik karate hain। lahasun ki do kali har subah khaali pet paani ke saath khaaen। khaana banaane vaale kisi bhi tel men lahasun ki kuchh kaliyn daal kar bhoon len। is tel ko gunaguna hone tak thnda karen aur parabhaavit hisase ki maalish karen। is vidhi ko din men do baar kiya ja sakata hai। haladi (Turmeric) haladi ke aushadhiy gun kisi se chhipe nahin hai lekim achachhi baat yah bhi hai ki yah jodom ke darad men bhi utani hi parabhaavi hai। haladi rakat snchaar tej karake jodon ke darad se aaraam deti hai aur garadan ki akadn ko bhi kam karati hai। adarak (Ginger) jodon ke darad ke ilaaj ke lie adarak bhi behatarim parabhaav dikhaata hai। yah harab bhi gunom se bharapoor hai jo ki rakat snchaar ko tej karati hai jisase garadan ke darad se raahat milati hai। ek din men lagabhag tin kap adarak ki chaay pien। adarak ki chaay bamaane ke lie paani men adarak ubaalen aur thnda karake isamen shahad milaaen। is pey ko pien। parabhaavit hisase ki adarak ke tel se masaaj bhi ki ja sakati hai। seb saaidar gilaas paani men kachacha seb saaidar siraka aur shahad milaakar pine se bhi laabh hota hai। laal mirach paaudar (Red Chillie Powder) laal mirach paaudar bhi jodon ke darad se raahat dene men bahut parabhaavi hai। upachaar ke lie ek kap naariyal ke tel ko garam karake, usamen do bade chamamach laal mirach paaudar milaaen। is misharan se parabhaavit hisase par lagaakar takariban 20 minat ke lie chhod den। jayaada aaraam ke lie is misharan ko paratidin darad vaale hisase par lagaaen। Disease: looj moshana- dasat (Loose Motion) Description: shauch ekadam patala ho aur baara- baar jaana pad raha ho, to yah dasat hai। dasat hone par shauch men paani ka bhaag jayaada hota hai। kai baar shauch jaate samay pet men darad (Pain) ya aintham (Crumping) bhi mahasoos hoti hai। Symptoms: - ek men saamaanay se kuchh jayaada baar shauch jaate hain jabaki doosari sathiti men lagaataar chhaha- saat ya usase jayaada baar shauch jaate hain। yah shauch har baar ekadam patali hoti hai। yah dasata, paacham snbndhi samasaya ke kaaran haate hain। jivaanuon davaara snkaraman tatha taॉkasin aadi phailaane se dasat home shuroo ho jaate hain। kai baar tanaav ya kisi parakaar ke dar ke kaaran bhi dasat shuroo ho sakate hain। aise dasat ko karonik ya jiran dasat kahate hain। kuchh anay kaaran niman hain- - baikatiriyaa, vaayaras ya parajivi ke kaaran - kuchh entibaayotik davaaon ke kaaran - bane padaarath n khaaen - naariyal paani, ninboo paani aur chhaachh aadi jayaada se jayaada len - adhapaka khaanaa, mit aadi n khaaen - yadi kisi ko dasat hain to, usase haath milaane ya chhoone ke jaroori khanij bhi sharir se baahar nikal jaate hain। is kaaran vayakati ko kamajori mahasoos hoti। dasat ki shikaayat kai kaaranon se ho sakati hai jaise- baasi khaana khaane, kisi khaane se elaraji hone, kisi tarah ka tanaav hone, dooshit paani ya khaana khaane, sharaab aadi jayaada pine se ya kabhi kabhi kuchh davaaiyon ke sevan se bhi। aaie ham aapako bataate hain ki ghareloo nusakhon ki sahaayata se kis tarah se aap looj moshan ki samasaya se raahat pa sakate hain। dasat ke upachaar ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Loose Motion) sarason ke bij (Mustard Seeds) sarason ke bij do chamamach karake pilaaya ja sakata hai। isase bhi dasat rook jaaenge। Disease: pet darad (Stomach Ache) Description: pet darad men darad chhaati aur pelavik rijan (pelvic region) ke bich ubharata ke kaaran bhi pet darad ki samasaya ho sakati hai। pet men darad kis hisase men hai, is sathiti ko dekhate hue bhi mimam kaaran bhi ho sakate hain: - apach - kabaj - maasik dharam (Pain in Periods) - khaane se elaraji - gais - alasar - pitat ki thaili men pathari - haaraniya - kidami mem pathari - yoorinari tarekat inphekashan (Urinary Tract Infectiom) - apemdikas (Appendix) - pelavik ho - pet men soojan ya sakhatapan a gaya ho - snsen jaladi jaladi chal rahi hon, yaami phool rahi hon - behoshi chha rahi ho - tej bukhaar ho Home Remedies: pet ka darad ek aam samasaya hai। gaisa, pet men pathari (Stone), haaraniya (Hernia) ya snkaraman (Infection) aadi hone par bhi pet darad hota hai। itana hi nahin kai baar jaroorat se jayaada kha lene par (Ovar Eating) bhi pet darad ki samasaya hoti hai। ham aapako kuchh ghareloo nusakhe bata rahe hain, jinahen aajamaakar aap pet darad se raahat pa sakate hain। phir bhi yadi pet darad ki samasaya lagaataar bani rahe to chikitasak ko dikhaana jaroori hota hai, par ghareloo nusakhon se saamaanay pet darad ko chutakiyon men thik kiya ja sakata hai। pet darad ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Stomach Ache) seb ka siraka bachaav ke lie saunph bhi behad gunakaari hai। bahut masaaledaar aur vasa vaale khaane se hone vaali apach ko behad jaladi thik kar deti hai। saunph men volaataail tel (volatile oil) hota hai jo ki ji milaakara, isamen ninboo milaaen। is paani ko pien। isase turnt raahat milati hai। ajavaayan (Carom Seed) ajavaayan pet ko duroosat rakhane aur khaane ko pachaame ke saath hi pet darad se bhi raahat ke daanon ko yoon bhi munh men rakhakar chabaaya ja sakata hai। pudina aur kaimomaail (Mint and Chamomile) pudina ya kaimomaail ki harabal ya garin ti bhi paachan shakati ko duroosat rakhati hai। ke dinon men yah pet ke saath hi poore sharir ke lie bhi phaayademnd hai। garam senk (Warm Compress) garam senk se pet ka darad turnt thik ho jaata hai। aisa karane se paachan kariya ko gati milati (Stress) Description: kisi baat se pareshaana, aahat ya dukhi hokara, vayakati ka man se gaham udaas hona hi tanaav hai। tanaav man se snbndhit hai। tanaav (Stress) ek tarah ka davnd hai jo sntulan aur saamnjasay n baitha paane ke kaaran hota hai। jo vayakati tanaav se garasit hota hai usaka man ashnt ho jaata hai, bhaavanaaen sathir nahin rah paatin। sahi aur galat ka phaisala karana mushakil ho jaata hai। aise men snbmdhit vayakati ki shaaririk aur maanasik donon hi sathitiyn dina-paratidin kharaab hoti jaati hain। Symptoms: - koi mujhe pasnd nahin karataa, aisi bhaavanaaen hona - naakhun kaatate rahana ya ek hi jagah takataki laga kar dekhate rahama - nind n aana - ya to bahut bhookh lagana ya bilakul bhookh n lagana - lagaataar saradi se pareshaan rahana - hamesha dukhi mahasoos karana ya bahut khushi ki baaton par bhi khush n hona - jayaada gusasa aur niraash hona - logom ke saath khud ko asahaj mahasoos karana - lagaataar sir darad aur pith darad - doosaron ko najarndaaj karana - kisi ek chij par dhayaan n lag paana - mam men hamesha nakaaraatamak vichaar aana - pet kharaab hona ya pet men alasar hona - man men aatamahataya jaise khayaal aana - bahut jayaada sona ya bilakul n sona Reasons: tanaav ke kaaran (Cause of stress) jab koi vayakati khud par dabaav mahasoos karata hai tab vayakati ke sharir se kuchh khaas kemikal nikalate hain jo sharir ko jayaada uraja aur taakat dete hain jisase aap khud ko sahaj mahasoos kar saken। jab khud ko asahaj ya dara hua mahasoos karate hain tab yah kemikal ulata asar dikhaame lagate hain। tanaav parisathiti par nirabhar karata hai, koi vayakati saadhaaram baat par bhi tanaav le leta hai jabaki koi vayakati bilakul bhi tamaav nahin letaa। koi badi- badi baat bhi nahin sochata jabaki koi kai chhoti-chhoti baatom ko ek saath sochata rahata hai। saamaanay baahari kaaran (Common External Reasons) - jivan men koi bada nakaaraatamak badalaav - sakool ya kaॉlej men kisi bhi tarah ka koi dabaav - rishaton men daraar - aarathik tngi - kaam ka jayaada bojh - bachache aur parivaar ki sathiti thik n hona saamaanay kaaran (Common Reasons of Stress) - bahut door ka sochate rahana - khud se nakaaraatamak baaten karate rahana - khud men kami dhoondhate rahana - khud men aatamavishavaas ki kami hona Treatments: tanaav door karane ke tipas (Tips to Prevent Stress) - kisi bhi parakaar ka masha n karen। - bharapoor nind aur aaraam jaroor karen। - khud ke upar dabaav mahasoos n karen। - man ko vayavasathit tatha majaboot karane ke lie pusataken jayaada parhen। - doosaron ko bhi sunana sikhen। - gusase par kaaboo sahaayak hai। Disease: esiditi ya amalapitat (Acidity) Description: esiditi (Acidity) Symptoms: - kabhi-kabhi chhaati men darad ho sakata hai। - khatati dakaaren aanaa, - khaana ya khatata paani men rakhakar chabaaen। saunph ke saath mishari bhi milaai ja sakati hai। aisa karane se esiditi se raahat milati hai। Disease: elaraji (Allergy) Descriptiom: elaraji (Allergy) kisi bhi chij ke parati atisnvedanashil hona hi elaraji hai, jise savaasathay ki bhaasha men etopi (atopy) bhi kahate hain। elaraji kisi se bhi ho sakati hai, mausam men badalaav se, kisi khaane ki chij se, paalatu jaanavar se, dhool se, dhuem se, saundaray parasaadhanon se ya davaaon aadi se। elaraji men sharir ka imayoon sisatam kuchh khaas chijon ko savikaar nahin kar paataa। in chijon ke parati imayooniti ayogay tarah se paratikariya deti hai। imayooniti davaara di jaane vaali paratikariya hi elaraji hoti hai। yoon dekha jaae to adhikatar elaraji khataranaak nahin hoti lekin kabhi kabhi samasaya gmbhir ho jaati hai। elaraji ko roka ja sakata hai, lekin isake lie elaraji paida karane vaale kaaranon se poori tarah door rahana hogaa। yoon to elaraji phailane vaali bimaari mahin hai phir bhi yadi kisi ko naak bahane aur nkhon se paani aane vaali elaraji ho to usase snparak banaakar rakhane men hi behatari hai। snbhav ho to usake davaara isatemaal kie gae saamaan ko bhi isatemaal n karen। Symptoms: - nkh men khujali hona aur nkh ka laal ho jaana - nkh se paani aana - egajima aur garamiyon men bukhaar - gale men khujali hona - tavacha par khujali hona - tavacha par pitat uthana - tavacha par laal chakatate aur daane hona - naak ke ndar baara- baar daane nikalana - naak mem baara-baar khujali hona - naak se paani aana Reasons: elaraji ke kaarana- (cause of allergy) 1. dhool (Dust) dhool ke kan bahut chhote jiv hote hain jo hamaare- aas paas ki jayaadaatar vasatuon par rahate hain। yah kam uchach aadarata men panapate hain jo maृt tavachaa, baikatiriya aur phngas aadi se apana khaana paraapat karate hain। 2. kit (Imsect) kiton se elaraji vaale logom ko kiton ke kaatane se dnk lagane se tavacha ekadam laal hokar phool jaati hai। itana hi nahin unahen ulati, chakakar aana aur bukhaar bhi ho sakata hai। 3. khaana (Food) kuchh logon ko rojamarara men khaayi jaane vaali chijom se bhi elaraji hoti hai, jaise moongaphali, doodh aur nda aadi। khaaday padaarath se elaraji vaale logon ko khaane ke baad ji michalaane, sharir men khujali hone ya daane nikalane ki samasaya ho sakati hai। 4. rabad (Latex) rabad se bana koi bhi utapaada, elaraji ka kaaram ho sakata hai। kuchh logon ko rabad se bane utapaad bhi nukasaan pahunchaate hain, jaise dasataane, kndoma, medikal upakaran aadi ke isatemaal se jalana, naak bahanaa, chhimkanaa, sms ki ghabaraahat aur khujali ki samasayaaen ho sakati hain। 5. khushaboo (Fragrance) achachhi khushaboo bhale achachhi lagati ho lekin yah bhi kuchh logon ki elaraji ka kaaran ho sakati hai। paraphayooma, khushaboo vaali momabatatiyn, kai tarah ke bayooti paraॉdakat aadi ki khushaboo se sir darada, ji michalaame aur maak ki elaraji ho sakati hai। 6. jaanavar (Pets) paalatu jaamavar bhi kai logon ki elaraji ka kaaran hote hain। jaanavaron ke baala, unake munh se nikalane vaali laara, roosi aadi se kai gmbhir pareshaaniyn ho sakati hain। 7. ghaas (Grass) kai baar ghaasa, ped aur phool bhi elaraji ka kaaran hote hain। yah sab mausami elaraji ka kaaran hote hain, jimase khujali, nkhon men jalana, lagaataar chhink aama aur khujali aadi ki samasaya ho sakati hai। Treatments: elaraji se nijaat paane ke lie upaay (Tips to Prevent Allergy) - dhoola, dhuma aur gndagi se bachakar rahen। - kuchh davaaon jaise esapirina, nimusalaaid aadi ke sevan men saavadhaani baraten। - khatati chijon, jaise achaar aadi ka isatemaal kam karem। - aise khaaday padaarath jinahen khaane se elaraji hai, unahem n khaaem। - gndagi se elaraji vaale logon ko samaya-samay par chaadara, takiye ke kavar aur parade aadi badalate rahame chaahie। Home Remedies: dhool (Dust), gndagi (Dirt), mausam mem parivaratan (Climate change), silama, aadi kuchh aise kaaran hain jinase vayakati ko elaraji (Allergy) ho sakati hai। parayaavaran men maujood chijon ke lie alaga-alag snvedanashilata hoti hai jisake chalate hamaara sharir paratikariya karata hai। aise men vijaatiy padaarathon ki sharir men asavikaarata elaraji hai। hona aadi elaraji ke kuchh lakashan hain। aaie aapako bataate hain elaraji se bachane ke kuchh ghareloo upaae (Home remedies of Allergy): 1.shahad (Honey)- shahad sharir ki rog paratirodhak kashamata ko barhaata hai। rojaana do chamamach shahad ka isatemaal sharir ko kaaphi laabh pahunchaata hai। ek gilaas gunagume paani mem shahad mila kar pine se ya doodh men shahad mila kar pine se kaaphi laabh elaraji se bachaane men haladi bhi kaaphi parabhaavashaali hai। haladi mem taakatavar enti ऑkasident paae jaate haim jo elaraji se ladne men madad karate hain। ek gilaas garam doodh men ek chamamach haladi milaakar pine se kaaphi laabh pahunchata hai। 4. lahasoon (Garlic)- lahasoon bhi ek enti elaraji khaaday padaarath hai jise apani daait men shaamil karana aavashayak hai। yah ek enti baॉyotika, (Lemon)- ninboo men uchach maatara men vitaamin si aur enti ऑkasident paaya jaata hai। minboo imayoon sisatam barhaata hai aur elaraji se door rakhane men kaaphi phaayademnd saabit hota hai। 6. adarak isamen maujood thiyaanin bhi elaraji se bachaane men madad karata hai। yadi kisi ko garin ti pasnd n ho to balaik ti bhi pi ja sakati hai। 8. baadaam (Almond)- baadaam mem vitaamin bi, i, maiganishiyama, jinka, seleniyam (selenium) tatha anay savaasathayavaradhak vasa paai jaati hai। jis kaaran yah tanaav se to raahat dete hi hain saath hi elaraji se bachaame men bhi madad karate hain। rog paratirodhak kashamata ko tej kar sharir aur dimaag ko majabooti dete hain। baadaam ko bhoon kar ya kachacha bhi khaaya ja sakata hai। yadi aise khaana snbhav n ho to baadaam ka paaudar banaakara, doodh ke saath khaaya ja sakata hai। Disease: motiyaabinda- keterekat (Cataract) Descriptiom: keterekat ya motiyaabind (Cataract) motiyaabind nkh ke lens men ubhara saphed rng ka dhababa hai, jo ki nkh ki daृshati ko parabhaavit karata hai। motiyaabind hone se vayakati ko koi bhi vasatu dhundhali najar aati hai। motiyaabind jayaadaatar bujuragon ko hota hai। motiyaabind keval ek nkh ya domom mkhon men bhi ho sakata hai, yahn tak ki yah ek nkh se doosari mkh men bhi phail sakata hai। Symptoms: - nkhon ke lens par saphed parat ka jamana - ek nkh se do chijen najar aana - kai dapha halaki roshani bhi bahut tej paratit hona - kisi bhi vasatu ka rng halaka najar aana - koi bhi vasatu dhundhali najar aana - chashame ka nnbar baara-baar badalana - tej roshani se pareshaani hona - raat ki laait men chhalale numa aakaृti najar aana - raat ko gaadi chalaane men dikakat homa - shaam hote hi nkhon ki roshani aur bhi kamajor hona Reasons: nkh ke mdar ka lens kaimare ki tarah kaam karata hai। yahi retina par laait ko phokas karata hai jisase chijen saaph najar aati hain। lens paani aur parotin se milakar banata hai। parotin is tarah se lens ke saath judi rahati hai ki yah lens ko saaph rakhati hai jisase ki roshani aara-paar ja sake। umar barhane ke saath kai baar kuchh parotin ek jagah ikatathi ho jaati hai aur lens ke ek hisase par jama ho jaati hai। aise men motiyaabind nkh ke lens men atayadhik parotin ke banane ke kaaran hota hai jo lems ko dhundhala bana deta hai। yah lens ke jarie roshani ko poori tarah jaane mahin deta jisase nkh se saaph dikhaai mahim detaa। aise men sabhi nae lens selasa, lens ke baahar ki or jama ho jaate hain jabaki sabhi puraane lens selasa, lens ke bichon bich ek jagah ikatatha ho jaate hain, jise motiyaabimd ya keterekat kahate hain। motiyaabind hone ke anay kaaran (other reason & causes of cataract) - nkhon men kisi tarah ka anay rog honaa, jaisa galookoma aadi - janamajaat nkh men motiyaabind hona - daayabitij hona - sharir men kisi pareshaani, jaise asathama ke lie sateraॉid lena - achaanak se tej roshani ke snparak men aane se ya lagaataar tej roshami men rahane se - dhoomarapaan ya sharaab aadi ka jayaada sevan karane se Treatments: motiyaabind ke upaay (tips to prevent cataract) - dhoop ya tej roshami se khud ko bachaaem, nkhon par chashama aur sir par topi pahan ke rahen - kisi bhi tarah ka koi nasha n karen - paushatik khaana khaaen - samaya-samay par nkhon ki jnch karavaaen - tanaav se door rahen - daayabitij niymtaran men rakhen Home Remedies: jab nkhon ki baat ho to samasaya ko gnbhirata se lema chaahie, kayonki yadi nkhon ki roshami ek baar chali gai to dobaara nahin paai ja sakati। motiyaabind (Cataract) bhi aisi hi gnbhir samasaya hai, jisamem mkhon ke lens par ek dhababa (spot on the eye lens) a jaata hai। jisase aap jo bhi chij dekhate hain vah aapako dhundhali najar aati hai aur vahn aapako dhababa jaisa najar aata hai। yoon to motiyaabind ko sarajari ke davaara hataaya ja sakata hai lekin kuchh ghareloo nusakhon ki madad se bhi motiyaabind ka ilaaj snbhav hai। yadi shurooaat men sachet hokar yah apanaae jaaen to snbhav hai aapako sarajari ya ऑparesham n karavaana pade। motiyaabind ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Cataract) lahasun (Garlic) lahasun ke asnkhay savaasathay laabh hain aur yah nkhon ke lie bhi samaan roop se laabhakaari hai। lahasun ki do se tin kaliyn (2 to 3 clove) rojaana khaane se nkhon se ekadam saaph dikhaai dene lagega aur kuchh hi dinon men dhababe ki shikaayat door ho jaaegi। paalak (Spinach) paalak khaane se motiyaabind kaaphi had tak thik ho jaata hai। paalak men bita kairotin (Bet Carotene) or entiऑkasident (Antioxidents) gun hote hain। paalak ko rojaana khaane se nkhon ka motiyaabind kuchh din men hi khatam ho jaata hai aur nkhen pahale jaisi ho jaati hain। doodh aur baadaam (Milk and Almond) motiyaabind se pareshaan logom ki mkhen jayaadaatar laal rahati hain aur samasaya se nipatama aur bhi mushakil hota hai। aise men doodh aur baadaam nkhon ko laabh dete hain। upachaar ke lie baadaam ko raat bhar doodh men bhigaakar chhod dem। is doodh ko subah chhaanakar isaki boonde mkhon men daalen aur baadaam ko chaba kar kha len। garin ti (Green Tea) garin ti se nkhon ki roshani tej ho sakati hai। garin ti saamaanay mkhon ki samasaya men bhi laabhakaari hai। rojaana tin se chaar baar garin ti pine nkhon ko savaasathay laabh hota hai। garin ti men maujood entiऑkasident (Antioxident) nkhon ko nai taajagi dete hain। kachacha papita (Raw Papaya) kachache papite men papen (Papain) naam ka enjaaim hota hai jo ki parotin (Protien) ke paachan men sahaayak hota hai। motiyaabind se pareshaan logon ko parotin ko pachaane mem dikakat aati hai, aise men kachacha papita motiyaabind se garasit logon ko laabh deta hai। kachacha papita rojaana isatemaal karane se nkhon ke lens nae jaise chamakane lagate hain। vitaamin si (Vitamin C) motiyaabind ke ilaaj mem vitaamim si mahatavapooran bhoomika nibhaata hai। vitaamim si ke sevan se motiyaabimd snrachanaaon ko roka ja sakata hai। aahaar men aise khaaday padaarathon ko isatemaal karen, jinamen vitaamin si jayaada se jayaada ho। isake alaava vitaamin si sapaliment (Vitamin C Suppliment) ke roop men bhi liya ja sakata hai। kachachi sabajiyn (Raw Vegetables) kachachi sabajiyn nkhon ke lie chamatakaar ka kaam kar sakati hai। kachachi sabajiyon mem poshak tatav aur vitaamin e (Vitamin A) ki uchach maatara hoti hai jo ki mkhom ke savaasathay ke lie jaroori hai। apane daimik aahaar men kachachi sabajiyon ko isatemaal karane se motiyaabind ke saath hi nkhon ki anay saamaanay samasayaaon se bhi nipata ja sakata hai। kachachi sabajiyon ko salaad ke roop men jitana smbhav ho khaaen। jaamun (Bilberrys) jaamun se motiyaabind poori tarah nahim hatata lekin daृshati ki asapashatata ko jaamun khaame se thik kiya ja sakata hai। jaamun mem enthosaayanosaaidas (Amthocyanosides) tatha phalevanaaidas (Flavonoids) kaaphi adhik hote hain jo ki retina (Retina) aur nkhon ke lains (Eye Lens) ki rakasha karate hain। Disease: saradi aur kaph (Cough And Cold) Description: saradi aur kaph (Cough and Cold) naak bah rahi hai, ya bnd hai jisase ki sns lene men takaliph ho rahi hai, gale men darad mahasoos ho raha hai ya gale men chubhan aur chhila (scratchy throat) jaise mahasoos ho raha hai aur khnsi ke saath balagam (muscus) pareshaan kar raha hai to samajh lijie aap saradi- jukaam aur kaph se pareshaan hain। Symptoms: - mkhon se khoob paani aana aur jalam hona - aavaaj bhaari homa - khaane men savaad aur khushaboo mahasoos n hona - gala chhila hua ya darad mahasoos hona - chhink aana - maak ka bnd hona - maak se khoob paani girama - naak se gale ki or balagam ka girana - mnsapeshiyom men darad ya khinchaav hona - sir bhaari mahasoos hona ya halaka darad hona Reasons: kaarana- (Cause of Cough and Cold) saradi hinovaayaras (rhinovirus) se phailati hai jo ki 10 se 40 paratishat tak saradi ko sharir men paravesh karaata hai। vahin koronaavaayaras (coronavirus) lagabhag 20 paratishat saradi ke lie jimamedaar hota hai। inake alaava resapiretari sinsitaayal vaayaras (respiratory syncytial virus) aur pairaaimphalooenja vaayaras (parainfluemz virus) 10 phisadi tak saradi ke lie jimamedaar hote hain। saradi, snkaraman se bhi phailati hai। ek snkaramit vayakati ya usake davaara isatemaal kie gae saamaan ke snparak men aane se doosare ko bhi saradi ki samasaya ho sakati hai। yah vaayaras sharir ke ndar pahunchakar vayakati ki rog kashamata ko parabhaavit karate hain aur kaaphi maatara men balagam banaana shuroo kar dete hain, jisase gala aur naak poori tarah parabhaavit ho jaate hain। itama hi nahin snkaramit vayakati ke chhinkane (sneezing), usase haath milaane se bhi saradi ke baikatiriya doosare vayakati ko parabhaavit kar sakate hain। saradi aur kaph ke lie kai anay kaaran (Other causes of Cough and Cold) - kamare men silan ya ghutan ho - tej dhoop se aane ke baad turnt thnda paani pina - sharir ki paratirodhak kashamata kamajor hona - bahut tej paraphayoom ya tel ka isatemaal - ऑphis ya ghar ke baahar bina haath saaph kie khaanaa-pina Treatments: saradi se raahat ke lie tipas (Tips to prevent cough and cold) - aaraam karen, khoob pey padaarath len aur savaasathayavaradhak khaama khaaen। - yadi bukhaar ya sharir men darad ho to pairaasitaamaॉl li ja sakati hai। - naak par baam ya baajaar men maujood sapare ka isatemaal kiya ja sakata hai। isase bnd naak khulegi aur raahat milegi। - garam paani men namak daal kar garaare karate rahen। - khaane-pine se pahale apane haath achachhi tarah dhoen। - smkaramik vayakati ke snparak men n aaen, jaise ki haath milaane ki jagah namasate ki ja sakati hai। - yadi aap khud snkaramit haim to bhid vaali jagahon par jaane se bachen aur apani chijem jaise roomaal aadi doosaron se door rakhen। - thndi aur baahar ki chijen khaane se parahej karen। Home Remedies: mausam men parivaratana, sarada-garam hone ya paradooshan aur elaraji (Allergy) ya snkaraman (Infection) ke kaaran saradi-khnsi ki samasaya ho jaati hai। kai baar snkaraman bhi isaka kaaram hota hai। aaie jaanate hain, saradi khnsi se bachaav ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Cough amd Cold): 1. haladi (Turmeric)- aadha kap garam paani ko ubaal len phir usamen ek chamamach kaali mirach paaudar (black pepper powder), ek chamamach haladi paaudar aur ek chamamach shahad milaaen। ab is misharan ko do se tim minat tak ubaal len aur miyamit taur par kaarhe ki tarah pien। 2. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ko ghisakar ya chhote-chhote tukadon men kaatakar ek kap paani men daalakar ubaal lem। din bhar men tin se chaar baar is ghol ko pien। shahad aur ninboo ko adarak ke ras mem milaakar pine se bhi kaph ki shikaayat door hoti hai। 3. ninboo (Lemon)- ek chamamach shahad men do chamamach ninboo ka ras milaakar garam kar lem। dim bhar mem kai baar is ghol ko dava ki tarah lete rahen। 4. lahasun (Garlic)- laung ke tel aur shahad men lahasun ki do se tin kali ko pis kar mila len। din bhar men kai baar thodi thodi maatara men isaka sevan karate rahen। 5. payaaj (Onion)- ek chamamach shahad men aadha chamamach payaaj ka ras len aur isako milaakar din bhar men kam se kam do baar avashay sevan karen। kaph aur gale ki kharaash se raahat milegi। 6. garam taral padaarath pien (Drimk warm liquids)- garam paani pien ye gale ki soojam (throat sweeling) ke lie phaayademnd hai। aap chaahen to koi anay garam padaarath bhi pi sakate hain। 7. shahad (Honey)- shahad gale ko aaraam pahunchaane ke lie ek paarnparik upaay hai। ek gilaas garam paani men shahad aur nimboo ka ras milaakar din men tin baar pime se khnsi se raahat milati hai। 8. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vimegar)- seb ka siraka har tarah ki khnsi ke lie achachha hai। 2 bada chamamach siraka 10 tola paani men milaakar garam karen। isamen ek chamamach shahad daalakar pien। khnsi men raahat paane ka kaaragar upaay hai। 9. tulasi ke patate aur shahad (Honey amd basil leaves)- dhule hue tulasi ke kuchh pataton ko koot kar usaka ras nikaalen aur usame shahad milaaen। ab ise chamamach men garam karake din men 3-4 baar len, is ghareloo upaay se khnsi men jaladi aaraam milata hai। Disease: titamas (Tetanus) Description: titanas (Tetanus) manushayon ke ghaav (Wound) men snkaramam hone se titanas hota hai jisaka kaaran kalosataridiyam titaani baikatiriya (Clostridium Tetani Bacteria) hai। yahi jivaanu ghaav ya chot mem vish paida karata hai jisase titanas ho jaata hai। dhire-dhire yahi jahar poore sharir men phailane lagata hai jisase sathiti ghaatak ho jaati hai। titanas ke kaaran kai baar vayakati ki maृtayu bhi ho sakati hai। titanas men sharir ki mnsapeshiyon men ainthan mahasoos hoti hai aur rook rook kar darad hota hai। haalmki kisi chot ke lagane ke baad yadi turnt titanas ka tika lagavaaya jaae to isase hone vaali pareshaaniyon se bacha ja sakata hai। Symptoms: - uchach rakatachaap - garadan men ainthan hona - chidchidaapan - chehare ki mnsapeshiyon ka jakad jaana - jabade ka bnd ho jaana - nigalane men dikakat hona - pasina khoob aana - mnsapeshiyon men ainthan aur akadn mahasoos homa - sns lene men takaliph hona - haृday gati ka tej hona Reasons: titanas ka kaaran (Cause of Tetamus) kalosataridiyam titaani (Clostridium Tetani)chhad ke aakar ka jivaanu hai jo duniya bhar men mitati men paaya jaata hai। kalosataridiyam titaami titanas rog ke lie jimamedaar jivaanu hai। yah baikatiriya do roopom mem paaya jaata hai, pahala doramnt ya nishakariy roop men doosara sakariy roop men jo jivaanuon ki snkhaya ko aur bhi barha deta hai। kisi bhi tarah ki chot men titanas ho sakati hai। - ghaav se - sarajari mem - parasav ke dauraan - koi phoda hone par - sui ya injekashan se nasha karane vaalon ko - kisi puraane jng lage lohe se chot lagane se Treatments: titanas se bachane ke lie tipas (Tips to Prevent Tetanus) - koi bhi aisa ghaav jisase tavacha phat gai ho, use turmt paani aur saabun se saaph kiya jaama chaahie। - ghaav ko kabhi khula n chhoden। khule ghaav ke smkaraman ka khatara jayaada hota hai। - yadi ghaav se khoon bah raha ho to to us par sooti aur sookha kapada bndhen। - rakat ko rokane ke lie ghaav ke upar dabaav daalen, jisase rakat bahana rook jaae। - ghaayal vayakati ko turnt titanas ka tika lagavaana chaahie। titanas ke anay upachaar (Treatment of Tetanus) - ghaav ko garam paani se dhoen aur koi entisepatik karim ya paaudar lagaaen। - taarapin ke tel se sharir ki maalish karen, isamen paira, jabade aur garadan par halake haath se dabaav daalate hue maalish karen। - ghaav ke upar tel ko garam karake usamen haladi milaakar lagaaen - momabatati ke mom ko pighalaakar bhi ghaav par lagaaya ja sakata hai - kate sathaan par nim ka tel lagaane se bhi titanas ka dar nahin rahata Disease: moch (Sprains) Descriptiom: moch (Sprains) sharir ke jod ke ligaament (ligament) ya samaayu jab kisi chot ke kaaran jaroorat se jayaada khinch jaate hain to is avasatha ko moch (Sprains or Moch) kaha jaata hai। jayaada khinchaav ke kaaran peshiyon ke phaaibar phat jaate hain aur ligaament men ghaav ho jaata hai। ligaament ek hadadi ko doosari hadadi se jodne (conmect) ka kaaray karate hain। Symptoms: - chot vaali jagah par asahaniy darad - chot vaali jagah par sunanapan hona - parabhaavit sathaan ko modne ya chalaane men pareshaani hona - parabhaavit sathaan par nila ya kaala dhababa aana - parabhaavit sathaan par soojan aana - bina sahaare ke chalane phirane men dikakat homa Reasoms: moch ke kaarama- (Causes of Sprains) moch sharir ke alaga-alag hisason men alaga-alag kaaranon se a sakati hai। moch saamaamay ya karonik bhi ho sakati hai। 1. enkal men moch (Ankle Sprains)- unchi-nichi jagah par chalane ya daudne se enkal men moch a sakati hai। kai baar haai hil pahanane se pair achaanak se mudta hai, yah bhi pair men moch ka kaaram ho sakata hai। 2. ghutane men moch (Kmee Sprains)- bhaagate- bhaagate achaanak gir jaane ya koi bhaari vasatu uthaakar chalane se ghutanon men moch a sakati hai। kai baar chalate chalate achaanak ghutama mud jaata hai। yah bhi ghutane mem moch ka kaaran ho sakata hai। 3. kalaai men moch (Wrist Sprains)- girane ke dauraan haath ke mudne, kisi ke davaara haath ko galat tarike se khinchane, khel ke dauraan aadi sathitiyon mem kalaai men moch a sakati hai। 4. kamar men moch (Waist Sprains)- kai baar sirhiyn charhane utarame men dikakat hone yaa, kisi unchi jagah se kamar ke bal girane se ya jaroorat se jayaada bhaari chij ko jhukakar uthaane se kamar men moch a sakati hai। 5. ngoothe men moch (Thumb Sprains)- kai tarah ke khel khelane ya kahin ngootha dab jaane ke kaaran chot lagane se ngoothe mem moch a sakati hai। 6. garadan men moch (Neck Sprains)- achaanak se garadan men jhataka lagane, jayaada uncha takiya lagaane, kisi parakaar se garadan men chot lagane ki sathiti men garadan men moch a sakati hai। anay kaaran (other causes & reason of sprains) - kai baar vayaayaam karane se pahale vaaramaap n hona aur achaanak se kathin vayaayaam shuroo kar dena bhi moch aane ka kaaran ho sakata hai। - pair men paraॉpar phutaviyar n hone se bhi pair ke mudne ya chot lagane ka khatara barh jaata hai jisase moch ki snbhaavana rahati hai। Treatments: moch se mijaat ke lie upaay (Treatmemt of Sprain Pain) - moch se mijaat ke lie parabhaavit sathaan par chane bndh den। in chanon ko baara- baar bhigaate rahem। jaise jaise chane phoolemge, moch thik hoti jaaegi। - moch vaale sathaan par ernd ke pataton ko halaka sa senk kar us par sarason ka tel lagaakara, parabhaavit sathaan par bmdh den। - til ke tel men aphim milaakar moch vaale sathaan par bndh dem। - moch vaale sathaan par haladi, choona aur shahad ko milaakar lagaane se chot thik ho jaati hai। - moch se mijaat ke lie tejapatata aur laung ko pisakar lep lagaaen। - sarason ke tel men ajavaayam aur lahasun ko garam karake, is tel se moch vaale sathaan ki maalish karen। - paan ke patate par sarasom ka tel lagaakar use halaka garam karen aur moch vaale sathaan par bndhen । - tulasi patatom ke ras men sarason ka tel milaakar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen। turnt aaraam milegaa। - akharot ke tel se maalish karane par bhi chot men aaraam milata hai। - namak ko garam karake, kisi mote kapade men bndhakara, chot vaale sathaan par bndh den। aaraam milegaa। - namak aur haladi ko milaakar chot vaale sathaan par lagaane se bhi aaraam milegaa। - paam ke patate ya aam ke patate par tel lagaakara, us par namak lagaaen aur garam karake chot vaale sathaan par bndh den। aisa karane se bhi moch thik ho jaaegi। - moch aur soojan men elovera lagaane se bhi aaraam milata hai। Home Remedies: unchi edi ke joote-chapapal pahanane, pair unche niche padne, vayaayaam bahut jayaada ya galat tarah se karane, bahut jayaada chalane, galat tarah se uthane baithane aadi aise kuchh kaaran hain, jinase sharir men moch (sprain) ki sathiti ban jaati hai। kai dapha darad asahaniy bhi ho sakata hai aur parabhaavit jagah par laal ya nila nishaan aur soojan bhi a sakati hai। yadi khinchaav ki pareshaani ho to pairon ko thamad se bachaayen aur aise kapade ka chunaav karen jo thanad ke dinon men aapake pairom ko hava n lagane den। aaie jaanem moch se raahat ke ghareloo upaay (Home remedies for sprain): 1. garam aur thnda senk (Hot amd cold compress)- sharir ke darad vaale hisase par karam se garam aur thnde paani ka sek karen, ye tamaavagarasat mnsapeshiyon ko aaraam pahunchaaegaa। ise kai tarike se kar sakate hain jaise ki tauliye ko garam paani men dubaayen aur tanaavagarasat mnsapeshi par laga sakate hain। tanaavagarasat mnsapeshi men aaraam ke lie gunagune paani se nahaaya ja sakata hai ya bhaap le sakate hain। baraph lagaakar bhi aaraam pa sakate hain। 2. mnsapeshi ko khinchana (Stretch your muscle)- din paratidin ki saamaanay shaaririk parakariya ke liye jaane se pahale, mnsapeshiyom ko khinchana mahatavapooran hota hai। isake lie halaki halaki satareching karen। agar aapako raat men sote samay pairon men khinchaav hota hai, to achachha hoga ki aap mnsapeshiyon ko khinchane ka abhayaas karen। 3. taral padaarath lete rahen (Take enough liquid)- taral padaarath ke saath paami ko niyamit ntaraal par lekar sharir men nami banaayen rakhen। 8 gilaas paami pine ke saath aapako phalom ka joos bhi pina chaahiye। parayaapat maatara men taral lena aapake mnsapeshiyon men kam marod paida karega aur aaraam degaa। 4. kela (Banana)- kele men parayaapat maatara men potaishiyam hota hai। yah sharir ke liye behad achachha hota hai। agar naashate ya bhojan ke baad paratidin ek kela khaate hain to yah mnsapeshiyon ko marod se door rakhega aur khinchaav se raahat degaa। 5. garam paid se sikaai (Hot pad)- ek samay aisa tha jab log garam paani ko paid par daalakar phir isatemaal karate the aur sharir par lagaakar sabhi parakaar ke darad se door rahate the। lekin ab baazaar men bijali se chalane vaale garam paid maujood hain। in paid se sikaai karane se mnsapeshiyon ka khinchaav door hota hai aur darad se raahat milati hai। 6. maalish (Massage)- parabhaavit hisase ki maalish karana bhi behad raahat deta hai। kisi bhi tel ko thoda gunaguna karake, usamen lahasun ki kuchh kaliyn daalem। kuchh der is tel ko aur garam karem aur gunaguna rahane par parabhaavit hisase ki halake haathon se maalish karen। kuchh hi der men pairon men khinchaav kam hoga aur darad men bhi aaraam milegaa। Disease: niman rakatachaap ya lo baladapareshar (Low Blood Pressure) Description: miman rakatachaap ya lo baladapareshar (Low Blood Pressure) lo baladapareshar ya niman rakatachaapa, ऑkasijan (oxygen) ko dimaag tak jaame se rokata hai। keval ऑkasijan hi nahi balaki anay poshak tatav bhi dimaag tak nahin pahumch paate। baladapareshar ko savaasathay ki bhaasha men haaipotenshan (hypotension) ke naam se jaanate hain। yoon to lo baladapareshar koi bimaari nahim hoti lekin yah sharir men panap rahi amay gnbhir bimaari ka smket hoti hai। aise men jab kisi ke sharir mem rakata-paravaah saamaanay se kam ho jaata hai to use niman rakatachaap ya lo balad pareshar kahate hai। naaramal balad pareshar 120/80 hota hai। aise men dila, kidani, phephade aur dimaag nshik roop se ya poori tarah se kaam karama bhi bnd kar sakate hain। Symptoms: - nkhon ke aage ndhera chhaana - ulati aur daayariya - garadan ka akad jaana - chakakar aana - chhaati men darada, sns phoolana - haathom aur pairon ka thnda hona - haृday men misad bitas mahasoos ki jaati hai Reasons: balad pareshar kam hone ke kaaran (causes of low blood pressure) 1. dil ki bimaari (heart disease)- baladapareshar kam hona dil ki gmbhir bimaari se juda hota hai, dil ki bimaari se haarat ki mnsapeshiyn kamajor ho jaati haim, jisase haarat parayaapat khoon ko pamap nahin kar paata aur hamaara bipi lo rahane lagata hai। dil ke marijon aur enimiya ke rogi lo bipi ko lekar saavadhaan rahen। 2. aarathosatetik haaiparatenshan taaip (arthostetic hypertension type)- isamen marij ko khade hone par chakakar aate hain, kayonki usaka balad pareshar ekadam se 20 paॉint niche a jaata hai। yah naravas sisatam par aadhaarit hota hai। lekim kai baar davaaon ke saaid iphekat se ya elaraji se bhi ho sakati hai। 3. khoon ki kami tatha anay ka (less blood and other reason)- sharir ke ndarooni ngon se khoon bah jaane ya khoon ki kami se, khaane men paushatikata ki kami ya aniyamitata se, phephadon ke ataik se, haarat ka vaॉlav kharaab ho jaane se, lo bipi ho sakata hai। achaanak sadama lagane, koi bhayaavah daृshay dekhane ya khabar sumane se bhi lo bipi ho sakata hai। isake alaava (other reason & causes of low blood pressure) - garabhaavasathaa, haaramon asntulan jaise ki thaayaraॉid ki sakariyata kam ho jaana - balad shugar davaaon ke parabhaav se - satarok tatha livar snbndhi bimaariyn - kuchh aavashayak vitaamin jaise bi12 aur aayaran ki kami Treatments: baladapareshar lo hai to kaya karen (some tips to prevent low blood pressure) - turnt baith ya let jaaen, mutathiyn bhinchen, bndhen, kholen, pair hilaayen। - namak aur chini vaala paami ya chaay pien। pairon ke niche do takie lagaakar leten। - jo log pahale se haai bipi ki dava kha rahe hain, ve dava khaana bnd kar den। - kam se kam aath gilaas paani aur anay pey roj pien। - bhojam men kaarabohaaidaret ki maatara kam kar den। - in sab ke alaava turanat daॉkatari salaah len। Home Remedies: - niman rakatachaap se pidit log namak jayaada khaaen - lagaataar chakakar a rahe hon, to paani jayaada pien - ek kap shakaraknd ka joos din men do baar piem - mitati ke baratan men raatabhar kishamish bhigaakar rakhen। subah kishamish chabaakar khaaen aur paani pi len - subah khaali pet tulasi ke patate ke ras men shahad milaakar khaaen - raat men baadaam bhigaakar rakhen, subah in baadaam ke chhilake utaarakar pis lem aur doodh ke saath ubaalen। is doodh ko gumaguna piem। Disease: saphed baala- gare heyar (Grey Hair) Description: saphed baala- gare heyar (Grey hair) umar ke saath baalon ka saphed hona paraakaृtik hai lekin kai baar kam umar men hi baal saphed hone lagate hain। aisa kai baar haaramonal gadbadi, badalati laaiphasataail aur paradooshan vaale maahaul ke kaaran bhi ho sakata hai। maujooda samay men tinej men hi bachachon ke baal saphed home lagate hain। Symptoms: - umar se pahale baal saphed ho jaana - baal naajuk hona - baal patale ho jaana - baalom ka tekasachar kharaab hona Reasons: kaarana- (Cause of Grey Hair) melaanin ke aadhaar par hi baalom ka rng kaalaa, saphed ya bhoora hota hai। jinake baalon men melaanim ki kami hoti hai unake baalon ka rng halaka hota hai jimake baalon men melaanim jayaada hota hai unake baal kaale hote hain। jin logom ke baal saphed ho jaate hain unake baalon men melaanin khatam ho jaata hai। melaanin pigament baalon ke phaॉlikal men rahata hai। kuchh maamalon men thaॉiraaida, animiya ya aanuvnshik kaaranon se bhi baal saphed ho sakate hain। baal safed hone ke anay kaaran (Other Reasons & Causes of Gray Hair) - vitaamin bi, aayaran aur kaॉpar tatha aayodin jaise tatavon ki kami se baal saphed hote hain। jin logon ke khaane men in minaral ki kami hoti hai unake baal samay se pahale saphed hone lagate hain। - aise vayakati jo bahut jayaada gusasail hote hain ya bahut jaladi tanaav men aate umake baal bhi jaladi saphed hone lagate hain। - kuchh vayakatiyon men umar se pahale baalon ka saphed hona aanuvmshik hota hai। - bahut lnbe samay tak kisi bimaari se pidit rahane ya jaladi jaladi bimaar padne vaale logon ke baal bhi umar se pahale saphed hone lagate haim। - baalon ki dekhabhaal thik parakaar se n ki jaae ya baalon ki saphaai ka dhayaan n rakha jaae to bhi baal umar se pahale saphed hone lagate hain। - bahut jayaada rasaayan vaale shainpoo ya baalon ke utapaad jaise ki heyar kalar ya jel aadi isatemaal karane vaale logon ke baal bhi jaladi saphed hone lagate hain। - bahut jayaada paradooshan vaale maahaul ya dhoop mem rahane se bhi baalon ka rng udne lagata hai। Treatments: baalon ko kaala karane ke lie upachaar (Tips & Remedies to prevent gray hair) - kachache papite ka pesat sir par takaribam 10 minat lagaakar rakhen। aisa karane se kuchh hi dinon mem baalon ka jhadna rookega saath hi baal kaale bhi honge। itana hi nahin baalon se dendaraph bhi khatam hogaa। - baal dhone ke lie kemikal shainpoo ka isatemaal bnd karen, isaki jagah besan aur doodh ya dahi ka isatemaal karen। aisa karane se baalom ka paraakaृtik rng bana rahegaa। - baal dhone ke lie mvala paaudar aur ninboo ka isatemaal karen। shikaakaai aur ritha milaakar ghar par hi shainpoo bhi banaaya ja sakata hai। - sir men laal payaaj ko pisakar usaka ras lagaaen। aisa karane se bhi saphed baal kaale hone lagate hain saath hi baalon ka jhadna bhi bnd ho jaata hai। - dahi mem kaali mirach aur ninboo ka ras milaakar sir ki tavacha aur baalon par lagaaem। takariban aadhe ghnte baad baal dho den, aisa karane se baal kaale hone lagenge। - desi ghi bhi saphed baalon ko kaala karane ka saral upaay hai। tel ki jagah desi ghi se baalon ki masaaj karen। - mvale ka parayog khaane men bhi karen। nvala khaane se bhi baal kaale hote hain। Home Remedies: aajakal umar se pahale hi baalon ka pakana ya saphed hona aam samasaya banati ja rahi hai। baalon ki thik se dekhabhaal n ho paane aur paradooshan ke kaarana, hamaare baal asamay hi saphed ho jaate hain। baalon ko kalar karana is samasaya ka koi upachaar nahim hai lekin kuchh ghareloo upachaar aajamaakar aap apane baalon ko saphed hone se rok sakate hain। jaanie saphed baalon ko kaala karane ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Grey Hair) 1. payaaj ka ras (Onion juice)- kuchh dinon taka, nahaane se 1/2 ghnta pahale rojaana sir mem payaaj ka pesat lagaaen। isase baal kaale home lagenge। 2. kachacha papita (Raw papaya)- sapataah men kam se kam 3 din das minat tak kachache papite ka pesat sir men lagaaen। isase baal nahin jhadenge aur kaale bhi hone lagenge। 3. naariyal tel (Coconut oil)- bhaृngaraaj aur ashavagndha ki jaden baalon ke lie varadaan maani jaati hain। inaka pesat naariyal ke tel ke saath baalon ki jadon men lagaaen aur 1 ghnte baad gunagune paani se achachhi tarah se baal dho len। isase bhi baal kaale hote haim। 4. ninboo ka ras (Lemon jiuce)- ninboo ke ras men nvala paaudar milaakar use sir par lagaane se bhi saphed baal kaale ho jaate hain। 5. desi ghi (Desi ghee)- paratidin shudadh ghi se sir ki maalish karane se bhi saphed baal kaale hote hain। 6. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ko kadadookas kar shahad men mila len। ise baalon par kam se kam sapataah men do baar niyamit roop se lagaaen। baalon ka safed hona kam ho jaaegaa। 7. jaitoon ka tel (Olive oil)- jaitoon ke tel ko halaka garam karen। isamen 4 garaam kapoor milaakar is tel se maalish karem। isaki maalish se kuchh hi samay men roosi khatam ho jaaegi aur baal bhi kaale rahenge। 8. nvala (Aamla)- nvale ke paaudar men ninboo ka ras milaakar use niyamit roop se lagaaen। shainpoo ke baad nvala paaudar paani men gholakar lagaane se bhi baalon ki kndishaning hoti hai, aur baal bhi kaale hote hain। nvala kisi na kisi rup me sevan bhi avashay karate rahen। 9. til ka tel (Sesame oil)- saradiyon mem til adhik se adhik khaaen। til ka tel bhi baalon ko kaala karane men madad karata hai। 10. kaali mirach (Black pepper)- aadha kap dahi men chutaki bhar kaali mirach aur chamamach bhar nimboo ras milaakar baalon men lagaae। 15 minat baad baal dho len। saphed baal phir se kaale hone lagenge। 11. menhadi (Henma)- lohe ki kadaahi men ek katori mehmdi paaudara, do bade chamamach chaay ka paani, do chamamach nvala paaudara, ek chamamach ninboo ka rasa, do chamamach dahi, shikaakaai v ritha paaudara, ek nda (agar aap lena chaahen to), aadha chamamach naariyal tel v thodaa-sa katatha daalakar raat ko bhigo den। ise subah baalon men lagaaen, phir do ghnte baad dho len। isase baal bima kisi nukasaam ke kaale ho jaaenge। aisa maah men kam se kam ek baar avashay karen। Disease: hadadi pharaikachar ya hadadi ka khisakana (Bone Fracture Or Dislocation) Description: hadadi pharaikachar ya hadadi ka khisakana (Bone fracture or dislocation) pharaikachar (Fracture)- hadadi ka tootama hi hadadi ka pharaikachar kahalaata hai। hadadi kai kaaramon se toot sakati hai, kahin girane se, takakar lagane se, jhataka lagane se ya achaanak se dabaav padne para। hadadi ka khisakana (Dislocation of bome) - do hadadiyn jab jude hue sathaan se khisak jaati hain to ise disalokeshan ya hadadi ka khisakama kahate hain। do hadadiyn ek jod par jaakar milati hain, lekin is jod par chot lagane ke kaaran isi jod se hadadiyn khisak jaati hain। hadadiyon ke khisakane par bhi bahut darad hota hai aur snbndhit sathaan par soojan a jaati hai। Symptoms: - asahaniy tarah se darad hona - aasa-paas ki tntarikaaon men kashati ke kaaran akadn - pharaikachar ki jagah par soojan a jaana - pharaikachar ke aasa-paas ke utakon men asathirata - pharaikachar vaale sathaan ka poori tarah se kaam bnd kar dena - behosh hona Reasons: kaarana- (Causes of bome frtacture or dislocation) pharaikachar ke kai kaaran ho sakate hain। hadadiyon ke kamajor hone ya hadadiyon se smbmdhit kainsara, sisata, ऑsatiyoporosis aadi hone se। pharaikachar ke baad hadadi men darad ke bhi kai kaaran ho sakate hain- - hadadiyon ke aasa-paas ke narav edingasa, jo hadadi ke tootane par sakariy hokar dimaag ko darad ka smket dete hain। - hadadiyn tootane se rakatasataraav ka hona aur soojan aanaa, jisase darad hota hai। - pharaikachar hone par mnsapeshiyn sikud kar hadadi ko bachaame ki koshish karati haim, yah bhi darad ka kaaran hota hai। - aisi koi duraghatama hone par jisase hadadiyn parabhaavit hon। - hadadiyom ka pharaikachar vayakati ki umar par bhi nirabhar karata hai kayonki jayaada umar men pharaikachar ke chnses barh jaate hain। kuchh sathitiyon men asahaniy darad bhi ho sakata hai jaise- - snkaramam hone par - galat tarike se palaasatar lagaane para, bahut dhila ya bahut taait Treatments: upachaara- (Tips to prevent bone fracture or dislocation) - pharaikachar vaali jagah ki baraph se sikaai karen। soojan kam hogi aur darad se aaraam milegaa। - pidit vayakati ko poori tarah aaraam karana chaahie। snbhav ho to snbmdhit jagah ko hilaane-dulaane se bachen। - garam sikaai karane se bhi aaraam milata hai। - yadi haath ya pair ki hadadi tooti ho to use unchaai par karake rakhem। - pharaikachar vaale sathaan ke aasa-paas ki jagah par maalish karen। - aadha anaanaas roj khaaen। - red mit khaane se bachen। - parijaravetiv khaana n khaaen। saavadhaaniyn- (Precautions) - kaar men baithakar hamesha sit belat pahamen। - koi khel khelate samay ya saaikil aur motarasaaikil chalaate samaya, snbndhit sephati upakaran jaroor pahanen। - yadi kisi ko ऑsatiporosis hai, to niyamit vayaayaam karen aur hadadiyon ko majaboot karane vaali daait len। Disease: chikan paॉkasa- chechak (Chickenpox) Description: chikan paॉkasa- chechak (Chickenpox) chechak ek vaayaral snkaraman (viral infection) hai jisase sharir par chhaale ki tarah daane banate haim aur umamen khujali (itching) hoti hai। chechak aise logon ko jayaada hota hai jo bimaar n padte hon ya jinahonne chechak se bachane ke lie tikaakaran n karavaaya ho। pahale ke samay mem yuva hone tak har koi chechak rog se ek m ek baar jaroor parabhaavit hota tha lekin aaj ke samay men is tarah ke rogon men kami aai hai। jayaadaatar logon ke lie, chechak ek halaki bimaari hai। phir bhi, yah tika lagaaya jaana behatar hai। chechak ke tike chechak aur usaki snbhaavit jatilataaon ko rokane ke lie ek surakashit aur parabhaavi tarika hai। Symptoms: - thakaan (kamajori) mahasoos hona - bukhaara, siradarad - bhookh men kami - sharir par laala-gulaabi, chhote daamon ka ubharana Reasons: kin logon ko hota hai adhik khataraa? (Risk Factors of Chicken Pox) chechak atayadhik smkaramit hoti hai, aur yah teji se phail sakati hai। vaayaras ke daane ke saath sidhe snparak men aane se ya khnsane ya chhinkane se hava men baikatiriya phailame se doosaron ko ho sakati hai। chechak (chechak) ka khatara tab aur adhik hota hai jaba: - kisi ko kabhi chechak n hui ho। - chechak ke lie tikaakaran n karavaaya ho। - bachache jo sakool ya haॉsatal mem snkaraman se parabhaavit hue hon। Treatments: upachaar (Treatments of Chicken Pox) - ek chamamach beking soda (bakimg soda) ko ek gilaas paani men gholakara, is paani ko rooi ki sahaayata se sharir par lagaaen। chechak se nijaat milegi। - chechak ke dauraan hone vaali khujali se bachane ke lie otamil (oatmeal) ko paani men daalakar nahaaen। - chechak (chechak) se hone vaali khujali se bachane ke lie kailaamaain loshan (calamime lotion) ko daanon ke upar lagaaen। - din men do se tin baar parabhaavit sathaan par shahad lagaaen। - chechak ko jaladi thik karane ke lie gaajar aur hare dhaniya ka soop banaakar pien। - chndan ke tel men rooi bhigaakara, parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen। - hari matar ko ubaalakar usaka pesat banaakara, daanon par lagaaen, aaraam milegaa। - elovera ka taaja ras nikaalakar daanon par lagaaem। tipas (Tips for Chicken Pox) - yadi chechak ke saath bukhaar bhi hai to khoob pey padaarath piem। paami, joos aur soop samay samay par lete rahen। yadi bachacha snkaramit mn ka doodh pita ho, to mn ko doodh nahin pilaana chaahie। - daanon ko n khujalaaen aur haathon ke naakhoon chhote rakhen। raat mem sote samay khujalaane se bachane ke lie haathon par galavas (gloves) pahanen। - khujali se bachame ke lie sharir ko thnda rakhen। halake kapade pahanen aur garam paani se nahaane se bachen। - is baat ka bhi dhayaam rakhen ki snkaraman ghar ke doosarom sadasayon tak n phaile। snkaramit vayakati ke kapade, bisatar aadi door rakhen aur unahen ghar ke anay sadasayon ke kapadon se alag hi dhoen। Home Remedies: sharir men teji se khujali honaa, laal daane nikal aana chikan paॉkas ya chechak (Chicken pox) ke paramukh lakashan hain। 1 varash se lekar 10 varash tak ke bachachon men chikan paॉkas ka khatara jayaada hota hai। khaana-paan mem hui aniyamitata chikan paॉkas ke phailane ka paramukh kaaran hoti hai। is dauraan maakhoon se chakataton ko hataane ki koshish nahin karani chaahie, aisa karane se yah phailata hai। chechak (Chechak) ke samay khaana-paan ka uchit dhayaan rakhana chaahie। masaaledaar aur ऑyali khaana khaane se bachen। chikanapaॉkas ke kisi marij ko kabhi esaparin nahin deni chaahie। isase usaki haalat kharaab ho sakati hai। chikan paॉkas hone par baahar aur bhid vaali jagah par jaane se parahej karen। ho sake to is dauraan logon se door rahen। jaanie chikan paॉkas se bachaav ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home Remedies for Chicken pox) miman upachaaron ko apanaakar is bimaari se raahat paai ja sakati hai: 1. jai ka aata (Oat Flour)- chikam paॉkas home par sharir men bahut tej khujali hoti hai। khujali se bachane ke lie jai ke aate ko paani men milaakar sanaan karana chaahie। 2 litar paani men 2 kap jai ka aata milaakar lagabhag 15 minat tak ubaalen, pake aate ko ek kaॉtan ke baig mem achachhi tarah se bndhakar baॉth tab men daalakar nahaaem। 2. bhoora siraka (Brown Vinegar)- aadha kap bhoore sirake ko paani men daalakar nahaane se sharir men ho rahi khujali se nijaat paayi ja sakati hai। isase daamon ki soojam kam hoti hai aur daane sookhane bhi lagate hain। 3. nimboo ka ras (Lemon Juice)- ninboo ka ras pine se chikan paॉkas men raahat milati hai। upachaar ke lie samay samay par ek gilaas saaph paani men ninboo nichodkar pite rahen। 4. nim ki patatiyn (Margos Leaves)- mim ki patatiyon ko garam paani men daalakar nahaane se khujali samaapat hoti hai। nim paraakaृtik roop se enti baikatiriyal gunon se bharapoor hota hai। aise men chikan paॉkas thik karane men behad phaayademmd hai। 5. beking soda (Baking Soda)- aadha chamamach beking soda ko ek gilaas gunagune paami men milaaen aur is lep ko poore sharir par lagaakar sookhane den। isase chikanapaॉkas jalad thik ho jaata hai। 6. seb ka siraka (Apple Cider Vinegar)- aadha kap seb ke sirake ko halake garam paani mem milaakar nahaane se raahat milati hai। is paani men takariban 20 minat tak jaroor baithen। 7. vitaamin i tel (Vitamin E Oil)- vitaamina-i yukat tel ko sharir par lagaane se chikan paॉkas ke dauraan hone vaali khujali se raahat milati hai। 8. gaajar (Carrot)- ubale gaajar aur dhaniya khaane se chikan paॉkas se aai kamajori kam hoti hai। gaajar aur dhaniya ka soop banaakar pime se raahat milati hai। 9. harabal chaay (Herbal Tea)- tulasi, genda aur kaimomaail ko milaakar chaay banaaie phir usamen shahad ya minboo milaakar pijie। is chaay ko din men 3-4 baar pine se raahat milati hai। 10. hari matar (Green Pea)- hari matar ko paani men pakaakar isake paani ko sharir men lagaaie, isase chikan paॉkas ke laal chakatate samaapat hote hain। 11. adarak (Ginger)- baath tab mem thmda paani len aur usamen adarak daalakar tis minat tak chhod den। usake baad is paami men baith jaaen। isase chikanapaॉkas ke dauraan hone vaali khujali men aaraam milata hai। Disease: haija (Cholera) Description: haija (Cholera) haija ek snkaraamak bimaari (infectious disease) hai, jo nton ko parabhaavit karati hai aur jisamen paani ki tarah patale dasat lag jaate hain। haija ka ilaaj samay rahate m kiya jaae to vayakati men paani ki kami (dehydration) ho jaati hai, jisase vayakati ki maut bhi ho sakati hai। haija dooshit paami pine ya dooshit khaana khaane ke kaaran phailata hai। aisa paani ya khaana jisamen vaaibariyo koleri baikatiriya (vibrio cholerae becteria) maujood ho, haija ka kaaran banata hai। haija (Haija) aisi jagah par jayaada phailata hai jahn, saaph saphaai ka abhaav ho, sivarayukat paami ki sapalaai ho, saaga-sabaji sivar ke paani men ugaai ja rahi hon ya kisi ka ghar naale aadi ke paas sathit ho। haijaa, bachachon se lekar bujuragom taka, kisi men bhi ho sakata hai। garabhavati mahilaaon tatha bachachon men bhi is rog ke hone ki aashmka jayaada rahati hai kayonki unaki paratirodhak kashamata kam hoti hai। haija men vayakati ke sharir se paani ke saath kai jaroori lavana, sodiyam aur poteshiyam aadi bhi nikal jaate hain, jisase vayakati ke sharir ka rakat amaliy ho jaata hai aur vayakati ki maृtayu ho jaati hai। Symptoms: - dasat ekadam patale aur chaaval ke paani jaise hona - dasat ke saath ulatiyn hona - parabhaavit vayakati ko atayadhik payaas lagana - parabhaavit vayakati ko peshaab kam aana - sharir ki mns peshiyon men ainthan hona Reasons: haija ka kaaran (Causes of Choler in Himdi) 1- dooshit paani, bhojana, phal ya doodh aadi ka parayog karane se। 2- rogi vayakati ke snparak men rahane se, masalana, usake saath khaane, uthane-baithane, usake davaara isatemaal kie gae kapade pahanane, usake davaara isatemaal kie gae kisi bhi saamaan ko isatemaal karane se। 3- makakhiyn bhi haija (Haija) phailane ka bada kaaram hain। khule men ki gai shauch ya gndagi par baithakar makakhiyn baikatiriya lekar doosari jagahon par phaila deti haim, jisase haija phailata hai। 4- khaame ko bina dhake rakhanaa, aur use khaanaa। 5- paani ko bina dhake rakhanaa। 6- kachacha ya adhapaka bhojana, khaasakar mns khaanaa। Treatments: upachaar (Treatment of Cholera) haija ka ilaaj karane se pahale rogi ko saapha-saphaai ka vishesh dhayaan rakhana haahie। haija akasar Description: inaphalooenja (Influenza) inaphalooenja ko saadhaaran bhaasha mem phaloo (flu) ke naam se jaana jaata hai, jisamen shavasan tntar men snkaraman (infection in respiratory system) ho jaata hai। is tarah ka phaloo adhikatar saradiyon ke mausam men vaayaral bimaari ke roop men hota hai। yah un logon ko jayaada parabhaavit karata hai jinaki rog paratirodhak kashamata kisi bimaari ke kaaran lagaaya jaata hain, vayakati khud ko khud hi phaloo ke jivaanu se snkaramit karata hai। phaloo tin parakaar ka hota hai, e, bi aur si। taaip e aur bi vaarashik inaphalooenja ka kaaran hote hain jisase lagabhag 20 phisadi log parabhaavit hote hain। taaip e men echa1ena1, echa2ena2 aur echa3ena3 shaamil hain। taaip e ke inphalooenja men parivaratan hota hai jisase parabhaavit vayakati ko parayaapat imayooniti nahin mil paati। taaip si bhi phaloo ke lakashan darashaata hai lekin is tarah ka phaloo kam hota hai। haalnki tinon tarah ka phaloo ek hi tarah se phailata hai aur inake lakashan bhi ek jaise hi hote hain। jatilataaen- (Complications during influenza) - yuvaa, bachachom tatha 65 ki umar se adhik ke bujuragom men jatilata ho sakati hai। - garabhavati mahilaaon ko bhi phaloo ka khatara jayaada rahata hai। - inphalooenja se nimoniyaa, kaan men snkaramana, saainas smkaraman aur baronkaaitis ka khatara barh jaata hai। - yadi uchach shareni ka phaloo ho to, entivaayaral davaaen upayukat gaarhaapan haarad hogaa, to aise palaॉk ko satebal kaha jaata hai aur yadi yah mulaayam hoga to ise tode jaane ke anukool maana jaata hai, aur ise anasatebal palaॉk kaha jaata hai। satebal palaॉk (Stable Plaque):- satebal palaॉk se rookaavat ki maatara se koi pharak nahin padtaa, m hi isase gnbhir haarat ataik hota hai। is tarah ka palaॉk dhire dhire barhata hai, aise men rakat paravaah ko nai aaratarij (artries) ka raasata dhoondhane ka mauka mil jaata hai, jise koletaral vesel (collateral vessal) kahate hain। ye vesel balaॉk ho chuki aaratari ko baaipaas kar deti hain aur dil ki mnsapeshiyon tak aavashayak rakat aur ऑkasijan pahunchaati hain। anasatebal palaॉk (Unstable Plaque):- asathaai palaॉk men, palaॉk ke tootame para, ek khataranaak thakaka ban jaata hai, aur koletaral ko vikasit hone ka poora samay nahim mil paata hai। vayakati ki mnsapeshiyn (muscle) gnbhir roop se daimej ho jaati hain aur vah kai baar sadan kaaradiek deth (sudden cardiac death) ka shikaar ho bachaayen। - haृday ko savasath rakhane ke lie dinacharaya men vayaayaam ko shaamil karana behad jaroori hai। - aisa bhojam karen, jisase haृday ko laabh ho। - haृday ko savasath rakhane ke lie sharir ka vajan niyntarit rakhen। - roj aadha ghnta paidal chalen। - liphat ki jagaha, sirhiyon ka isatemaal karen। Home Remedies: haarat balaॉkej ke ghareloo upachaara- (home remedies for heart blockage) ek kap doodh men lahasun ki tin se chaar kali daalakar ubaalen। is doodh ko roj pien। ek gilaas doodh men haladi daalakar ubaalen aur gunaguna rahane par shahad daalakar pien। ek gilaas gunagune paani ka isatemaal karen। Disease: kaan men snkaraman (Ear Infection) Description: kaan men snkaraman (Ear Infection ) kaan sharir ke sabase mahatavapooran aur smvedanashil ngon men se ek hain। sharir ka (Treatment of Ear Infectiom in Hindi) kaan ke snkaraman se bachane ke lie sabase jaroori hai saapha-saphaai ka vishesh dhayaan rakhanaa। isake atirikat kuchh miman baaten par amal kar bhi kaanom ke ras nikaalakar kaan ke aas paas malane se bhi aaraam hota hai। dhayaan rahe ras ko kaan ke ndar nahim daalana hai। 5- seb ke sirake men baraabar maatara men paami milaakar rooi ko usamen bhigaaen। is use mikasi men pisakar ras nikaal len। payaaj ke ras ki kuchh boonde kaan men daalen। Disease: daayabitik retinopaithi (Diabetic Retinopathy) Description: daayabitik retinopaithi (Diabetic retinopathy) daayabitik retimopaithi ek bimaari hai, jo madhumeh (diabeties) se pidit vayakati ki retina (mkh ka parada jahm tasavir banati hai) ko parabhaavit karati hai। yah retina ko rakat Diabetic Retinopathy) madhumeh (Diabetes), yadi bahut lnbe samay tak rah jaae to yah sharir ke doosare ngon ko bhi parabhaavit karata hai aur yah parabhaavit ng nkhen bhi ho sakati hain। daayabitiz rakat vaahikaaom ki divaar ko parabhaavit karata hai, jisase retina (jisapar chhavi banati hai) tak ऑkasijan le jaane vaali naadiyn kamazor ho jaati hain। daayabitiz ke marizon men agar shugar ki maatara niyntarit nahin rahati, to vah daayabitik retinopaithi ki samasaya se garasat ho sakate hain। is samasaya ka pata tab chalata hai jab yah bimaari gnbhir roop le leti hai। mdhepan ka ek paramukh kaaran hai ‘daayabitik retinopaithi’ bhi hai। daayabitik retinopaithi ke do mukhay charan hote hain। shurooaati charan ko naan parolipheretiv daayabitik retinopaithi (enapidiaara) kahate hain। is charan men retina kashetar ki malikaaen kashatigarasat ho jaati hain। saamaanayat bimaari ka yah shurooaati charan hota hai, jisamen lakashanon ka pata mahin chalata hai। kuchh maamalon men kashatigarasat rakat nalikaaon ke phatane se retina ke madhay bhaag mem rakat fail jaata hai। is sathiti ko daayabitik maikayulopaithi kahate hain, isase daृshati parabhaavit hoti hai aur dhundhala dikhane lagata hai। isake umanat aur vikasit charan ko parolipheretiv daayabitik retinopaithi (pidiaara) kahate hain। yah daayabitik retinopaithi ki sabase sabase gnbhir charan hai। is charan men retina kashetar men kamazor avmchhaniy rakat malikaaen tezi se panapane lagati hain jo retina ki ऑkasijan aapoorati men baadha paida kar use kashatigarasat karati hain। is kaaran retinal ditechamemt ya galookoma bhi ho sakata hai। karib 20 phisadi madhumeh piditon men pidiaar ki vajah se gnbhir daृshati dosh ho sakata hai jo ndhepan ka kaaran banaata hai। Treatments: surakasha ke lie kuchh tipas (Tips to prevemt diabetic retinopathy) - samaya- samay par nkhon ki jnch karaayen, yah jnch bachachon men bhi aavashayak hai। - rakat men kaॉlesatarol aur shugar ki maatara ko niyntarit rakhen। - agar hone ke das saal baad har tin mahine par nkhon ki jnch karaayen। - garabhavati mahila agar daayabitik hai to chikitasak se snparak karen। saamaamay upachaar (Treatment for diabetic retinopathy) - Description: galookoma (Glaucoma) galookomaa, kaala motiya ya knch bindu roga, tntar men gnbhir evn nirntar kashati karate hue dhire-dhire daृshati ko samaapat hi kar deta hai। kisi vasatu se parakaash ki kiranen nkhon tak pahunchati haim, v usaki chhavi daृshati patal (Retina) par banaati hai। retina se yah soochana vidayut tarngom davaara masatishak tak netar tmtuon davaara pahunchaai jaati hai। nkh men ek taral padaarath bhara hota hai yah taral padaarath mkh ke gole ko chikana kie rahata hai yadi is taral padaarath ka risaav ruk jaae to nkh ke ndar ka daab barh jaata hai। galookoma men ntar metar par daaba, parabhaavit nkhon ki daab sahane ki kashamata se adhik ho jaata hai, isake parimaamasavaroop netar tntu ko kashati pahunchati hai, jisase daृshati chali jaati hai। kisi vasatu ko dekhate samay galookoma se garasit vayakati ko keval vasatu ka kendar dikhaai deta hai। samay ke saath sathiti bad se badatar hoti jaati hai। saamaanayata: log is par bahut kam hi dhayaan dete hain, lekin jab dhayaan dete hain tab tak bahut der ho chuki hoti hai। saamaanay taur par yah rog bina kisi lakashan ke vikasit hota hai v domon nkhon ko ek saath parabhaavit karata hai। haalmki yah rog 40 varash se adhik aayu ke vayasakon ke bich paaya jaata hai, phir bhi kuchh maamalon men yah navajaat shishuon ko bhi parabhaavit kar sakata hai। madhumeha, aanuvmshikataa, uchach rakatachaap v haृday rog is rog ke paramukh kaaranon men se hain। vishav satar par kaala motiya lagabhag chhah karod logon ko parabhaavit karata hai aur bhaarat men yah ndhatav ka doosara sabase kaaran hai। Symptoms: - tayoobalaait ya balab ki roshani chaaron or se dhundhali dikhane lagati hai, nkhon men tej darad bhi hone lagata hai। - dhundhalaapana, kai rogiyon ko raat men dikhana bhi bnd ho jaata hai - mitali ya ulati hona - siradarad Reasoms: galookoma ke kaaran (Causes of Glaucoma) maanav nkh men sathit kaaraniya ke pichhe nkhon ko sahi aakaar aur poshan dene vaala taral padaarath (Aqueous Humor Fluid) hota hai, lens ke chaaron or sathit siliyari utatak is taral padaarath ko lagaataar banaate rahate hain yah taral padaarath putaliyon ke davaara nkhon ke bhitari hisase mem jaata hai is tarah se nkhon men is taral padaarath ka banana aur bahana lagaataar hota rahata hai। savasath nkhon ke lie yah aavashayak hai nkhon ke bhitari hisase men kitana dabaav rahe yah taral padaarath ki maatar par nirabhar rahata hai। galookoma rogiyon ki nkhon men is taral padaarath ka dabaav atayadhik barh jaata hai kabhi-kabhi nkhon ki bahaav nalikaaon ka maarag rook jaata hai, lekim siliyari utak ise lagaataar banaate hi jaate hain, aise men jab mkhon men daृshati-tntu ke upar taral ka dabaav achaanak barh jaata hai to galookoma ho jaata hai। yadi nkhon men taral ka itana hi dabaav lnbe samay tak bana rahata hai to isase nkhon ke tntu bhi nashat ho sakate hain। samay rahate yadi is bimaari ka ilaaj nahin karaaya jaata hai to isase daृshati poori tarah ja sakati hai। Treatments: saamaanay upachaar (Treatment and tips to prevemt Glaucoma) - khaane men paalak jayaada khaaen - vitaamin e nkhon ke savaasathay ke lie behad jaroori hai। aise khaaday padaarath khaaen jinase vitaamin e ki poorati ho। - saunph bhi savasath nkhon ke lie achachha ghareloo nusakha hai। Disease: bavaasir (Piles) Description: bavaasir (Piles) ek asaadhay rog hai। ise hemorahoyadas (Haemorrhoids), paailas ya moolavayaadhi bhi kahate hain। bavaasir ko aayuraved men arash yaani diraghakaalin paraanaghaatak bimaari kaha jaata hai। bavaasir men nt ke ntim hisase ya malaashay (gudaa) ki bhitari (Causes of Piles) khooni ho ya baadi donon hi bavaasir (Piles) ke lie jo kaarak jimamevaar hote hain vo lagabhag ek hi hain। bavaasir ke kuchh aham kaaran niman hain: kabaj (Constipation) bavaasir ki phail jaati hain। jisake kaaran vayakati ko bavaasir (Haemorrhoids) ho jaati hai। talaa-bhuna hua bhojan (Fried and roasted food) jayaada miracha- masaale, tali hui aur chatapati chijen khaame, mmsa, ndaa, rabaṛi, mithaai, malaai jaise der se pachane vaale bhojan karane se bhi bavaasir rog hota hai। aavashayakata se adhik bhojan karana bhi bavaasir ka paramukh kaaran hai। garam paani (Hot water) shauch karane ke baad maladavaar ko garam paani se dhone se bhi bavaasir rog ho sakata hai। davaaiyn (Medications) davaaiyon ka adhik sevan karane ke kaaran bhi bavaasir (Bawasir) rog ho sakata hai। ko hataane ke lie bhi kai vidhiyn upalabadh hai। masason men injekashan davaara aisi dava ka paravesh kiya jaata hai jisase masase sookh jaate hain। - masason par ek vishesh upakaran davaara rabar ke for Piles mooli ka niyamit sevan bavaasir ko thik kar deta hai। raat ko sote samay kele khaane chaahie isase rogi ko bahut adhik laabh milata hai। paalaka, bathuaa, patata gobhi, chaulaai, soyaa, (Eye Imfection) nkhon men inphekashan haanikaarak sookasham jivaanu baikatiriya aur vaayaras ke kaaran hota hai। ye haamikaarak sookasham jivaanu maamasoon ke mahine men sabase jayaada sakariy hote hain। ye mkhon ki upari bhaaga, putali, kaॉramiya aur palakon par aakaraman karate hain jisase nkhon men soojana, jalam hoti hai। nkh jarurat se jayaada laal ho jaati hai aur nkhon se jarurat se jayaada paani ka disachaaraj hone lagata hai। Symptoms: - nkhon se paani nikalana - nkhon se mavaad nikalana - dhundhala vijan - mkhon ka sookh jaana - palakon par soojan - nkhon men khoojalaahat - nkhon men darad aur jalan - nkhe laal hona Reasons: nkhon ke inphekashan ke kaaran (Causes and Reasons of Eye Infection) nkhon ke inphekashan se sabase jayaada nkhon ki palaken parabhaavit hoti hai। palakon ke ndaruni hisase men soojan hone se nkhom ki sundarata to khatam hoti hi hai, samay par ilaaj nahin karaane se ghaav hone ka bhi khatara rahata hai। inphekashan jab nkhon ke ndar nsoo ki garnthi ko parabhaavit karata hai to soojan se nsoo ki garnthi bnd ho jaati hai aur yah kaaphi darad karane lagata hai। sabase jayaada gnbhir sathiti tab hoti hai jab inphekashan kaॉraniya ko parabhaavit karati hai। isamen kaॉraniyal alasar ka khatara rahata hai aur nkhon ki roshani tak chali jaati hai। knjekativaaitis (Conjunctivitis)- knjekativaaitis nkhon ka sabase kaॉman inphekashan hai jise pink aai bhi kahate hain। yah ek vaayaral imphekashan hai jo kaaphi teji se phailata hai। agar mn ko isaka inphekashan hai to navajaat ko bhi yah inphekashan ho sakata hai। vaairal keraatitis (viral keratitis)- pink aai ki tarah yah bhi ek qaॉman aai inphekashan hai jo harapis ke vaayaras (Herpes simplex virus) ke kaaran hota hai। yah bhi kaaphi teji se phailata hai। phngal keraatitis (Fungal keratitis)- yah ek phngal inphekashan hai jo mkhon men kntekat lains lagaane se ho sakata hai। 2006 men yah inphekashan us samay characha men aaya tha jab ek khaas tarah ke kntekat lains solayooshan ke isatemaal se kaaphi log is inphekashan ke shikaar ho gae the। vaise nkhon men phmgal inphekashan kisi bhi tarah ke chot se ya phir ऑragenik maitar ke jaane se hota hai। taraakoma (Trachoma)- yah inphekashan kaaphi gnbhir hota hai aur gamadi jagah men teji se phailata hai। gndagi par pamapane vaale makakhiyon aur kiṛon ke nkh men ghusane se yah inphekashan hota hai। taraakoma nkhon ke niche vaale palak ko snkaramit karata hai, agar yah lnbe samay tak raha to kaॉraniya tak men ghaav hone tak ka khatara rahata hai jisase marij hamesha ke lie mdha ho sakata hai। indophathelaamitis (Emdophthalmitis)- jab nkhon ka inphekashan nkh ke ndar kaaphi gahare tak asar daal deta hai to use indophathelaamitis kahate hain। yah vaayaral aur baikateriyal domon tarah ke smkaraman se hota hai। nkhom men gahari chot lagane se bhi isaka khatara rahata hai। Treatments: dekhabhaal aur ilaaj (Care and Treatmemt of Eye Infection) mkhon ke inphekashan ka ilaaj ab kaaphi saral aur aasaan ho gaya hai। entibaayotik aai daraॉpa, malaham aur senk se kai tarah ke snkaraman ka sahi tarike se ilaaj ho jaata hai। kai tarah ke vaayaral inphekashan kuchh dinom tak rahane ke baad khud hi thik ho jaata hai to gnbhir inphekashan hone par daॉkatar ko dikhaana jaroori hota hai। nkhon ki dekhabhaal ke saamaanay upachaara- (Tips to Prevemt Eye infection) -tariphala jal se mkhom ko dhote rahen, kaaphi kaam karegaa। -imali ke bij ko chndan ki tarah pisakar nkhon ki palakon par lep lagaane se kaaphi raahat milati hai। -subah uthate hi munh men thnda paani bharakar mumh phulaakar thnde jal se mkhon par chhinte maaren। aisa din men tin baar karen। yah nkhon ke inphekashan ke lie kaaphi asaradaar hai। -saphed payaaj ke ras men shahad aur karapoor milaakar shishi men rakh len aur ise raat mem sote samay nkhon men daalen। nkhon ke sabhi tarah ke inphekashan men yah kaaphi kaaragar ilaaj hai। -do ratati phitakari ko baarik pisakar gulaab jal men gholakar rakh len। is nechural aai daraॉp ki do-do boond din men tim baar nkhon men daalen। yah sabhi tarah ke inphekashan men kaaragar hota hai। nkh ka soojama, laali ko kam karata hai aur nkhon men kich aur mavaad ka aana bnd ho jaata hai। anay tipasa- (Other Tips to prevent Eye Infection) -jisaki nkhe laal hain unake saamane jaane se bachen। agar unake saamane gae hain to nkhon men nkh daal kar baat nahin karen। umase milane ke baad turnt nkhon saabun se haath dhoen aur phir nkhon ko thmde paani se dhoen। -knjekativaaitis (conjunctivitis) ke samay sakoola, ऑphis aur saaravajanik jagahon par enti vaairal sapare ka chhiṛakaav baara-baar karate rahana chaahie। -agar aap kntekat lains lagaate hain to apame nkhon ko chhoone se pahale haathom ko achachhe tarah se saaph kar len। -pidit vayakati se door rahen aur usaka tauliyaa, rumaala, beda, takiya ko hamesha enti-sepatik likavid se saapha-suthara rakhen। Home Remedies: nkh men hone vaala inphekashana, gnde haathon se nkh ko masalame se,
