ke ghareloo upaay (Home remedies for eye infection): 1. garam paani (Hot Water)- halake garam paani ke isatemaal se nkh ko dhoen, isase nkhon ke upar jamane vaali gndagi hat jaati hai। isake baad rui ki madad se nkhon ko pochhen। 2. gulaab jal (Rose Water)- gulaab jal se nkh ko dhone se nkhon ka inphekashan kam ho jaata hai। do boond gulaab jal nkhon men daalen। is upaay ko rojaana din men do baar karen। 3. paalak aur gaajar ka ras (Spinach & Carrot Juice)- paalak aur gaajar ka ras nkhom ke snkaraman ke lie kaaphi laabhadaayak hota hai kayonki imame paae jaane vaale vitaamin nkhon ke lie kaaphi mahatavapooran hote haim। paalak ke 4 ya 5 pataton ko pisakar usaka ras nichod len। 2 gaajar ko bhi pisakar ras nikaal len। ek gilaas men aadha kap paami len aur usamen gaajar aur paalak ke ras ko mila kar pien। aisa rojaana karane se nkh ka snkaraman kam hone lagata hai। 4. nvale ka ras (Aaml juice)- nkhon men snkaraman hone par nvale ka ras pine se bahut laabh milata hai। 3 se 4 mvale ke phal ko pis kar usaka ras nikaal len। ek gilaas paani men us ras ko mila kar pien। nvale ke ras ko subah khaali pet aur raat mem sone se pahale din mem do baar isatemaal karen। kuchh hi dimon men nkhon ka inphekashan door ho jaaegaa। 5. shahad aur paani (Honey and Water)- shahad se nkhon ko dhona chaahie। isase nkhon ko behad laabh pahunchata hai। ek gilaas paani men 2 chamamach madhuras ko milaakar khuli nkhon men chhapake maaren। aisa karane se nkhon ka snkaramam door hoga aur nkhon ki gndagi bhi saaph hogi। 6. haladi aur garam paani (Turmeric and Water)- garam paani men haladi ko milaakar rui se nkhon ko ponchhana chaahie। haladi paraakaृtik roop se enti baikatiriyal aur enti sepatik gunon se bharapoor hoti hai। yah mkhon ki saphaai bhi karati hai aur snkaraman se bhi door rakhati hai। 7. aaloo (Potato)- aaloo men parachur maatara men sataarach hota hai, jisake isatemaal se nkhon ke snkaraman ko thik kiya ja sakata hai। aaloo ko patale- patale tukadon men kaat len। raat men sone se pahale us kate hue aaloo ko 15 minat tak apani nkhon ke upar laga kar rakhen aur baad use utaar den। Disease: piliya (Jaundice) Description: piliya (Jaundice) piliya ek aisa rog hai jo ek vishesh parakaar ke vaayaras aur kisi kaaranavash sharir men pitat yaani rakat men bilirubin (Bilirubim Disorder) ki maatara barh jaane se hota hai। isamen marij ko pila peshaab hota hai। usake maakhoona, tavacha aur nkhon ka saphed bhaag pila pad jaata hai aur marij ko kaaphi kamajori, kabaja, ji michalaanaa, siradarada, bhookh n lagana aadi shikaayat hone lagati hai। yah bahut hi sookasha‍m vishaanu (Virus) se hota hai। shuroo men jab rog dhimi gati se v maamooli hota hai tab isake lakashan dikhaai nahin paṛate hain, lekin jab yah gnbhir ho jaata hai to marij ki nkhe v naakhoon pile dikhaai dene lagate hain। jin vaayaras se yah hota hai usake aadhaar par mukha‍yath piliya tin parakaar ka hota hai (Types of Jaundice) vaayaral haipetaaitis e, vaayaral haipetaaitis bi tatha vaayaral haipetaaitis naॉm e v naॉn bi। sharir men esiditi ke baṛh jaame, kaaphi dinon tak maleriya rahane, pitat mali men pathari atakane, jayaada sharaab pine, adhik namak aur tikhe padaarathon ke sevan se aur khoon men rakatakanon ki kami hone se bhi piliya (Piliya) rog hota hai। Symptoms: - nkh ke saphed bhaag ka pila ho jaana - aamaashay men soojan hona - ji michalaana - tavacha ka rng pila ho jaana - daahini pasaliyon ke niche bhaaripam aana aur darad hona - pitat ke kaaran mal ka rng phika ya saphed ho jaana - pet men darad hona - bhookh nahin lagana - vajan lagaataar kam hona - shaam mem thakaa-thaka mahasoos karana aur 102 digari ke aasapaas bukhaar rahana Reasons: piliya rog ke kaaran (Causes and Reasons of Jaundice) jab sharir men laal rakat koshikaaen 120 din ke saaikil men ek mechural parakariya ke tahat tootati hai to vesat baai parodakat ke rup men bilirubin (Bilirubin Disorder) ka utapaadan hota hai। bilirubin ke jarie sharir ki saari gndagi livar se chhan kar baahar mikalati hai। yah gndagi peshaab aur mal ke jarie baahar nikalati hai। agar livar men snkaraman hai ya phir rakat men bilirubin ki maatara 2.5 se jayaada ho jaati hai to livar ke gndagi saaph karane ki parakariya avarudadh ho jaati hai aur isi parisathiti men piliya ki bimaari ho jaati hai। piliya rog ke anay kaaran (Other Reasons & Causes of Jaundice) agar kisi snkaraman se laal rakat koshika apani saamaanay parakariya se pahale hi tootame lagati hai to rakat men bilirubin ki maatara baṛhane lagati hai। is parisathiti ko pari hepatik jaॉnadis kahate hain। maleriyaa, sakil sel enimiyaa, thelisimiya men aur kai aanuvnshik kaaranon se bhi rakat men bilirubin ki maatara achaanak baṛhane lagati hai jisase piliya (Piliya) rog hota hai। agar kisi kaaran se livar ko mukasaan pahumcha hai to livar se bilirubin banane ki kashamata hi kam ho jaati hai। ise intaraa-hepaatik jaॉnadis bhi kaha jaata hai। vaayaral haipetaaitis (Viral Hepatitis), livar ka alakohalik hona (Alcohol), tej bukhaar (Fever), livar kainsar (Liver Cancer), galat davaaon ke sevan aur pairaasitaamol (Medicine Side effects) ke jayaada sevan se bhi intaraa-hepaatik jaॉnadis hote hain। motaapa men livar saairosis hone ka khatara rahata hai। jisase intaraa-hepaatik jaॉnadis ki snbhaavana rahati hai। gaॉl balaadar men patathara, painakariyaaj ka sahi dhng se kaam nahin karanaa, painakariyaaj kaimsar ya phir gaॉl balaadar ke kainsar men bhi livar davaara baai parodakat bilirubin ko sharir se nikaalane ki parakariya bnd ho jaati hai। matija rakat men bilirubin ki maatara kaaphi baṛh jaati hai aur gnbhir piliya rog ho jaata hai। Treatments: dekhabhaal aur ilaaj (Care and Treatment for Jaundice) - dihaaidareshan home par aai vi phalooyadas (IV fluids in case of dehydration) - enti baayotikas (amtibiotics) - enti vaayaral dava (amtiviral medicines) - balad tarnsaphayoojan (blood transfusions) - sateraॉyadas (steroids) - kimotherepi, rediesham therepi aur navajaat ke lie phototherepi (chemotherapy/radiation therapy & phototherapy for newborns) - doodh v paani ubaal kar pien। - taaja v saaph aur garam bhojan karen। - sa‍vacha‍chh shauchaalay ka hi parayog karen। - sirinj ko 20 minat tak ubaal kar hi lagavaaen। - pine ke lie hamesha savachachh aur baikatiriya rahit paani ka hi isatemaal karen। - khaana banaane, parosane, khaane se pahale v baad men aur shauch jaane ke baad men haath saabun se acha‍chhi tarah dhoma chaahie। - bhojan jaalidaar alamaari ya dhaka‍kan se dhak kar rakhana chaahie, taaki makakhiyon v dhool se bachaaya ja saken। - rogi bacha‍chon ko daॉka‍tar jab tak yah n bata dem ki ye rog muka‍t ho chooke hai sa‍kool ya baahar nahin jaane de। - raka‍t dene vaale va‍yakatiyon ki poori tarah jnch karane ke baad hi rakat len। agar rakat men bilirubin ki maatara jayaada hogi to aapako bhi piliya ho sakata hai। Home Remedies: piliya rog sookasham vishaanu ke kaaran hota hai। is rog ke hone par vayakati ke naakhun aur mkhen pili dikhaai deti hain। chikitasa ki bhaasha men piliya ko vaayaral haipetaaitis (Viral Hepatitis) kahate hain। piliya rog saapha-saphaai ke abhaav men ya dooshit paani aur bhojam ke sevan ke kaaran hota hai। piliya rog ke hone par vayakati ko bhookh n laganaa, bukhaar rahanaa, ji michalaanaa, sir mem darad honaa, peshaab ka pila aana tatha kamajori v thakaan laganaa, jaise lakashan najar aate hain। piliya hone par vayakati ka livar parabhaavit hota hai। yadi samay rahate piliya rog ka upachaar n kiya jaae to vayakati ki maृtayu bhi ho sakati hai। jaanen piliya se bachaav ke ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies for Jaundice) 1. tamaatar ka ras (Tomato juice)- piliya home par ek gilaas tamaatar ke ras men ek chutaki namak aur kaali mirach milaakar subah khaali pet piem। aaraam milegaa। 2. mooli ki patati (Radish leaves)- mooli ki patatiyon ko pisakara, usaka ras nikaalen। lagabhag aadha litar mooli ki patatiyon ka ras rojaama pien। das din ke bhitar rogi ko piliya se aaraam milegaa। 3. papite ki patati (Papay leaves)- ek chamamach papite ki patati ke pesat men ek chamamach shahad milaakara, rojaana takariban do haphaton tak khaaen। piliya ke upachaar ke lie yah behad phaayademnd ghareloo nusakha hai। 4. ganana (Sugarcane)- ganamaa, paachan kariya ko duroosat karata hai saath hi livar ko bhi behatar tarike se kaaray karame men madad karata hai। upachaar ke lie ek gilaas ganane ke ras men ninboo ka ras milaakar rojaana do baar pien। 5. tulasi ki patati (Basil leaves)- tulasi ki das se panadarah patati ka pesat banaakara, gaajar ke ras men mila len। is ras ko rojaanaa, do se tin haphaton tak pien। piliya rog se raahat milegi। 6. jau (Barley)- ek kap jau ko tim litar paani men achachhi tarah ubaal len aur tin ghnte tak dhak kar rakh den। is paani ko din men kai baar pien। 7. mimboo (Lemon)- ninboo livar ko kashatigarasat hone se bachaata hai। ek gilaas paani men do ninboo nichoden aur pien। 8. baadaam (Almond)- baadaam ki 8 giri, 2 khajoor aur 5 ilaayachi ko paani men raatabhar bhigaakar rakhem। subah sabake chhilake utaarakara, pisakara, pesat taiyaar karen। isamen thoda sa makakhan aur chini milakar khaaen। 9. haladi (Turmeric)- ek gilaas gumaguna paani len aur usamen haladi milaayen, is paani ko din bhar mem tin se chaar baar pien। piliya ke upachaar ke lie behad parabhaavi upaay hai। 10. chhaachh (Buttermilk)- piliya home par chhaachh behad laabhakaari hai। dahi ko mathakar chhaachh taiyaar karen aur isamen kaali mirach aur bhuna jira milaakar pien। 11. kela (Banana)- pake hue kele ko kuchalakara, usamen shahad milaayen। is tarah ke kele ko din men do baar khaaen। 12. gaajar ka ras (Carrot juice)- gaajar ka taaja ras nikaalakar pien, piliya men raahat milegi। 13. bel ki patati (Wood apple leaves)- bel ki patati ko pisakar paaudar bana lem। is paaudar ko paani men milaakar rojaana pien। piliya ke upachaar ke lie behad parabhaavi upaay hai। 14. kaimomaail chaay (Chamomile tea)- kaimomaail piliya rog men behad laabhakaari hai। kaimomaail ki patatiyon ki chaay banaakar pine se piliya rog jaladi thik hota hai। is chaay ko piliya thik home ke baad bhi pina jaari rakh sakate hain। 15. nvala (Gooseberry)- mvala vitaamin si se bharapoor hota hai। piliya rog men nvale ka sevan karane se behad laabh hota hai। mvale ke sevan se livar bhi majaboot hota hai। Disease: dooradarashita ya dooradaृshati dosh (Hyper Myopia) Description: dooradarashita ya dooradaृshati dosh (Hyper Myopia) dooradarashita ya dooradaृshati dosha, men koi bhi vayakati door ki chizon ko aasaani se aur saaf dekh sakate hain jabaki isamen karib ki chize dhundhali (blurr) dikhaai deti hain। dooradaृshati dosh ko savaasathay ki bhaasha men haaiparopiya (hyperopia) kahate hain। dooradaृshati dosh kitana gnbhir hai yah aapake dekhane ki kashamata par nirabhar karata hai। dekhane ke lie nkh ke do bhaag jimamedaar hote hain, kaॉramiya aur lensa। kaॉraniya nkh ke saamane ka paaradarashi hisasa hota hai jabaki lens nkh ke ndar bana hota hai jo ki chizon ko dekhane par unake shep men bhi badalaav karata hai। kaॉraniya aur lens donon ek saath kaaray karate hain aur aane vaali roshani ko milaate hain aur ise retina par phokas karate haim। retinaa, aai baॉl yaani nkh ke gole ke pichhe hota hai। jab nkh men parakaash paravesh karata hai to us par thik se phokas nahin ho paataa, yahi door daृshati dosh hota hai। yadi nkh ka gola saamaanay se chhota ho tab bhi door daृshati dosh ho sakata hai। door daृshati dosh bahut aam samasaya hai jise aasaami se thik bhi kiya ja sakata hai। Symptoms: - asaamaanay thakaan mahasoos hona। - nkh ke chaaron aur jalan ya darad - tanaavagarasat hona - dhundhala dikhana (nkh ke ekadam paas kaa) - parhame likhane mem dikakat hona Reasoms: dooradarashita ya dooradaृshati dosh ke kaaran (Causes & Reasoms of Hyper Myopia) dooradarashita ya dooradaृshati dosh mem door ki chijen saaph aur paas ki chijem dhundhali najar aati hain। nkh ke visharaam ki sathiti men, parakaash ki samntar kiranen daृshatipatal ki snvedanashil parat se kuchh pichhe phokas hoti hain। isi kaaran vayakati ko paas ki chijen dekhane men pareshaani hoti hai। isake alaava yadi maata pita ko door daृshati dosh hai to yah bachachon ko bhi parabhaavit kar sakata hai। isake alaava umar barhane ke saath bhi yah samasaya shuroo ho sakati hai। dooradarashita ko door karame ke lie sabase aasaan tarika chashama ya kaॉnataikat lens hota hai। lens ke parayog se nkhon men paravesh karame vaali roshani par behatar tarah se kendarit kar paate hain। Treatments: dooradarashita ya dooradaृshati ki rokathaam ke lie tipas (Treatment & Tips to Prevent Hyper Myopia) - let kar nahin parhana chaahie। - parhane likhane ke dauraan behatar roshani honi chaahie। - hari sabajiyn aur phalon ka parayog khaane mem jaroor karen। - tivi ya knpayootar par lagaataar kaam na karen, lagaataar na dekhen। - tivi ya knpayootar par kaaray karate vaqt bhi kamare men parayaapat roshani hona jaruri hai। Home Remedies: dooradarashita ya dooradaृshati dosh ke ghareloo upaaya- (Home Remedies for Hyper Myopia) nkhom ki raushani tej ho isake lie vitaamin se pooran bhojan karen। doodh aur dahi jaise khaaday padaarath jaroor khaaen। nda bhi nkhon ke lie behad phaayademnd hai। saunpha, mishari aur baadaam ko baraabar maatara mem milaakar paaudar banaaen aur subaha- shaam khaaen। baadaam aur gaund se bame ladadoo bhi nkhon ke lie phaayademnd hain। nkhom ki roshami tej karame ke lie salaad (salad) jaroor khaaen। nkhon ke vayaayaam (Eye exsercise) jaroor karen। Disease: munh ke chhaale (Mouth Ulcer) Description: munh ke chhaale (Mouth Ulcer) maauth alasar ko munh men chhaala aana kahate hain। munh ke ndar jo maram aur mulaayam utak hote hain, jise mayookas menbaren (mucous membrane) kahate hain, usi men chhaale paṛate hain। yah akasar khaane ke dauraan ya kaaphi garam khaane se gaal ke chamaṛe ke katane se hota hai। munh men agar chhaale ho jaaen to kuchh bhi khaane men kaaphi pareshaani hoti hai। khaana to door paani pina bhi mushakil ho jaata hai। chhaale hone par munh men tej jalan aur darad hota hai। kuchh logon ko to bhojan nali tak men chhaale ho jaate hain। munh men chhaala (Muh ke Chhale) aana ek naaramal bimaari hai, jo kuchh dinom baad apane aap thik ho jaati hai। kuchh logon ko chhaale baara-baar aate hain। aise logon ko apani poori daॉkatari jnch karaani chaahie, taaki sahi ilaaj kiya ja sake। munh mem chhaale hone ke kai kaaran hote haim। kai baar pet ki garami se bhi chhaale ho jaate hain। Symptoms: - chabaane aur barash karane men pareshaani - bhookh men kami - masaaledaara, khatata aur namakin chij khaane par tej jalan - munh ke ndar saphed aur laal gola-gol chhaale Reasons: munh men chhaalon ke kaaran (Causes of Mouth Ulcer) kabaj (Constipatiom) lnbe samay tak kabaj rahane se munh men chhaale a jaate haim। aayuraved ke anusaar munh men chhaale pet ki kharaabi tatha pet ki garami ki vajah se hote hain। kabaj isaki mool vajah hai। gaal ya jibh ka katana (Imjury in Cheek and Tounge) kai baar koi chij khaate samay dnton ke bich jibh ya gaal ka hisasa a jaata hai, jisaki vajah se chhaale ho jaate hain। aise chhaale munh ki laar se apane-aap thik ho jaate hain। davaaon ke saaid iphekat (Medicine Side Effects) davaaon ke saaid iphekat ki vajah se bhi munh men chhaale hote hain। lnbe samay tak entibaॉyotik davaaon sevan karane se munh men chhaale aane ki smbhaavama jayaada hoti hai। jayaada entibaॉyotik ke sevan se hamaari ntom mem laabhadaayak kitaanuon ki snkhaya ghat jaati hai, natija munh men chhaale ho jaate hain। dnton ki galat snrachana (Wrong Structure of Teeth) dmton ki galat snrachana ki vajah se bhi mumh men chhaale hote haim। yadi dnt aade-tirachhe, nukile ya aadhe toote hue hain aur isaki vajah se ve jibh ya munh mem chubhate hain ya unase lagaataar ragad lagati rahati hai, to vahn chhaale ho jaate hain। Treatments: ilaaj aur dekhabhaal (Treatment of Mouth Ulcer) - jab tak chhaale khatam nahin ho masaaledaar aur khatata khaana bnd kar den। - khoob paani pien। - gunagune namaka-paami se kulala karen। - munh ko hamesha saaph rakhen। - darad hone par pen kilar dava le sakate haim। - chhaale vaale jagah par enti-sepatik jel lagaaen। - medikedet maauth vaash se munh saaph karen, kulala karen। - subah subah gaay ke doodh se bane dahi ke saath ek kela khaane se aaraam milata hai। - khoob tamaatar khaaen। tamaatar ka ras ek galaas paami men milaakar kulala karame se chhaale mit jaate hain। - yadi chhaale saamaanay haim, to vitaamin 'bi' kaॉmapalekas tatha pholik esid ki goliyn 2-3 din tak lene se chhaale thik ho jaate hain। - chhaale par boro galisarin bhi lagaai ja sakati hai ya poteshiyam paramainganet ke ghol se kulala karane par chhaale khatam hote hain। Home Remedies: munh ke ndar ki satah ke kisi bhi tarah se katane ya usake upar koi phoda nikalame se alasar ya chhaala ho jaata hai। munh ka alasar hone par vayakati ka munh tatha jibh parabhaavit ho jaate hain jisase vayakati ko kuchh bhi khaane ya pine men pareshaani hoti hai। jaanie munh ke chhaalon se bachaav ke ghareloo nusakhe (Home remedies for mouth ulcer): 1. naariyal ka doodh (Cocomut milk)- naariyal ka doodh munh ke alasar men darad se raahat deta hai saath hi jalan ko door karata hai। upachaar ke lie ek chamamach naariyal ke doodh men thoda sa shahad milaakar alasar ke upar lagaaen। is upaay ko din men tin se chaar baar karen। isake alaava maariyal ke doodh se kulala karane par bhi aaraam milata hai। 2. dhaniya ke bij (Coriamder seed)- dhaniya ke bij bhi munh ke alasar se raahat dete hain। alasar se hone vaali jalan ko bhi door karate hain। upachaar ke lie paani men dhamiya ke bij daalakar ubaalen aur is paani ko chhaanakar alag rakhen। is paani ko munh men ghuma ghuma kar kulala karen। is upaay ko bhi din bhar men tin se chaar baar karen। 3. beking soda (Baking soda)- beking soda ya sodiyam baai kaarabonet bhi munh ke alasar se nijaat dila sakata hai। esidik khaane- pine se hone vaale alasar men yah behad laabhakaari hai। upachaar ke lie ek chhoti chamamach bekimg paaudar mem paani milaakar pesat taiyaar karen aur parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen। 4. shahad (Honey)- munh ke alasar se raahat dene men shahad bhi behad parabhaavi hai। shahad men enti ऑkasident aur enti maaikarobal gun hote hain। upachaar ke lie rooi ke phaahe ko shahad men dubaakara, parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen। isi tarah galisarin aur vitaamin i tel ko bhi lagaaya ja sakata hai। 5. elovera (Aloevera)- elovera ka rasa, parabhaavit sathaan par lagaame se alasar se hone vaale darad se raahat milati hai। elovera paraakaृtik entisepatik ki tarah kaaray karata hai jisase chhaale jaladi thik hote haim। 6. dhaniya patati (Coriander leaves)- dhaniya patati ko kachacha chabaane se munh ke alasar se raahat milati hai। dhaniya patati men fॉlik esid ke saath vitaamin bi 1, bi 2, bi 6 aur vitaamin si paaya jaata hai। dhaniya patati ko dndi ke saath lagabhag 10 minat tak chabaana chaahie। isake parayog se munh se aane vaali duragndh se bhi raahat milati hai। 7. tulasi (Basil)- tulasi men enti vaayarala, enti baikatiriyal aur enti phngal gun paae jaate hain। upachaar ke lie 5 se 6 tulasi ki patatiyon ko dhokar achachhi parakaar chabaakar khaaen aur usake baad thoda paani pi len। is upaay ko din men do baara, subah aur shaam karen। 8. baraph (Ice)- barapha, alasar ke kaaran munh men hone vaale darad se raahat deti hai। baraph ko parabhaavit sathaan par lagaane se, snbndhit jagah thodi der ke lie sunan pad jaati hai jisase alasar se hone vaali jalan aur darad se raahat milati hai। Disease: alasar (Ulcer) Description: alasar (Ulcer) pet ya chhoti mton men hone vaale alasar ko pepatik alasar (Peptic Ulcer) ke roop men jaama jaata hai। pet ke pepatik alasar ko gaisatarik alasar bhi kahate hain। alasar aahaar aur tanaav ya phir pet men amal (acid) ki atirikat maatara jama home se hota hai। aamaashay ka alasar pet ke alasar se jayaada kaॉman bimaari hai। pepatik alasar aamaashay aur pet ke bich ki patali surakasha divaar men ghaav ke baad chhed ho jaane se hota hai। lnbe samay tak entibaayotikasa, darad aur sateraॉyad ki dava khaane ke alaava sharaab ke sevan se pet aur aamaashay ka alasar hota hai। pet mem esid aur enjaaim ke banane se chhoti nt ke upar aamaashay ke paas chhed ya ghaav ho jaata hai jise alasar kahate hain। adhiknshath yah helikobaikatar paailori (helicobacter pylori) naam ke ek jivaanu ke snkaraman se hota hai। kuchh logon men alasar ke lakashan aasaani se jabaki doosaron men ye jaladi mahin dikhaai paṛate hain। kabhi-kabhi alasar unahem bhi ho jaata hai, jinahonne isake kisi bhi lakashan ka anubhav nahim kiya hai। Symptoms: - agar pet ka darad alasar ke kaaran ho raha hai, to raat men aur jab bhi aap bhookhe hon, yah achaanak tivar ho sakata hai। - khaama khaane ke do ghnte baad bhookh mahasoos karanaa। - gais aur dakaar men vaृdadhi। - thakaavat ka ahasaas honaa। - pet bhara hua mahasoos honaa, aur dher saara taral padaarath pi paane men asamarathataa। - bhookh men kami। - vajan ghatanaa। - sine ki hadadiyon aur pet ki maabhi ke bich kisi bhi sathaan par darada। - halaki matali (nausea), jo subah jaagane par sabase aam hoti hai। Reasons: alasar ke kaaran (Causes of Ulcers) koi bhi ek khaas kaaran nahin hota hai jo alasar ke lie utataradaayi hota hai। bahut saare kaaran ke parabhaav se alasar paida hota hai। lekin yah sapashat hai ki pet aur aamaashay ke baach enjaaim aur paachak ras ke asntulan se jo esid bamata hai usi se alasar banata hai। aam taur par adhiknsh alasar H. Pylori baikateriya ke snkaraman se hi hota hai। yah baikateriya pet aur chhoti nt ke bich jo surakasha divaar hoti hai, vahin rahata hai। aamataur par yah koi nukasaan nahin pahunchaata hai। lekin isake snkaraman se kabhi-kabhi pet ke mdaruni satah aur nt men soojan ho jaati hai jo baad men alasar ka rup dhaaran kar leta hai। pen kilaras aur enti inphalaametari dava ke lagaataar sevan se chhoti mt aur pet ke bich ki surakasha divaar men soojan aur chhed ho jaata hai jisase alasar hone ki snbhaavana rahati hai। aur bhi hain kai vajah (Other Reason for Ulcer) sharaab aur dhoomarapaan ka jayaada sevan kisi gnbhir bimaari ki vajah se redieshan therepi ki vajah se kise ho sakata hai alasar (Whom May be More Prome to Ulcer) pet ke alasar ke dher saare kaaran home par bhi jin logon men isake vikasit hone ka adhik khatara hota hai, ve hain: ech paailori baikatiriya se snkaramit loga। miyamit roop se daragas ya sui se davaaon ka sevan karane vaale loga। alasar ke paarivaarik itihaas vaale loga। niyamit roop se sharaab pine vaale loga। livara, gurade, ya phephaṛon se juṛi bimaariyon vaale loga। 50 saal se adhik umar ke loga। Treatments: dekhabhaal aur ilaaj (Treatment for Ulcer) - poha aur saunph ko baraabar maatara men milaakar chooram bana lijie, 20 garaam chooran ko 2 litar paani men subah gholakar rakhie, ise raat tak poora pi jaaen। ala‍sar men aaraam milegaa। - patata gobhi aur gaajar ko baraabar maatara men lekar joos bana lijie, is joos ko subaha-shaam eka-ek kap pine se pepatik alasar ke marijon ko aaraam milata hai। - ala‍sar ke marijon ke lie gaay ke doodh se bane ghi ka isatemaal karana phaayademnd hota hai। - ala‍sar ke marijon ko baadaam ka sevan karana chaahie, baadaam pisakar isaka doodh bana lijie, ise subaha-shaam pine se ala‍sar thik ho jaata hai। - sahajan ke pata‍te ko pisakar dahi ke saath pesat banaakar len। is pesa‍t ka sevan din men ek baar karame se ala‍sar men phaayada hota hai। Home Remedies: alasar (ulcer) sharir ki upari tavacha ya mayookas jhilali par ubhara hua ghaav hota hai। alasar jayaadaatar helikobaikatar paayalori (Helicobacter pylori) naam ke jivaanu davaara hota hai। pet ki nt (Intestine) men kai parakaar ke daravay nikalate hain jo bhojan ko pachaane men sahaayak hote hain lekin jab yah daravay jayaada maatara men nikalate hain to pet v nt ki komal tavacha ko jalaane lagate hain। isake kaaran pet men ghaav bam jaata hai। jaanie alasar se bachaav ke ghareloo upaay (Home remedies for ulcer): 1.poha (Bitten rice)- poha alasar ke upachaar men behad phaayademnd hai। poha aur saunph ko baraabar maatara men milaakar paaudar bana len। is paaudar ki 20 garaam maatara ko 2 litar paani men gholakar rakh dijie। dopahar se raat tak is paani ko poora khatam karen। alasar se raahat milegi। 2. patata gobhi aur gaajar (Cabbage amd carrot)- patata gobhi men lekatik esid hota hai jisase emino esid banata hai jo pet men rakat ka paravaah barhaata hai। isake saath hi patata gobhi mem vitaamin si (vitamin c) bhi uchach maatara men hota hai। patata gobhi aur gaajar ko baraabar maatara men milaakar joos taiyaar karen aur subah shaam eka-ek kap pien। 3. naariyal (Coconut)- naariyal men entibaikatiriyal gun paaye jaate hain, jo ki alasar paida karane vaale baikatiriya ko maar dete hain। naariyal ke doodh aur paani men bhi enti- alasar gun paaye jaate hain। alasar ke upachaar ke lie rojaama naariyal paani pien। naariyal ke tel ka sevan bhi alasar se bachaata hai। 4. gaay ka doodh (Cow milk)- haladi men enti baikatiriyal gun hote hain, gaay ke doodh men haladi milaakar pine se bhi alasar rogiyon ko laabh milata hai। 5. baadaam (Almomd)- alasar rogiyon ko baadaam pisakara, khaane se laabh hota hai। baadaam ko pisakar usaka doodh jaisa bamaakar pien। 6. sahajan (Drum stick)- sahajam ki phali bhi savaasathay ke lihaaj se behad phaayademnd hai। isamen enti baikatiriyal gum hote hain jo rogon se ladne men sahaayak hote hain। sahajan ki phali ko pisakara, dahi ke saath milaakar khaane se alasar rog men aaraam milata hai। 7. shahad (Honey)- kachacha shahad bhi pet ke alasar men behad laabhakaari hai। shahad mem galookoj pairaॉkasaaid (glucose peroxide) paaya jaata hai, jo pet men maujood haanikaarak baikatiriya ko khatam kar deta hai। isake saath hi shahad ke sevan se pet ki jalam se bhi aaraam milata hai। 8. kela (Banana)- kela men entibaikatiriyal tatav paae jaate hain। kela khaane se esiditi se bhi raahat milati hai। kachacha aur paka donon hi tarah ka kela khaane se alasar rogiyon ko behad aaraam milata hai। kachache kele ki sabaji banaakar usamen ek chutaki hing milaakar khaaen। 9. lahasun (Garlic)- lahasum pet ke alasar men behad laabhakaari hai। upachaar ke lie do se tim lahasun ki kaliyon ko kuchalakara, paani ke saath khaaen। 10. belaphal (Wood apple)- pet ke alasar men belaphal aur usaki patatiyon ka sevan bhi behad laabhadaayak hai। patatiyon men maujood teninas pet ko, kisi bhi tarah ke nukasaan se bachaata hai। belaphal ka ras bhi pet ki jalan aur darad ko door kara, alasar se bachaata hai। Disease: daayariya (Diarrhea) Description: daayariya (Diarrhea) lagaataar looj moshan yaani patala dasat aanaa, ulati homa daayariya kahalaata hai। daayariya vaayarala, baikateriyal snkaraman ke kaaran to hota hi hai lekin sabase kaॉman kaaran hai khaana-paam men gaṛabaṛi, paradooshit paani aur nt ki gaṛabaṛi। din men agar tin se adhik baar paani ke saath patala dasat ho raha ho to yah daayariya ka lakashan hai। daayariya men sharir men paani ki kami ho jaati hai jise dihaaidareshan kahate hain jo kaaphi gmbhir hota hai। isase sharir kamajor ho jaata hai, sharir men snkaraman phailane ka khatara kaaphi baṛh jaata hai। samay par ilaaj nahin hone par marij ki jaam bhi ja sakati hai। aam taur par daayariya 3 se 7 dinon tak pareshaan karata hai। daayariya vaise to kabhi bhi ho sakata hai, lekin barasaat men vaayaral daayariya jayaada pareshaam karata hai। isaki vajah gmda paani aur khaanaa-pina hai। daayariya achaanak ho jaata hai aur koras poora hone ke baad hi khatam hota hai। pet men jayaada esiditi banane se bhi daayariya hoti hai। yah sabhi umar ke logon ko pareshaan karata hai। ekayoot daayariya (Acute Diarhea) vayasakon ko saal bhar men ek baar aur baṛe bachachon ko do baar hota hai। is bimaari men sabase jayaada khatara dihaaidareshan se hota hai, jisamen sharir se saara paani aur khatam ho jaata hai। nt men paani jaane se pahale hi vo paas ho jaata hai। Symptoms: - nton men soojan se hua daayariya - patala dasat ya looj moshan (paani ki taraha) agar do haphate tak rahe। - dasat ke saath khoona, nv aur pota aata hai। isase sharir kaaphi kamajor ho jaata hai। - ulati, mitali aane ke saath patala dasat aata hai। yah pet aur nt men esiditi banane se hota hai। Reasons: daayariya ke kaaran (Causes & Reasons of Diarrhea) vaayaral daayariya (Viral Diarrhea) vaayaral imphekashan se sabase jayaada daayariya hota hai। isake lakashan kabhi saamaanay to kabhi kaaphi gnbhir ho jaate hain। patala dasata, looj moshana, pet men marod aana aur bukhaar isake saamaanay lakashan hain। vaayaral daayariya 3 se 7 din tak rahata hai। vaayaral daayariya niman vaayaral smkaramam ke kaaran hote hain rotaavaayaras (Rotavirus)- navajaat bachachom men rotaavaayaras vaayaral snkaraman se vaayaral daayariya ka khatara rahata hai। isase bachane ke lie bachachon ko enti rotaavaayaras imjekashan bhi lagaaya jaata hai। norovaayaras (Norovirus)- yah vaayaral daayariya vayasakom aur sakool jaate bachachon ko sabase jayaada pareshaan karata hai। narasing homa, de keyar sentar aur resatorent men isake snkaramam ka khatara sabase jayaada rahata hai। edemovaayarasa(Adenovirus)- yah vaayaral snkaraman har umar ke logon ko hota hai। baikatiriyal snkaraman se daayariya (Bacterial infections) baikatiriyal snkaraman se hua daayariya kaaphi siriyas hota hai। baikatiriyal snkaraman paradooshit paani, bhojana, phood pavaaijaning se hoti hai। baikatiriyal snkaramam se hui daayariya men lagaataar ulati aamaa, lagaataar looj moshan hote rahamaa, dasat ke saath siraph paani aane ki shikaayat se marij ki haalat kaaphi gmbhir ho jaati hai। baikatiriyal snkaraman se pet men gais bhi ban jaati hai। gmbhir baikatiriyal snkaraman men kabhi-kabhi dasat ke saath khoona, pota aur nv bhi aati hai। aur bhi hain kai vajah (Some more causes) nton men soojan ke baad bhi daayariya hota hai i-kolaai ke smkaraman se bhi daayariya hota hai alakohal sevan ke saaid iphekat men bhi daayariya hota hai daayabitij ke marij ko bhi daayariya ki shikaayat rahati hai rediyotherepi, kimotherepi mem bhi daayariya ki shikaayat hoti hai kisi khaas entibaayotikas ke sevan se bhi daayariya hota hai, khaasakar vaise enti baayotikas jo nt par parabhaav daalate hain parajivi jo paradooshit paani aur khaane ke jarie hamaare pet men jaata hai, vo hamaare paachan tntar ko bigaaṛ deta hai aur jisase daayariya ki shikaayat hoti hai kainsar ki davaa, vajan ghataane ki davaa, balad pareshar ki dava ke saaid iphekat ki vajah se bhi daayariya hota hai elaraji se bhi daayariya hoti hai, khaasakar vaise chij khaane se masalana- aaratiphishiyal savitanar ya doodh men laikatoj ki maatara rahane se daayariya ho sakata hai। Treatmemts: ilaaj aur dekhabhaal (Treatment and Care for Diarrhea) - daayariya hone par tela-masaalon vaale khaame se parahej karana chaahie। - daayariya men doodh ya doodh se bame padaarath nahin khaana chaahie, marij ki haalat aur bigaṛ jaati hai। - kele, chaavala, seb ka murababa aur tosat ka misharam jise baraat kahate hain, isake sevan se daayariya men raahat milati hai। - kachacha kela aur chaaval nton ki gati ko niymtarit karane aur dasat rokame men sahaayata karate hain। - parayaapat maatara men taral padaarath len lekin agar phir bhi daayariya baṛh raha ho to turnt daॉkatar se snparak karen। Home Remedies: jab vayakati ki paachan kariya (Digestive System) suchaaroo roop se kaaray karana bnd kar deti hai, tab use ulati aur patale dasat hone lagate hain। yahi sathiti daayariya kahalaati hai। daayariyaa, baikatiriyal tatha vaayaral inphekashan (Bacterial amd Viral Infection) ke kaaran hota hai, jo dooshit bhojan ya khaane ke davaara vayakati ke sharir men pahunch kara, paachan kariya ko parabhaavit karate haim। daayariya kai dauraan vayakati ke pet men darad hota hai, pet men ainthana, ji michalaana aadi samasayaaen bhi ho sakati hain। daayariya ke dauraan vayakati ko di-haaidareshan (Dehydration) ho sakata hai, jisase sathiti aur bhi bigad sakati hai। daayariya ke lakashan vayakati men do se chaar din men ubharate hain। jaanie daayariya se bachaav ke lie kuchh ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies of Diarrhea) niche diye gae upachaaron ke davaara daayariya bimaari men raahat paai ja sakati hai: 1. dahi (Yogurt)- dahi men maujood baikatiriyaa, sharir mem maujood vishaile baikatiriya ka naash kara, daayariya se bachaate hain। daayariya ke upachaar ke lie do katori dahi khaame se hi behad aaraam milata hai। saade chaaval men dahi milaakar bhi khaai ja sakati hai। 2. adarak (Ginger)- adarak ka parayog phood paॉijaning (food poisoning) hone par bhi kiya jaata hai, aise men daayariya se raahat dene men bhi adarak kaaphi parabhaavashaali hai। adarak ke parayog se pet ki ainthan (stomach cramps) aur darad se bhi raahat milati hai। upachaar ke lie adarak ko kadadookas karake, usamen shahad (honey) milaakar khaaen। isake tumrat baad paani n pien। adarak ki chaay (bina doodh ki) bhi kaaphi aaraam deti hai। 3. methi daana (Methidana)- daayariya ke ilaaj ke lie methi daana behad phaayademnd bataaya gaya hai। ek chhoti chamamach methi daana ko chabaakara, ek badi chamamach dahi khaane se daayariya se nijaat milati hai। isake alaava ek chamamach methi daana aur jira (cumin) ko bhoon kar paaudar bama len aur do badi chamamach dahi men milaakar khaaen। is misharan ko din bhar men tin baar khaane se behad aaraam milata hai। 4. seb ka siraka (Apple cider vimegar)- seb ka siraka bhi daayariya men behad phaayademnd hai। seb ke sirake ka esidik guma, daayariya ke baikatiriya ko khatam kar deta hai। upachaar ke lie ek gilaas paani mem ek chamamach siraka milaaen aur pi lem। is misharan ko ek din mem do se tin baar tab tak pien jab tak daayariya thik n ho jaae। 5. kela (Banana)- kele men kaaphi maatara mem paikatim tatav (pectin content) aur pauteshiyam hota hai, isalie daayariya men kela khaane ki salaah di jaati hai। daayariya hone par do se tin pake hue kela roj khaaen। 6. kaimomaail chaay (Chamomile tea)- kaimomaail daayariya ke upachaar mem behad phaayademnd hai। daayariya ke upachaar ke lie kaimomaail ki chaay banaakar pien। 7. saphed chaaval (White rice)- saadaa, saphed gile chaaval bhi daayariya ke dauraan khaane ki salaah di jaati hai। is tarah ke chaaval supaachay hote hain। is tarah ke chaaval khaane se dasat kam aate hain। saada chaaval ko thoda gila karake khaaen। savaad ke lie chaaval mem dahi milaakar kha sakate hain। 8. gaajar ka soop (Carrot soup)- gaajar ka soop bhi daayariya men behad phaayademnd hai। daayariya ke dauraan sharir mem hui poshak tatavom (nutrients) ki kami ko poora karane ke saath hi gaajar ka soop imayooniti (immunity) ko majaboot karata hai। soop banaane ke lie, gaajar ko kaat kar ubaal len aur jab gaajar ubalakar paami men ghul jaae taba, paani ko chhaam kar alag kara len। isamen savaadaanusaar mamaka, bhuna jira aur kaalimirach paaudar milaaen। Disease: susati (Lethargy) Description: susati (Lethargy) kai baar sharir men saphoorati (energy) nahin rahati। sharir ekadam thaka hua mahasoos karata hai, aur bahut kamajori mahasoos hoti hai। kai baar aalas itana hota hai ki hamesha nimd aati rahati hai। isi avasatha ko lithaaraji ya susati kahate hain। tanaavapooran maahaul ya poshan ki kami ke kaaran sharir kamajor hone lagata hai। kai baar raat men achachhi nind n sone par bhi agale din thaka hua mahasoos karate hain। lekin jayaada susati sharir ke lie behad haanikaarak bhi hai। kai baar yah susati maut ki vajah bhi ho sakati hai, kayonki jayaada susati se baren ke selas bhi susat hone lagate hain aur dhire dhire kaaray karana bnd kar dete hain। poore sharir ki savabhaavik parakariya dhimi pad jaati hai, jo kai samasayaaon ka kaaran ho sakati hai। aise men sharir ko ekativ banaaye rakhana behad jaroori hota hai। Symptoms: - eknt achachha lagana - kamajori mahasoos hona (Weakness in Body) - kisi kaam men man n lagana - chhote se chhota kaam karane men chidchidaana - har samay nind aur aalas aana - har samay lete rahame ka man hona - man mem hamesha nakaaraatamak vichaar aana Reasons: susati ke kaaran (Causes of Lethargy) susati ka anubhav sabhi ko hota hai, lekin thoda aaraam karane ya raat ki nind ke baada, agali subah tak susati door ho jaati hai। yadi isake baad bhi susati bani rahe to yah bimaari ka snket ho sakata hai। kisi bhi vayakati ki susati ka asar n keval usake shaaririk balaki maanasik v saamaajik satar par bhi padta hai। susati, vayasat dimacharayaa, kharaab jivam shaili, bimaariyn, aniyamit v asntulit khaana-paan v anay kaaranon se ho sakati hai। aamataur par achachhi nind lene aur aur dinacharaya men badalaav se is samasaya ko kaaphi had tak thik kiya ja sakata hai lekin kai baar chikitasak ki salaah leni hi padti hai। is samasaya ke anay kaaran (Reasons of Lethargy) kamajori ki vajah se। jayaada tanaavagarasat rahane se। mind poori n hone ki vajah se। sharir men vitaamin ki kami se। sharir men khoon ki kami ki vajah se। Treatments: susati se bachane ke upaay (Tips to Prevent from Lethargy) - roj yog aur vayaayaam karen। - subah ki taaji hava men tahalen। - tanaavamukat rahane ka parayaas karem। - khaane men vitaamin ki maatara barhaaen। - kam se kam 8 ghnte ki nind jaroor len। - nvale ka murababa bhi sharir ko saphoorati deta hai। - halaka sngita, halaki aavaaj men sunem। isase bhi maanasik susati door hoti hai। - kai baar sugndhit telom ki maalish se bhi sharir ki susati aur susati mitaai ja sakati hai। - sntulit aur paushatik bhojan karen, jisamem hari sabajiyn, daalen, dahi aur mausami phal shaamil hon। - apani ungaliyon ke poron se chehare ki masaaj karen। aisa karane se balad sarakuleshan barhegaa, jisase vayakati ekativ mahasoos karegaa। Home Remedies: bhaagadaud bhari aadhunik jindagi aur kai tarah ke tanaava, n keval shaaririk balaki maanasik roop se bhi vayakati ko thaka dete hain। thakaavat har kisi ko hoti hai paranatu kai logon ko poore sharir men darad ki shikaayat rahati hai। darad ko kam karane ke lie log akasar penakilar le lete hain। ye davaaen tunrat aaraam deti hain paranatu lamabe samay tak isaka parayog nukasaan pahuncha sakata hai। aaie jaanen thakaavat se bachaav ke lie ghareloo nusakhe (Home remedies for lethargy) 1. garim ti (Green tea)- thakaavat ko door karane ke lie ek kap garim ti pina behad parabhaavi hai। niyamit roop se garin ti pine se vajan bhi kntarol men rahata hai। mnsapeshiyon men darad (muscle pain) hone par aap garin ti behad laabhakaari hai। 2. adarak ki chaay (Ginger tea)- adarak ki chaay kudarati penakilar ke roop men kaaray karati hai। yah vayakati ko tarotaaja bhi mahasoos karaati hai। tulasi ke kaarhe men adarak milaakar bhi piya ja sakata hai। 3. saunph (Saunf)- kisi pakavaan men savaad barhaane ke saath hi saunph sns men taajaग़i laane men bhi behad parabhaavakaari hai। saunph ka parayog rasoi men zaroor hota hai। saumph khaane se pet saaf rahata hai aur aap khud ko tarotaaja mahasoos karate hai। 4. ajavaayan (Ajwain)- ajavaayan ke patate bhi darad nivaarak dava ki tarah kaam karate hain। yah sharir ke toote-phute ki ng ki maramamat karane aur jodon ke darad men bahut laabhaparad hote hain। 5. kadadoo ke bij (Pumpkin seed)- kadadoo ke bij men maiganishiyam hota hai, jo aalas v thakaavat se ladne men madad karata hai। aadhe ghnte ki ekasarasaaij men agar aap thaka hua mahasoos karati hain to isaka matalab hai ki aapamen maiganishiyam ki kami hai। vayaayaam ke dauraan sharir mem ऑkasijan ke niramaan ke lie maiganishiyam jaroori hai। isaki kami ki vajah se thakaavat jaladi hoti hai। 6. akharot (Wallnut)- akharot men omega 3 phaiti esid paaya jaata hai। omega 3 phaiti esid n keval thakaan aur aalas se raahat deta hai, balaki yah avasaad se bhi bachaata hai। isalie akharot khaane se aapaki jhapakiyon ki samasaya door hogi। 7. anaaj (Whole grain)- anaaj men phaaibar ki maatara adhik hoti hai। isalie aalas aur thakaan mitaane men yah madadagaar saabit hota hai। anaaj men kaॉmapalekas kaarabohaaidaret (complex carbohydrate) hote hain। ye thakaan se ladne men madadagaar hote hain। 8. laal mirach (Red chilly)- laal mirach men vitaamim si paaya jaata hai, jo thakaan door karata hai। laal mirach se dimaag ekativ rahata hai aur ham hamesha tarotaaja mahasoos karate hain। 9. dahi (Curd)- dahi men maujood achachhe baikatiriya paachan tntar (immune system) ko majaboot rakhate hain। 4 sapataah tak din men do baar yadi dahi khaaya jaae to shaaririk aur maanasik sehat ke saath rog paratirodhak kashamata bhi barhati hai aur thakaan kam hoti hai। Disease: masatishak ka daura (Cerebral Stroke) Description: hamaare sharir men masatishak aur maadiyon ko paraanavaayu (Oxygen) aur poshak tatavom ki nirntar aapoorati rakat vaahikaaon se rakat ke davaara ki jaati hai। jab bhi in rakatavaahikaaom men kisi kaaran kashati pahunchati hai ya avarodh niramaan hota hai tab masatishak ke kuchh hisason ko rakat ki aapoorati bmd ho jaati hai। jis tarah haraday ko rakat ki aapoorati n hone par haृdayaghaat a jaata hai, usi parakaar masatishak ke kuchh hisase ko 3 se 4 minat se jayaada rakat m milane par paraanavaayu aur poshak tatavon ke abhaav men nashat hone lagata hai, ise hi masatishak ka daura bhi kahate hain। Symptoms: - kamajori mahasoos hona (Weakness in Body) - disha aur niradesh samajhane men pareshaani - siradarad hona - bharam ki sathiti - bolane men takaliph hona - ji michalaana aur ulati hona - sharir ke ek hi taraph ke chehare, haath ya tng men sunanapam - dhire ya asapashat bolana - achaanak ladkhadaanaa, chakakar aanaa, sharir ka sntulan bigadma - ek ya donon nkhon se dekhane men kathinaai Reasons: masatishak ke daure ke kaaran (Causes & Reasons of Cerebral Stroke) masatishak ka daura hone ke mukhayata: 2 kaaran hote hain, jo niman hain: 1. arakatata masatishak ka daura (Ischemic stroke)- daura padne ka sabase aam kaaran hai। yah dimaag ke kisi rakatavaahini ke snkiran hone ya avarodhar niramaan hone ke kaaram hota hai। yah bhi do parakaar ka hota hai- 1.1. tharomabotik satarok (Thrombotic stroke)- is parakaar ke masatishak ke daure mem masatishak ki rakat vaahini men khoon ke jam jaane ke kaaran ya thakake ke kaaran avarodh ho jaata hai। jim rogiyon mem khoon ke ndar kolesataraॉl ka paramaan jayaada hota hai, aise rogiyon ki rakatavaahini mem bhitari satar par vasa jama ho jaati hai jise palaak kahate hai। is par khoon ka thakaka jama ho jaane par dhire-dhire poori rakatavaahini men avarodh hone lagata hai aur masatishak ke us hisase ko rakat n milane par tharomabotik satarok pad jaata hai। 1.2. inbolik satarok (Embolic stroke)- is parakaar ke masatishak ke daure men rakat ka thakaka ya injekashan ya salaain davaara galati se rakat vaahini men paravesh kiya hua hava ka chhota bulabula masatishak ke kisi chhoti rakatavaahini men phasane ke kaaran rakatavaahimi men avarodh niramaan ho jaata hai aur masatishak ke us hisase ko rakat n milane par inbolik satarok pad jaata hai। 2. rakatasataraav masatishak ka daura (Hemorrhagic stroke)- masatishak ki kisi rakatavaahini men rakatasataraav hone ke kaaran hone vaale is parakaar ke masatishak ke daure behad gnbhir hote hai। uchach rakatachaapa, rakat vaahini ki janamajaat vikaृti ya rakat vaahini men phulaav ke kaaran masatishak men rakatasataraav ho sakata hai। isake do parakaar hain- 2.1. intaraa- karaaniyal haimarej (Intra-cranial hemorrhage)- is parakaar men masatishak ke kisi rakatavaahini men rakatasataraav hone ke kaaran masatishak ke us hisase ko rakat ki aapoorati men kami aane ke kaaran baren selas ko kashati pahunchati hai। is parakaar ke masatishak ke daure ka paramukh kaaran uchach rakatadaab hai। lagaataar kai samay tak uchach rakatachaap ke kaaran rakatavaahini kamajor aur kadi ho jaati hai aur parinaamata: phat jaati hai। 2.2. saba- aarakamoid haimarej (Sub-archnoid hemorrhage)- is parakaar men masatishak aur kapaal ke bich ke satar men kisi rakatavaahini men rakatasataraav home ke kaaran sab aarakamoid sapes mem rakat ekatarit ho jaata hai। isaka paramukh kaaran rakat vaahimi ki janamajaat vikaृti ya rakat vaahini men phulaav hota hai। is parakaar men rogi ko tej saradarad ka anubhav hota hai। 2.3. tarnsent ishachemik ataik (Transient ischemic attack)- ek tisare parakaar ka bhi masatishak ka asathaai daura hota hai jisame satarok ke lakashan kuchh mimaton se lekar kuchh ghnto tak hi rahate haim aur baad men thik ho jaate hain। ise tarnsent ishachemik ataik (Transient ischemic attack) ya tiaaie (TIA) kaha jaata hai। yah is baat ki chetaavani deta hai ki aapako koi samasaya hai aur isaka ilaaj n karaane par nikat bhavishay men aapako satarok pad sakata hai। Treatments: masatishak ka daure se bachane ke lie upaay (Treatments & Tips to Prevents Cerebral Stroke) - sharaab aur dhoomarapaan bnd karen। - phala, sabajiyn itayaadi aahaar lena chaahie। - tamaav se door rahen। niyamit vayaayaam aur yog karem। - agar aap motaape ke shikaar hai to apana vajan niyntarit rakhen। - agar baara-baar siradarad ki pareshaani hoti hai to chikitasak se isaki jnch karaaen। - agar aap uchach rakatachaap (Hypertension), madhumeh (Diabetes), haraday rog (Heart disease) se pidit haim to niyamit daॉkatar se jnch karaate rahen। Disease: maayopiya (Myopia) Description: aajakal adhikaash logon ki mkhon men ripharaikativ (Refractive) vikaar yaani kiranon ke vakar ki samasaya ke lakashan dikhaai dene lage hain। isamem nikat daृshati dosh yaani maayopiya (Myopia) se sabase jayaada log parabhaavit hain। chikitasakon ke anusaara, bachapan men dekhame ki kashamata ka vikaas aur kishoraavasatha men nkh ki lnbaai barhati hai lekin nikat daृshati dosh home ki vajah se yah kuchh jayaada hi barh jaati hai। aisi sathiti men nkh men jaanevaala parakaash retina par kendarit nahin hotaa। isi vajah se tasavir dhundhali dikhaai deti hai lekin is dosh ko kaॉnatekat lens ya sarajari se thik karaaya ja sakata hai। Symptoms: - chakakar aana - bachachon ko sakool men balaik borad par likha hua n dikhana - telivijan dhumdhala dikhana - nkhon ka bhainga hona - doori par likhe akashar n parh paana - sir men darad rahana Reasons: maayopiya ke kaarana- (Causes & Reasons of Myopia) aise log jo nikat daृshati dosh ki samasaya se pareshaan hain yaani ki jinahen thodi door ki chijen bhi saaph dikhaai nahin detin, use ripharekativ erar (Refractive error) kahate hain। maayopiya se garasat logon men aaibaॉl bahut lnbi ho jaati hai ya phir kaॉraniya (Cornia) bahut jayaada karavi ho jaata hai jisase nkh men pahunchane vaala parakaash thik tarah se phokas nahin kar paataa। aise men kisi bhi chij ki tasavira, retina par n banakara, usake saamane ban jaati hai jisase chijen dhundhali dikhaai deti hain। yah samasaya umar ke saath barhati jaati hai। maayopiya ki samasaya se joojh rahe log chashama ya kntekat lains ke jariye samasaya se nijaat pa sakate hain lekin samasaya jayaada ho to ऑpareshan davaara maayopiya ka ilaaj snbhav hai। isake alaava niman kaaran bhi hain: (Other Reasons & Causes of Myopia) daayabitij (Daibetes) se garasit hone para। aanuvmshiki (Genetic Disorder) kaaranon se bhi aisa ho sakata hai। lnbe samay tak ek hi lains ka parayog karanaa। (Use of lenses) kisi bhi chij ko bahut paas se ghoorakar kaaray karanaa। kam roshani men koi kaaray karanaa, jaise parhana ya tivi dekhanaa। Treatments: maayopiya se bachaav ke lie saamaanay upachaar (Treatment & tips for Myopia) - barithing vayaayaam karen। - tariphala chooran rojaana len। - lnbe samay tak telivijan dekhane ya parhane se bachen। - jahm kaam karen, vahm parayaapat roshani honi chaahie। - nkhon ki roshani barhaane ke lie nvala ka parayog karen। - munh men paani bhar kar nkhon ko taaje paani se dhoen। - paradooshan ya dhoop men nikalane se pahale nkhon par chashama pahanen। - likaresi ki jad ka paaudar aur shahad milaakar doodh ke saath len। - naariyala, mishari, saunph aur baadaam ko milaakar mikasar taiyaar karen aur paaudar banaayem। din men do baar khaaen। Disease: khararaate lena (Snoring) Description: sote vakat sns ke saath tej aavaaj aur vaaibaresham (Sound & Vibration) aana khararaate (Snoring) kahalaata hai। khararaate lena saadhaarama-si pareshaani hai, lekin jab yah bimaari ka roop le leti hai to gnbhir samasaya ban jaati hai। sns lene mem baara-baar rukaavat hone par sharir men ऑkasijam ka leval kam ho jaata hai, jisase bipi barh jaata hai। sharir mem ऑkasijan kam hote hi dil ko ऑkasijan ke lie jayaada pareshar lagaana padta hai। jab yah samasaya barh jaati hai to haarat ataik bhi ho sakata hai। Symptoms: - subah uthane par gale aur maak ka sookha homa - din ke samay bhi nimd mahasoos hona - chhote chhote kaamon ke baad bhi thakaan mahasoos homa aur aalas aama - gale aur naak se tej aavaaj nikalana - sote vakat munh khul jaana aur hava nikalana Reasons: khararaate ya sanorimg ke kaarana- (Causes & Reasons of Snoring) jayaadaatar logon ko lagata hai ki khararaate aane ki vajah jayaada thakaan hai isalie ve ise anadekha kar dete hain। isase samasaya gnbhir ho jaati hai। daraasala, sote samay sns men rukaavat khararaate aane ki mukhay vajah hai। gale ke pichhale hisase ke snkare ho jaane par ऑkasijan snkari jagah se hoti hui jaati hai, jisase aasapaas ke tishoo vaaibaret (Tissue Vibrate) hote hain। isi se khararaate aate hain। kai baar log pith ke bal sote hain, jisase jibh pichhe ki taraph ho jaati hai। taaloo ke pichhe yoovayal (taaloo ke pichhe thodaa-sa lataka hua mnsa) par jaakar lag jaati hai, jisase sns lene aur chhodne mem rukaavat aane lag jaati hai। isase sms ke saath aavaaj aur vaaibaresham hone lagata hai। miche vaale jabade ka chhota hona bhi khararaate aane ka ek kaaran hai। jab vayakati ka jabada saamaanay se chhota hota hai to letame par usaki jibh pichhe ki taraph ho jaati hai aur sns ki nali ko balaॉk kar deti hai। aise men sns lene aur chhodana़e ke lie pareshar lagaana padta hai, jis kaaran vaaibareshan hota hai। naak ki hadadi terhi hona (Crooked Nose Bome) aur usamen mns barha (Meat soar) honaa। isamen bhi sns lene ke lie pareshar lagaama padta hai। Treatments: khararaate ya sanoring se bachaav ke lie upaaya- (Tips & Treatments to Prevent Snoring) - sone ki pojishan badalen। - nashe vaale padaarathon se door rahen। - takiye ke kavar badalate rahen। - raat ke samay halaka khaana khaaen। - gale ki regayular ekasarasaaij karen। - khoob paani pien aur sharir ko haaidaret rakhen। - naak ki hadadi men samasaya ho ya phir mns barha ho to daॉkatar se samay rahate milen। - kai baar pareganensi men vajan badhana़e ya sone ki sathiti sahi n hone par bhi khararaate aate hain। aise men karavat lekar sona chaahie। - pith ke bal sone ki bajaay karavat lekar soen। isase sms ki mali men rukaavat nahin hoti। sote samay sir ko thoda uncha karake soen। isase aapaki jibh aur sns ki nali men rukaavat nahin aaegi। - agar khararaate aane ka kaaran jayaada vajan hai to samay rahate vajan kntarol karem। jim jaॉin karen। niyamit yog aur ekasarasaaij karane se vajan ko kntarol kiya ja sakata hai। Disease: sanabaran (Sumburn) Descriptiom: sanabaran ya dhoop se jhulasama (Sumburn) dhoop ke kaaran tavacha ka parabhaavit hona aam baat hai। koi bhi vayakati yadi dhoop men jayaada der rahata hai to sooray ki kiranon usaki tavacha (Skin) ko nukasaan (Damage) pahuncha sakati hain। yadi tej dhoop ki vajah se tavacha jayaada jal ya jhulas jaae to yah sathiti sanabaran (Sunburn) kahalaati hai। Symptoms: - parabhaavit hisasa chhoone par garam lagata hai। - parabhavit hisasa gahara laala, kaala ya gahara bhoora najar aata hai। - dhoop se aane ke baad turnt tavacha ke pharak ko dekha ja sakata hai। - parabhaavit hisase par jalan aur darad mahasoos ho sakata hai। - tavacha par paramaanemt pharak aaya hai isaka pata 24 ghnte ke ndar dekha ja sakata hai। - tavacha rookhi tatha bejaan najar aati hai। - chhote chhote chhaale ya paani vaale daane bhi ho sakate hain। - parabhaavit jagah par soojan bhi a sakati hai। - bukhaar ke saath ulati bhi lag sakati hai। Reasons: sanabaran ya dhoop se jhulasane ke kaaran (Causes & Reasons of sunburn) sooraj ki alataraavaॉyalet kiramon ke sidhe taur par snparak men aane par sanabaran hota hai। sharir paraakaृtik roop se mailenin (Natural melanim) ka niramaan karake khud ko sooraj ki kiranon ke parakop se bachaata hai। mailenin ek rnjak yaani pigament (Pigment) hota hai jo tavacha ke rng ke lie jimamedaar hota hai। kaale ya snvale logon ki tavacha gore rng ke logon ki apekasha kam daimej hoti hai kayonki snvali tavacha men pigament jayaada banata hai। gore (Fair) logon men pigament kam hota hai isalie unaki tavacha sooray ke snparak men aane par jaladi kashatigarasat hoti hai। isake alaava maidaani ilaakom (Grounded Area) men rahane vaale logom ki apekasha pahaadi ilaakon (Hill Tract) men rahame vaale logon ki tavacha bhi jaladi kashatigarasat (Damage) hoti hai kayonki vahn sooraj maidaam ki apekasha najadik aur tej hota hai। Treatments: dhoop se jhulasane ya sanabaran se bachaav ker lie upaay (Tips & Treatment for Sumburm) - poori baahon ke kapade pahanen। - khire, tamaatar aur aaloo ka ras lagaaen। - sanabaran vaale hisase par thndi patatiyn rakhem। - har chaar ghnte par sanasakarim lagaaen। - dhoop men jaane se aadha ghnta pahale sanasakarin ka parayog karem। - koshish karen ki subah 10 se shaam 4 ke bich dhoop men n jaaen। - dhoop se jhulasi tavacha par elovera bhi behad phaayada pahumchaata hai। - kaॉtan ka kapada thnde doodh men bhigaakar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen। - parabhaavit hisase par thndi dahi lagaane se bhi bahut aaraam milata hai। - dhoop men nikalane se pahale khud ko achachhi tarah se dhakakar nikalen, masalan nkhon par chashamaa, sir par sakaaraph ya kaip pahamen। Disease: galasua (Mumps) Description: galasua (Mumps) galasua (Mumps) ek vaayaral snkaraman (Viral Infection) hai। yah haalnki sharir ke kai hisason ko parabhaavit kar sakata hai lekina, mukhay roop se laar garnthiyon ko parabhaavit karata hai jo kaan aur jabade ke bich men paratayek gaal ke pichhe sathit hoti hain। galasua laar garnthiyon (Salivary Glands) ki soojan (Swelling) aur darad (Pain) ka kaaran banata hai। yah rog mukhay roop se 5 se 15 varash ki umar men adhik dekhane ko milata hai। ladkon ki apekasha ladkiyon men (Specially in girl) yah rog jaladi hota hai। entibaayotik davaaon se galasua ka ilaaj snbhav nahin hai, yah do haphaton men yah apaneaap hi samaapat ho jaata hai। darad nivaarak dava jaise ibooparophen ya peraasitaamol ka upayog kiya ja sakata hai aur sooje hue bhaag par thnda paik lagaane se bhi madad milati hai। ek saadhaaran se parikashan se galasua ki pushati ho sakati hai kayonki kaanon ke ekadam saamane jabade men soojan dikhaai deti hai। kalachar ya rakat parikashan (Blood test) davaara bhi nidaan ki pushati ho sakati hai। rakat men entibaॉdi ki upasathiti aasaami se vaayaral snkaraman ki pushati kar deta hai। Symptoms: - kaan men darad hona - pet men darad hona - bhookh n lagana - chabaane aur nigalane men darad hona - bukhaar - siradarad - gaalom men soojan dikhaai dena - kamazori Reasoms: galasua ke kaaram (Reasons & Causes of Mumps) galasua ya mamapas perotid garnthiyom men vaayaral snkaraman (Viral Infection) se hone ke kaaram hone vaali bimaari hai। yah garnthiym laar banaati hain jo chehare ke donon taraph jabade ki hadadi ke niche sathit hoti hai। yah snkaramit laar (Infected Saliva), chhinkane ya khnsane (Sneezing or Coughing) tatha snkaramit vayakati (Infected Person) ke saath baratan saajha karane aadi se ek vayakati se doosare vayakati men phailati hai। mamapas ke vaayaras se snkaramit marija, perotid garnthi men soojan shuroo hone ke 7 din pahale aur 7 din baad tak snkaraman phaila sakata hai। lakashanon ki shuruaat aamataur par vaayaras se snparak ke baad 14-18 dinon men hoti hai। aisa kaha jaata hai ki koi bhi vayakati keval ek baar hi galasua se pidit hota hai, lekin kuchh log dobaara bhi snkaramit ho sakate hain। mamapasa, khaana aur paani sheyar karane se bhi phail sakata hai। yoon to yah rog bachachon men jayaada dekhane ko milata hai lekin isake lakasham kisi bhi umar ke vayakati ko parabhaavit kar sakate hain। yah bahut gnbhir bimaari nahin hai lekin kai baar samasaya barh bhi jaati hai। Treatments: saamaanay upachaar Home Remedies: jaanen galasua ya mamapas ke ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies for Mumps) phalon ka ras m pien। parayaapat maatara men paani pien। emaemaaar ke tike lagavaayen। tikha ya amaliy khaane se bachem। sooje hue hisase par thndi ya garam patati ka sek karen। kaali mirach ka lep parabhaavit sathaan par lagaane se aaraam milata hai। elovera ko chhilakar us par haladi daalakar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaaen। adarak ko pisakar parabhaavit sathaan par lagaane se bhi mamapas men aaraam milata hai। pipal ke patate ko sek kar us par ghi ya tel lagaakara, parabhaavit sathaan par bndhen। methi ke paaudar men jau ka aata milaakar parabhaavit sathaan par lep karane se aaraam milata hai। baragad ke ped ki patatiyon ko bhi tel lagaakar garam karake parabhaavit sathaan par lagaame se aaraam milata hai। Disease: kaali khnsi (Whooping Cough) Description: kaali khnsi (Whooping Cough) vahooping kaph ya kaali khnsi (Whooping cough) gnbhir kisam ki khnsi hoti hai, jo jayaadaatar 5 se 15 varash aayu tak ke bachachon ko hoti hai। ise kukur khnsi bhi kaha jaata hai। yah khnsi bachachon men home vaali ek snkaraamak tatha khataramaak bimaari hai। yah mukhayata: shavasan tntar (Respiratory System) ko parabhaavit karati hai। bhaarat jaise vikaasashil desh men paratayek ek laakh ki aabaadi par 578 bachache paratayek varash is bimaari se garasit hote hain। yah rog ladkon ki tulana men ladkiyom ko jayaada hota hai। 6 mahine se kam umar ke bachachom men is bimaari se maृtayu dar adhik hoti hai। haalnki yah bimaari saal ke kisi bhi mahine men ho sakati hai kintu saradi ke mausam men kaali (kukura) khnsi hone ki bahut adhik snbhaavana rahati hai। baara-baar khnsi home aur ulati hone se bachache shaaririk roop se bahut kamajor ho jaate hain। kuchh bhi khaate-pite samay khnsi ka daura paraarnbh ho jaata hai। lagaataar khnsi ka daura chalane par ulati hoti hai। baara-baar ulati home par khaaya hua bhojan pet se baahar nikal jaata hai। kai baar aushadhi khilaate samay bhi khnsi shuroo ho jaati hai aur ulati hone jaane ke kaaran aushadhi bhi mikal jaati hai। khnsi ke rogi bachache ko bisatar par jaane ke baad thodi der baad khnsi ka parakop adhik hota hai। bachache ke jora-jor se bolane aur chilalaane par khnsi ka daura paraarnbh ho jaata hai। Symptoms: - ghabaraahat hona - khnsate- khnsate mkh se paani aana - sns bmd hone ka ehasaas hona - bukhaar ya jukaam hona - gale ki nason ka phool jaana - chehare ka pila pad jaana - khnsate khnsate gale ka roomdh jaana - hava jayaada lene ki chhatapataana - sns lene men ghur ghur ki aavaaj aana Reasons: kaali khnsi ke kaarana- (Cause & Reason of Whooping Cough) kaali khnsi (Whooping cough) himophaailas paratusis (Haemophilus Pertussis) jivaanuom ke snkaraman se hoti hai। rog ke jivaanu rogi bachache ki naak aur munh men chhipe rahate hain। jab rogi bachache jor se khnsate aur chhinkate hain to rog ke sookasham jivaanu vaayu men phailakar doosare savasath bachache tak pahunch jaate hain। rogi bachache se baatachit karame, usake saath uthane-baithane se yah rog doosare bachachon men bhi phail jaata hai। ghar men kisi ek vayakati ko kaali khnsi ho jaane par dhire-dhire poore ghar men khnsi phail jaati hai। chhote bachachon men kaali khnsi ki utapatati saradi-jukaam ke kaaram hoti hai। adhik saradi lagame, paani men adhik bhigane v saradi ke dinon men nnge pnv ghoomane se saradi-jukaam hota hai। aise men kuchh bachache moongaphali, akharot v anay koi meva aur ghi, tel makakhan se bani chijen khaakar thnda paani pite hain to unahem khnsi ho jaati hai jo saradi ke parakop se kaali (kukura) khnsi men parivaratit ho jaati hai। kuchh bachachon ko kaali khmsi ka rog elaraji ke kaaram hota hai। elarajik vasatu ke snparak men aane par sns lene men pareshaani hoti hai। gale men jalan v khujali hoti hai। gale men soojan hone se khnsi ka parakop barhane ke kaaran rogi ko bahut pida hoti hai। khnsate hue rogi ka munh laal pad jaata hai। munh se laar girane lagati hai। nkhon men se nsoo bahame lagate hain। rogi bachache bhayabhit hokar rone lagate hain। anat men ulati hone par khnsi ka parakop kuchh kam ho jaata hai। Treatments: saamaanay upachaar Home Remedies: jaanen kaali khnsi se bachaav ke ghareloo upaay (Home Remedies for Whooping Cough) 1. suhaagaa, kalamishoraa, phitakari, kaala namak aur yavakashaar ko pisakar chooran taiyaar kar len। ise tave par bhoonakar 2-2 garaam ki maatara men shahad ko milaakar bachachon ko chataane se kaalikhnsi door ho jaati hai। isake alaava tave par bhuna hua suhaaga v vnshalochan ko milaakar shahad ke saath rogi bachache ko chataane se bhi kaalikhnsi door hoti hai। 2. pipala, kaakadaasingi, atis aur baheda sabhi aushadhiyon ko 20-20 garaam ki maatara mem lekar baarik koota-pisakar chooran taiyaar kar len। isamen 10 garaam nausaadara, 10 garaam bhuna hua suhaaga milaakar pis len। isake 3 garaam chooran ko din men 2-3 baar chaatame se kaali khnsi door ho jaati hai। 3. adoosa ke sookhe pataton ko mitati ke baratam men rakhakara, aag par garam karake usaki raakh ko taiyaar kar len। us raakh ko 24 se 36 garaam tak ki maatara men lekar shahad ke saath rogi ko chataane se kaalikhnsi door ho jaati hai। 4. mooli ka 50 mililitar ras aur ganame ka ras milaakar din men 2 baar pilaane se kukar khnsi mem laabh milata hai। 5. 3 mililitar naariyal ka tel halaka garam karake bachache ko pilaane se khnsi ka parakop kam ho jaata hai। naariyal ki jata ki bhasam karake lagabhag 1 garaam ka chautha bhaag shahad men milaakar ya paani se khaaen। isase 2-3 baar men hi khnsi ka veg v khnsi khatam ho jaati hai। 6. adarak ke ras ko shahad mem milaakar 2-3 baar chaatane se kaali khnsi ka asar khatam ho jaata hai। 7. 3 baadaam raat ko paani men daalakar rakh den। subah uthakar baadaam ke chhilake utaarakar lahasun ki ek kali aur mishari ke saath milaakar pis len। is misharan ko bachachon ko khilaame se kaali khnsi door ho jaati hai। 8. bachachon ko kukar khnsi hone par lahasun ki maala pahamaate hain jisase isaki gndh khnsane ke saatha-saath anadar chali jaati hai aur isi ka ras aadha chamamach shahad ke saath bhi pilaaen। isase kaali khnsi door ho jaati hai। das boond ya ek chamamach lahasun ka ras (umar ke anusaara) shahad milaakar paratidin do-tin baar sevam karane se khoob laabh milata hai। 9. tave ko aag par rakhakar laung ko bhoon len, phir us laung ko pisakar shahad men milaakar chaatane se kaali khnsi thik ho jaati hai। bachachon ko kaali khnsi men ek chauthaai garaam se kam golochan ko subaha-shaam shahad ke saath chataame se laabh milata hai। 10. tulasi ke pataton ke 3 garaam ras men shahad milaakar chaatane se kaalikhnsi men bahut adhik laabh milata hai। 11. tulasi ke patate aur kaalimirach samaan maatara men pis lem। isaki moong ke baraabar ki goliyn bana lem। eka-ek goli ko chaar baar dena chaahie। isase kaali khnsi nashat ho jaati hai। 12. kaali khnsi hone par bachachon ko bisatar par sulaane se pahale usake sine aur kamar par kapoor ko tel men milaakar maalish karen, kaali khnsi bamad ho jaaegi। 13. haladi ki 3-4 gmthon ko todkar tave par bhoonen aur pisakar chooran bana len। is chooran ko 3-3 garaam subaha-shaam paani se lene se kaalikhnsi men aaraam aata hai। Disease: parosatet disaऑradar (Prostate Disorder) Description: parosatet disaऑradar (Prostate Disorder) parosatet galaind jayaada barh jaane par parosatet disaऑradar (Prostate Disorder) kahalaata hai। lagabhag tis phisadi purush 40 ki umar men aur pachaas phisadi se bhi jayaada purush 60 ki umar men parosatet ki samasaya se pareshaan hote haim। parosatet galaimd ko purushon ka doosara dil bhi maana jaata hai। pauroosh garnthi sharir men kuchh behad jaroori kariya karati hai। jaise yoorin ke bahaav ko kntarol karana aur parajanam ke lie simem banaanaa। jaise-jaise umar barhati hai, yah garnthi barhane lagati hai। is garnthi ka apane aap men barhana hi haanikaarak hota hai aur ise bipiech (Benigm Prostatic Hyperplasia) kahate hain। parosatet garnthi ke jayaada barh jaane se mootar utasarajam ki pareshaani ho jaati hai। garnthi ke aakaar men vaृdadhi ho jaane par mootar nalika avarudadh ho jaati hai aur yahi peshaab rukane ka kaaran banati hai। parosatet garnthi ke aakaar mem vaृdadhi hone ka kaaran sapashat nahin hai। barhati umar ke saath purushon ke sharir men hone vaala haaramon ka parivaratan ek kaaran ho sakata hai। Symptoms: - raat ko kai baar peshaab ke liye uthanaa। - mootar ki kuchh maatara mootaraashay men shesh rah jaati hai, is shesh rahe mootar men rogaanu panapate hain। - peshaab karane men kathinaai mahasoos honaa। - peshaab karane ke baad bhi mootar ki boonde tapakati rahati hain, yaani mootar par niyntaran nahin rahataa। - aisa mahasoos hota hai ki peshaab a raha hai lekin baatharoom mem jaane par boonda-boomd ya ruka-ruk kar peshaab hota hai। - peshaab men jalan mahasoos hoti hai। - ndakoshon men darad uthata rahata hai। - jaladi jaladi peshaab honaa। - peshaab ki dhaar chaaloo hone men vilnb honaa। Treatmemts: parosatet upachaar (Treatmemt & Tips to Prevent Prostate Disorder) parosatet garnthi men vaृdadhi hone par mariz ko chikitasakiy upachaar ki aavashayakata hoti hai। mootar thaili ke lagaataar bhare rahane se guradom par dabaav barh jaata hai, jisase imake kharaab hone ka khatara paida ho jaata hai। rog ki paraarnbhik avasatha men davaaon davaara garnthi ki vaृdadhi ko kam karane ka parayaas kiya jaata hai। kuchh marizon ko davaaiyon se koi laabh nahin hotaa, aisi sathiti men shalayakariya karake rogi ke sharir se parosatet garnthi nikaal di jaati hai। chikitasa ki aadhunik padadhati se kam se kam chira-phaad v rakata-saraav davaara parosatet garnthi ki bimaari ka ilaaj snbhav hai। aisi hi ek aadhumik takanik hai lezar kiranon se parosatekataॉmi। lejar parosatekataॉmi (Laser Prostatectomy) isamen lejar kiranon ke maadhayam se parosatet garnthi ke us hisase ko kaatakar alag kar diya jaata hai jisase mootar nalika ka maarag avaroodadh ho raha thaa। lezar parosatekataॉmi men ek phaaibar ऑpatik telisakop doorabin ko mariz ke mootaradavaar se mootaraashay ki or bheja jaata hai। yahm parosatet garmthi ke barhe hue hisase ko kaatakar nikaal diya jaata hai aur parosatet ke tukade ko mootaraashay men dhakel diya jaata hai। mootaramaarag men nali daal di jaati hai jisase mootar utasarajam nirabaadhit roop se hota rahata hai। mootaraashay mem dhakele gae garnthi ke bache hue hisason ko vahn se nikaal diya jaata hai। parosatet ke n tukadon ko paitholaॉji (Pathology) jmch ke lie bheja jaata hai jahn garnthi ke aakaar men vaृdadhi ke kaaranon ki jnch ki jaati hai। parosatet garmthi ke lezar sarajari se nikaalane ke baad peshaab karane ki barhi aavaृtati, tivar ichachha v mootaraashay pooranata: khaali n hone jaisi shikaayaten door ho jaati hain aur mootar ka paravaah bhi thik ho jaata hai। parosatet garnthi ko hataane se kaya samasaya a sakati hai? (Problems to Remove Prostate Gland) parosatet garnthi ke saraav se shukaraanuon ko poshan aur surakasha milati hai। shalayakariya davaara garnthi ko nikaal die jaane par koi viparit parabhaav mahin padata kayonki parosatet ke alaava semaainal vesikalas (Seminal vesicles) bhi is kaaray ko karati hai। Home Remedies: jaanen parosatet disaऑradar ke ghareloo upachaar (Home Remedies of Prostate Disorder) 3 se 4 litar paani rojaana pien। bhojan men vitaamin si ki maatara jayaada len। charabiyukat aur vasaayukat bhojan ka parayog bnd kar den। rojaana soyaabin khaaen isase tetosataron ka leval kam ho jaata hai। alasi ko mikasi men pisakar paaudar bana len aur paratidin 20 garaam paani ke saath len। chaay aur kaॉphi ka sevan n karen, isase mootaraashay gariva kathor hoti hai jisase peshaab karane men dikakat hoti hai। sitaaphal ke bij kachacha ya bhoon kar ya phir doosare bijon ke saath milaakar kha sakate hain। ise apane har din ke khaane men shaamil kiya ja sakata hai। ise salaad men milaakar bhi khaaya ja sakata hai। poha men milaakar ya soop men daalakar bhi kha sakate hai। kachache sitaaphal ke bij men kaaphi maatara men poshak tatav maujood hote hain। jaise aayarana, phaॉsaphorasa, taripatophaina, kaॉpara, maiganishiyama, maiganija, vitaamin ke, parotina, jaroori phaiti esid aur phaaitosaterola। ye bij jink ke behatarim saroton men se ek maane jaate hain। har din 60 miligaraam jink ka sevan parosatet se joojh rahe marijon men behad phaayada pahunchaata hai aur umake savaasathay men bhi sudhaar karata hai। in bijon men bitaa-satiosaterol bhi hota hai jo tesatosateron ko dihaaidarotesateron men badalane nahin detaa। jisase is garnthi ke barhane ki snbhaavana n ke baraabar ho jaati hai। Disease: edas (AIDS) Descriptiom: edas ya ekavaayarad imayoon dephisienshi sindarom (Acquired Immune Deficiency Syndrome) duniya ki sabase khataramaak aur jaanaleva bimaariyom men se ek hai। yah echaaaivi vaayaras ke kaaran phailane vaala rog hai। duniyaabhar men edas ke saravaadhik maamale asurakashit yaum snbndhon ke kaaran hote hain। Symptoms: - akaaram vajan ghatate jaanaa। - gale ya bagal men soojan bhari gilatiyom ka ho jaanaa। - ta‍vacha par darad bhare aur khujali vaale chakate ho jaamaa। - bina kisi vajah ke lagaataar daayariya bane rahanaa। - bima kisi vajah ke lagaataar thakaan bame rahana aur teji se vajan giranaa। - munh men ghaav ho jaanaa। - munh men saphed chhaale jaise nishaan honaa। - yaadadaashat men kami, dipareshan ya amay dimaagi bimaari - lnbe samay tak bukhaar rahana Reasons: edas ke kaarak (Causes of Aids in Hindi) duniyaabhar men edas ki phailane ki sabase badi vajah (Causes of Aids) asurakashit yaun snbndhon ko maana jaata hai। lekin kai anay kaaran bhi hai jo edas ke lie jimamevaar maane jaate haim: asurakashit sekas (Unsafe Sex):- ek se adhik saathiyon ke saath yaun snbndh banaane se echaaaivi edas phail sakata hai। yah samalaingik snbmdhon men bhi ho sakata hai। snkaramit rogi davaara (From HIV+ Victim):- echaaaivi paॉjitiv purush ya mahila ke saath asurakashit yaun snbndh banaane ke kaaran bhi yah phailata hai। snkaramit khoon chaṛhaane (Through Blood Transfusion):- bina jnch kiya hua raka‍t garahan karane ke kaaran bhi echaaaivi se pidit home ka khatara rahata hai। yah edas ko phailaame ki doosari sabase badi vajah maani jaati hai। snkaramit sui ke isatemaal se (Through Infected Needles):- daragas ki samasaya ma siraph nashe tak simit hai balaki agar ek hi injekashan se kai log daragas len to yah edas ka kaaran ban sakata hai। siraph daragas hi nahin davaai lene ke dauraan bhi snkaramit sui ka isatemaal haanikaarak hota hai। snkaramit baled se (Through Infected Blood):- saath hi naai ke yahn bina sataralaaijad (rogaanu-mukata) usatara ya puraana inaphekated baled (Infected Blade) isatemaal karane se bhi yah phail sakata hai। snkaramit maata se (HIV Positive Mother):- echaaaivi smkaramit maata ke davaara yah bachache men khoon ya parasav ke samay aur doodh pilaane ke dauraan pahunch jaata hai। Treatments: edas se bachaav (Tips to prevent AIDS in Hindi) surakashit sekas (Use Safety):- edasa, echaaaivi snkaraman aur anay sekas snkaramit bimaariyn rokane ke lie hamesha snbndh banaate samay kndom aadi ka parayog karana chaahie। apame jivanasaathi ke parati vaphaadaar rahama chaahie aur ek se adhik va‍yakati se yaumasnbndh banaane se bachana chaahie। isatemaal ki gai suiyom ka parayog na karen (Use Disposable Syringe):- sui lagavaate samay hamesha yah dhayaan rakhen ki disapojebal sirinj ya suiyon ka hi isatemaal ho। khoon ke lena-den se pahale jnch (Test Before Blood Tramsfusion):- khoon lene ya dene se pahale usaki jnch avashay kar len। yadi aap echa.aai.vi smkaramit ya edas garasit hain to rakatadaan na karen। garabhavati mahilaaen dhayaan rakhen (Tips for HIV+ Pregnant):- garabhavati mahilaaon ko apana echaaaivi tesat jaroor karaana chaahie। agar jnch paॉjitiv hai to bachacha ho jaame ke baad echaaaivi se garasat mn ko bachache ko apana doodh nahim pilaana chaahie। is kes men botal se doodh pilaana behatar maana jaata hai। shak hone par echa.aai.vi tesat (HIV AIDS Test):- yadi aap ko echa.aai.vi edas hone ka sndeh ho to turnt apana echa.aai.vi parikashan karaana chaahie। echaaaivi edas ki davaaiyn (HIV AIDS Drugs):- echaaaivi paॉjitiv vayakati ko ilaaj ke dauraan enti-retarovaayaral daragas die jaate hain। Disease: jika vaayaras (Zik Virus) Description: ibola vaayaras ke baad duniyaabhar men aatnk phailaani vaali mai bimaari hai jikaa। jika vaayaras logon ke lie itana khataranaak hai ki vishav savaasathay sngatham me jika vaayaras par ga‍lobal imarajensi ghoshit ki hai। jika vaayaras baraajil samet kai anay ameriki deshon men phaila hua hai aur inahin deshon ke aane vaale logon ke davaara isake vishav ke anay deshon men phailane ke aasaar haim। aaiye jaanen jika vaayaras aur isake snkaraman ke vishay men pooran jaanakaari (Zik Virus Information im Hindi)। Symptoms: - nkhen laal hona - joṛom men darad - bukhaar - ulati - kamazori Treatments: jika vaayaras ka ilaaj (Treatment of Zik Virus in Hindi) * sidisi ke anusaar jika inphekashan se ladne ke lie abhi kisi injekashan ya davaai ko ijaad nahin kiya gaya hai। isase pidit vayakati ko poori tarah se aaraam karana chaahie, khoob saara paani pina chaahie, bukhaar ki saamaanay davaai leni chaahie। * jika vaayaras se snkaramit hone par khud ko machachhar ke kaatane se bachaana chaahie anayatha yah vaayaras machachharom davaara anay logon men pahunch sakata hai। pidit rogi ka machachharon se bachaav bahut jaroori hai। nota: bukhaar aame par esaparin (Aspirin), baroophen jaisi davaaiyn bilakul nahin leni chaahie। garabhavati mahilaaon ke lie khaas niradesh (Tips For Pregnant Women) sidisi ke davaara anay deshon men rahane vaali garabhavati mahilaaon ko yah sujhaav diya gaya hai ki vah apharikaa, dakashin amerika ya jika parabhaavit anay deshom men na jaaen। jika vaayaras se parabhaavit jagahon par rahane vaali garabhavati mahilaaon ko niman baaton ka khayaal rakhana chaahie: * khud ko machachharon ke kaatane se bachaana chaahie। * raat ko sote samay machachharadaani ka parayog karana chaahie aur machachharon ke kaatane se bachane vaali karim lagaani chaahie। * agar machachharon ke kaatame par siradarada, hala‍ka bukhaara, laal nkhen, jodon mem darad jaise lakashan dikhen to turnt daॉkatar se salaah leni chaahie। * agar garabhavati nahin hain to kuchh dinon ke lie pareganensi ke palaan ko taal dena chaahie। garabhavati mahilaaon ko machachharon se bachane ki poori koshish karami chaahie kayonki jika vaayaras ke kaaran unake garabh men pal rahe bachachon ke masatishak ko sabase adhik nukasaan hota hai।
